# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Elimination of Flux Trapping in Superconducting Circuits in Ambient Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27415)
*Rohan T. Kapur,Alex Wynn,Sergey K. Tolpygo,Neel Parmar,Anil Mankame,Adam A. Libson,Rabindra Das,Michele Kelley,Pauli Kehayias,Nathaniel J. O'Connor,Collin N. Muniz,Justin L. Mallek,Jennifer M. Schloss*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于片上加热器产生的局部热梯度与超导薄膜中的蚀刻沟槽（moats）相结合的实际解决方案，用于消除环境磁场冷却过程中超导电路中捕获的磁通涡旋，实验表明该方法可在基本磁屏蔽环境下有效抑制大规模电路中的所有磁通，克服了超导高性能可扩展计算长期面临的关键挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导数字电子学（superconductor digital electronics）和基于超导量子比特（superconducting qubits）的量子计算是前景广阔的新一代计算技术，但超导薄膜在冷却或存在非零背景磁场$B_r$时会产生磁通涡旋（magnetic vortices），这些涡旋会降级电路或量子比特性能，这一问题长期阻碍超导高性能可扩展计算的发展。

Method: 采用集成在芯片上的电阻加热器（on-chip resistive heaters）产生可控局部热梯度（local thermal gradients），并结合在超导电路薄膜中蚀刻出的沟槽（moats）。热梯度驱动磁通涡旋向沟槽移动，使其远离电路区域和钉扎位点（pinning sites）而被捕获。实验在环境磁场$B_r\leq 60\ \upmu$T条件下进行冷却操作。

Result: 通过磁成像（magnetic imaging）和电路电学读出（electrical circuit readout）验证，该方法能有效移除冷却过程中捕获的磁通以及电路运行产生的磁通核（magnetic flux nucleated by circuit operation）。在基本磁屏蔽环境下，该方案能够抑制大规模电路中的所有磁通。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个消除超导电路中磁通涡旋的实用方案，克服了长期阻碍超导体实现高性能可扩展计算（high-performance scalable computing）的关键挑战之一。

Abstract: Superconductor digital electronics and quantum computing with superconducting qubits are promising next-generation computing technologies. When cooled down or operated in the presence of a nonzero background magnetic field $B_r$, superconducting thin films comprising the circuits can trap magnetic vortices that can degrade circuit or qubit performance. In this work, we report a practical solution for eliminating flux trapped during cooldown in ambient magnetic fields, $B_r\leq 60$ $\upmu$T, based on controlled local thermal gradients and moats, etched holes in the superconducting films of the circuit. Thermal gradients created by integrated on-chip resistive heaters move vortices towards the moats, where they become trapped away from circuitry regions and pinning sites. Using magnetic imaging and electrical circuit readout, we demonstrate that this approach is capable of removing magnetic flux trapped during field cooling and magnetic flux nucleated by circuit operation. If used in an environment with basic magnetic shielding, this solution is capable of suppressing all magnetic flux in a large-scale circuit, overcoming one of the long-standing challenges preventing high-performance scalable computing using superconductors.

</details>


### [2] [The Second Law, Symmetry of Time Reversal and Thermodynamic Equilibrium in Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27628)
*Vladimir Kozhevnikov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本篇论文旨在弥补热力学第二定律在磁性材料（尤其是超导体）应用理解上的重大缺口，分析了超导体系中平衡态、可逆性及时间反演对称性等基本概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管热力学第二定律普遍适用于所有物质和辐射状态，但其在磁性材料（特别是超导体）中的应用仍存在显著的理解不足。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 本文通过概念性分析，聚焦超导特异性的三类关键因素：(1) 场强 $\textbf{H}$ 在磁化形成中的首要作用；(2) 热力学平衡态下样品的零熵特性；(3) 非平衡态下两类超导电流的区分。在此基础上推导时间反演对称性（time reversal symmetry）与第二定律的关系。

Result: 论证了超导体中的时间反演对称性是热力学第二定律的必然推论，因而在平衡态下是超导材料的强制性属性。同时给出了实现平衡态的必要条件。

Conclusion: 对上述方面的认识对于推进各类超导材料的超导研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: The Second law, universally applicable to all states of all sorts of matter and radiation, is undeniably the brightest jewel in the tiara of laws of thermodynamics; recall that the achievements of this law include the principle of least action, the atomistic structure of matter, the quantization of radiant heat, and much more. However, there is a significant gap in understanding the application of the Second law to magnetizing materials, especially to superconductors. This communication is targeted to fill the gap. The concepts of equilibrium and reversibility in thermodynamic processes are considered with particular attention to specifics of superconductivity. These include (1) the primary role of the field strength $\textbf{H}$ in forming magnetization; (2) the zero entropy of samples in a state of thermodynamic equilibrium; and (3) two kinds of superconducting currents in samples out of equilibrium. As shown, time reversal symmetry in superconductors is a consequence of the Second law and, therefore, is a mandatory property of these materials in a state of equilibrium. Necessary conditions for achieving the latter are framed out. Awareness of these aspects is important for advancing research on superconductivity in all kinds of superconducting materials.

</details>


### [3] [Thickness dependence of diode efficiency in superconducting Fe(Se,Te)/FeTe thin-film heterostructure devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27639)
*Kaito Arizono,Kenshin Inamura,Kouta Kondou,Yusuke Kobayashi,Tsutomu Nojima,Jobu Matsuno,Junichi Shiogai*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Fe(Se,Te)/FeTe异质结器件中的超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect, SDE），发现SDE效率随超导层厚度增加而单调增大，并实现了近100%的整流效率，揭示了结构反转不对称性（structural inversion asymmetry）和Rashba自旋-轨道相互作用（Rashba spin-orbit interaction）在涡旋诱导SDE中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应因其在无能耗整流器中的潜在应用而受到关注，然而连接电子能带结构反转不对称性、自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interaction）与涡旋钉扎（vortex pinning）的微观起源尚不明确。本研究旨在通过调控Fe(Se,Te)超导层厚度，阐明结构反转不对称性对涡旋诱导SDE的影响。

Method: 构建Fe(Se,Te)/FeTe异质结器件，系统改变超导Fe(Se,Te)层的厚度tFST，测量SDE效率随厚度的变化关系，并在半波与全波振荡配置中测试整流性能。

Result: SDE效率随tFST单调增加，归因于体Fe(Se,Te)层中的能带弯曲（band bending）诱导了结构反转不对称性及Rashba自旋-轨道相互作用；在半波和全波振荡配置中实现了近100%的整流效率。

Conclusion: 结果表明，结构架构（structural architecture）对实现基于超导薄膜异质结的高效SDE器件至关重要。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE) is a nonreciprocal transport phenomenon, in which the superconducting critical current density depends on the polarity of the current. It has attracted recent attention because of its potential applications to a rectifier without energy dissipation. While SDE has been observed in a wide range of superconducting materials with broken inversion symmetry as well as thin-film heterostructures, the microscopic origin linking structural inversion asymmetry of electronic band, spin-orbit interaction, and vortex pinning remains to be clarified. In this study, we investigate SDE in Fe(Se,Te)/FeTe heterostructure devices as a function of the superconducting Fe(Se,Te) layer thickness tFST to elucidate the role of structural inversion asymmetry on the vortex-induced SDE. We find that the SDE efficiency monotonically increases with increasing tFST, which can be understood by considering that the band bending in the bulk Fe(Se,Te) layer induces the structural inversion asymmetry and thus, the Rashba spin-orbit interaction. In addition, we demonstrate almost 100% rectification for the Fe(Se,Te)/FeTe heterostructure devices in half- and full-wave oscillation configurations. Our findings point out the importance of structural architecture for realization of highly efficient SDE devices based on superconducting thin-film heterostructures.

</details>


### [4] [Imaging geometry- and phase-controlled spectra in a surface-state Andreev cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28189)
*Adrian Greichgauer,Yoichi Ando,Jens Brede*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunnelling spectroscopy）研究了与超导Nb(110)耦合的受限Cu(111)表面态，发现安德烈夫空腔（Andreev cavities）中的局域谱由几何定义的安德烈夫轨迹（Andreev trajectories）控制，并通过半经典相位累积图景（semiclassical phase-accumulation picture）加以解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管安德烈夫物理（Andreev physics）在输运测量中已被充分确立，但二维空腔（two-dimensional cavities）中的局域谱（local spectra）在实空间（real space）中仍 largely unexplored（ largely unexplored）。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究受限表面态与超导体耦合时的局域谱行为。

Method: 采用扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunnelling spectroscopy）对与超导Nb(110)耦合的受限Cu(111)表面态进行实空间探测；通过引入面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field）和涡旋相位纹理（vortex phase textures）来探究谱学特征的演变，并结合最小半经典相位累积图景（minimal semiclassical phase-accumulation picture）进行理论描述。

Result: 面内磁场引起的低能谱塌缩（collapse of the resolved low-energy spectrum）的磁场尺度由安德烈夫轨迹（Andreev trajectories）可用的横向展宽（transverse extent）控制；零场激发能（zero-field excitation energy）随特征轨迹长度（characteristic trajectory length）演化；在单个岛（individual islands）内观察到空间变化（spatial variations），并对涡旋相位纹理（vortex phase textures）有响应。

Conclusion: 上述趋势可由最小半经典相位累积图景（minimal semiclassical phase-accumulation picture）统一描述；几何定义的安德烈夫轨迹（geometry-defined Andreev trajectories）可作为局域谱学（local spectroscopy）可及的相位相干超导空腔（phase-coherent superconducting cavities）的设计原理（design principle）。

Abstract: Andreev cavities provide a setting in which superconducting proximity spectra are shaped by phase-coherent electron-hole motion along extended trajectories. While such Andreev physics is well established in transport, local spectra in two-dimensional cavities remain largely unexplored in real space. Here we use scanning tunnelling spectroscopy to study confined Cu(111) surface states coupled to superconducting Nb(110). The in-plane magnetic-field scale for the collapse of the resolved low-energy spectrum is controlled by the transverse extent available to Andreev trajectories, while the zero-field excitation energy evolves with the characteristic trajectory length. These trends, together with spatial variations within individual islands and the response to vortex phase textures, are captured by a minimal semiclassical phase-accumulation picture. Our results identify geometry-defined Andreev trajectories as a design principle for phase-coherent superconducting cavities accessible by local spectroscopy.

</details>


### [5] [Excitation of Collective Modes in a Chiral Superfluid by Thermal Quench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28306)
*Noble Gluscevich,J. A. Sauls*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 基于含时Ginzburg-Landau场论，研究了通过快速冷却经过二级相变进入超流态时，除Kibble-Zurek机制产生的拓扑缺陷外，新形成手性畴的集体激发模式，并报告了阻尼依赖的动力学标度指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解快速冷却通过二级相变（second-order phase transition）进入超流态时，除已知的Kibble-Zurek机制所产生的拓扑缺陷（topological defects）之外，系统是否还会激发其他集体模式，以及阻尼如何影响相变动力学。

Method: 采用含时Ginzburg-Landau场论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau field theory）进行理论建模，并通过在存在高斯时空白噪声（Gaussian space-time white noise）条件下进行温度淬火（temperature quench）的数值模拟，利用序参量振幅的傅里叶分量（Fourier components）追踪粗化动力学（coarsening dynamics）。

Result: 发现热噪声会激发玻色子集体模式，其功率谱密度（power spectral density, PSD）在弱阻尼下于玻色子模态质量对应的频率处陡峭起始，随后按1/ω衰减。Kibble-Zurek冻结时间和关联长度对淬火速率的标度指数依赖于阻尼；动力学指数z从z=1平滑过渡到z=2，而关联长度指数ν≈1/2与阻尼无关。

Conclusion: 快速冷却通过二级相变时，不仅产生拓扑缺陷，还会激发手性畴的集体模式；阻尼在决定动力学标度行为中起关键作用，但关联长度指数保持对阻尼不敏感。

Abstract: Based on time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau field theory we show that rapid cooling through the second-order phase transition into superfluid \Hea\ excites collective modes of newly formed chiral domains, in addition to topological defects that are formed via the Kibble-Zurek mechanism. Simulations of temperature quenches in the presence of Gaussian space-time white noise generate a highly excited inhomogeneous condensate. Large-scale simulations exhibit a complex network of domain walls and vortices. We report results for the excitation of bosonic collective modes by thermal noise as well as nonequilibrium temperature quenches, followed by coarsening dynamics tracked in terms of the Fourier components of the order parameter amplitudes. For thermal states, the spectrum of bosonic excitations is defined by a power spectral density (PSD) for each mode, which is sensitive to the Langevin damping. For weak damping the PSD onsets sharply at the frequency corresponding to the mass of the bosonic mode, then decays as $1/ω$. We also track the dynamics of the order parameter following a temperature quench. We report results for the scaling exponents of Kibble-Zurek freeze-out time and correlation length as a function of quench rate for several damping rates. The dynamical exponent $z$ is shown to transition smoothly from $z=1$ to $z=2$ as the damping is increased, while the correlation length exponent, $ν\approx 1/2$, is independent of damping.

</details>

### [6] [Heterogeneous synaptic motifs bridge microscale structure and macroscale nonlinear dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27946)
*Meiyi Zhang,Jinjian Yu,Louis Tao,Yuxiu Shao*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种包含二阶突触基序（second-order motifs）的随机循环神经网络（RNN）平均场理论框架，推导出P种群网络的低秩方程，揭示链式基序（chain motifs）如何通过突触变异的关联性影响介观群体动态，并应用于小鼠初级视觉皮层的网络逆向工程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期突触分辨率连接组学（connectomics）发现脑回路中存在精细尺度的结构连接（如二阶相关突触耦合），同时大规模神经活动记录显示出异质性群体动态。这引发了一个核心问题：微观突触结构能否以经典脑回路模型无法实现的方式贡献于宏观异质性动态与计算？

Method: 构建包含多种细胞类型、非线性非负神经响应以及任意边际与二阶相关突触统计的随机RNN；推导P种群网络的平均场低秩方程（mean-field low-rank equations），其中突触与基序强度由突触前和突触后神经元群体身份决定；框架仅需2P个潜在动态变量（P个描述平均群体活动，P个捕捉群体内变异）。

Result: 理论与仿真结果一致表明，链式基序诱导突触变异中的相关性，使微观涨落得以整合并影响介观平均群体动态；将该框架应用于小鼠初级视觉皮层（mouse primary visual cortex），成功逆向工程出能够复现跨群体异质性活动的网络连接。

Conclusion: 该框架弥合了突触组织（synaptic organization）与非线性异质性群体动态之间的鸿沟，提供了关于精细尺度连接、异质性动态与功能计算之间关系的原则性方法（principled approach）和可检验预测（testable predictions）。

Abstract: Recent breakthroughs in synaptic-resolution network connectomics have revealed that brain circuits feature fine-scale structural connectivity, such as pairs of correlated synaptic couplings known as second-order motifs. Large-scale recordings of neuronal activity in networks containing nonlinear neurons reveal macroscopic heterogeneous population dynamics throughout the brain. These findings rekindle the inquiry into this intriguing question: Can microscale synaptic structures contribute to macroscopic heterogeneous dynamics and computations in ways that canonical brain circuit models cannot? To answer this question, we create random RNNs with various cell types, nonlinear non-negative neural responses, and arbitrary marginal and second-order correlated synaptic statistics. We derive mean-field low-rank equations for P-population networks in which the pre- and postsynaptic neuronal population identities determine the synaptic and motif strengths. Our framework requires 2P latent dynamic variables with P variables describing mean population activity and P variables capturing within-population variability. Theoretical and simulational results demonstrate that chain motifs induce correlations in synaptic variability, enabling microscopic fluctuations to be integrated and influence mesoscopic mean population dynamics. We apply this framework to reverse engineer network connectivity that recapitulates the heterogeneous activity across the population in the mouse primary visual cortex. By bridging the gap between synaptic organization and nonlinear heterogeneous population dynamics, our results offer a principled approach and testable predictions regarding the relationship between fine-scale connectivity, heterogeneous dynamics, and functional computations.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mtrl-sci'></div>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Ultrafast non-thermal suppression of ferroelectricity by carrier screening in LiNbO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27494)
*Man Tou Wong,Zhuquan Zhang,Zi-Jie Liu,Keith A. Nelson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文通过飞秒激光脉冲在铌酸锂（LiNbO₃）中释放俘获载流子，利用时间分辨二次谐波产生和受激拉曼散射探测，发现即使稀薄的光激发载流子也能快速且持续地抑制极化（polarization）和拉曼磁化率（Raman susceptibility），该抑制是非热效应、源于瞬态载流子屏蔽（transient carrier screening），展示了一种高效、可逆且对称性保持的超快铁电调制机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电材料（ferroelectric materials）在节能电子、存储和光学应用中至关重要，但载流子（charge carriers）在非平衡条件下的作用尚不明确（elusive），尤其需要理解载流子是否及如何影响超快时间尺度上的铁电性。

Method: 使用飞秒激光脉冲（femtosecond laser pulses）在 LiNbO₃ 中释放俘获载流子，通过时间分辨二次谐波产生（time-resolved second-harmonic generation）和受激拉曼散射（stimulated Raman scattering）跟踪响应；结合通量（fluence）和温度依赖性分析，排除热效应。

Result: 即使是稀薄（dilute）的光激发载流子也能诱导极化（polarization）和拉曼磁化率（Raman susceptibility）的快速且持续抑制；通量和温度依赖性分析确认该抑制是非热的（non-thermal），源于瞬态载流子屏蔽（transient carrier screening）。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了一种高效、可逆且对称性保持（symmetry-preserving）的机制，可在超快时间尺度上调制铁电性，为控制铁性（ferroic）和竞争量子相（competing quantum phases）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials are key to energy-efficient electronics, memory, and optical applications. While charge carriers typically screen and suppress ferroelectricity, their role under nonequilibrium conditions remains elusive. Here, we use femtosecond laser pulses to liberate trapped carriers in LiNbO3 and track the response using time-resolved second-harmonic generation and stimulated Raman scattering. Even dilute photoexcited carriers induce a rapid yet enduring suppression of polarization and Raman susceptibility. Fluence- and temperature-dependent analyses confirm the suppression is non-thermal and arises from transient carrier screening. These findings reveal an efficient, reversible, and symmetry-preserving mechanism to modulate ferroelectricity on ultrafast timescales, offering a new route to control ferroic and competing quantum phases.

</details>


### [8] [Mapping the Growth of Two-Dimensional $π$-Conjugated Polymers on Au(111): Organometallic Intermediates and Edge Terminations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27512)
*Simon W. Briesenick,Wyatt A. Behn,Manuel González Lastre,Chang Wan Kang,Pablo Pou,Ekaterina D. Ulyanov,Rubén Pérez,Dmytro F. Perepichka,Peter Grutter*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用扫描隧道显微镜（STM）、高分辨率原子力显微镜（AFM）和密度泛函理论（DFT），揭示了在Au(111)表面上通过三溴三氧杂三嗪（tribromotrioxaazatriangulene）前驱体构建Kagome晶格聚合物的过程中，存在此前未报道的有机金属中间态，并发现残留溴在稳定聚合物边缘及调控有序Kagome晶格生长路径中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome晶格为探索具有平带（flat bands）的类石墨烯π共轭分子体系提供了重要空间，然而在表面合成此类有序聚合物网络的生长机制尚不完全清楚，尤其是中间态结构和边缘化学环境对有序生长的调控作用有待揭示。

Method: 结合扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）与高分辨率原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy, AFM）对Au(111)表面的三溴三氧杂三嗪前驱体在Ullmann偶联过程中的演化进行表征，并辅以密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算分析。

Result: 发现了此前未被报道的有机金属中间态（organometallic intermediate states），其中金吸附原子（Au adatoms）掺入生长中的聚合物晶格；在高达250°C时，大部分聚合物边缘仍保持溴化状态，大量边缘还与Au adatoms成键，且这些Au adatoms与相邻溴原子配位。

Conclusion: 残留溴可能通过稳定聚合物边缘与Au adatoms的相互作用，进而影响有序Kagome聚合物晶格的生长路径（growth pathways）。

Abstract: Kagome lattices provide an exciting space for the exploration of graphene-like $π$-conjugated molecular systems with flat bands. Using heterotriangulene-derived precursors, along with an on-surface Ullmann coupling process, makes growing polymers with Kagome lattices accessible and straightforward. Here, we use scanning tunneling microscopy alongside high-resolution atomic force microscopy to examine the evolution of tribromotrioxaazatriangulene on Au(111) into ordered, covalent films. Using density functional theory and scanning probe methods, we find previously unreported organometallic intermediate states involving Au adatoms incorporated within the growing polymer lattice. We also find that a majority of polymer edges remain brominated up to 250 $^{\circ}$C and a large number of edges bonded to Au adatoms coordinated to an adjacent bromine atom. These observations suggest that residual bromine could play a role in stabilizing the polymer edges to Au adatoms and thereby influence the growth pathways that lead to ordered Kagome polymer lattices.

### [9] [A BRAVE Alloy Design Campaign (Bayesian Risk-aware Alloy discoVery and Exploration)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27522)
*Mrinalini Mulukutla,Danial Khatamsaz,Trevor Hastings,Wenle Xu,Daniel Salas,Joydeep Kundu,Vasanth C. Shunmugasamy,Daniel Lewis,Jacob Hempel,Clinton Strosser,Alexandra Salinas,Brent Vela,Nicolas Flores,Sina Hossein Zadeh,Ali Rachidi,David Elbert,Brady Butler,James Paramore,Dimitris Lagoudas,Justin Wilkerson,George Pharr,Douglas Allaire,Vahid Attari,Ibrahim Karaman,Ankit Srivastava,Raymundo Arróyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过风险感知贝叶斯优化（risk-aware Bayesian optimization）在Al-V-Cr-Mn-Fe-Co-Ni-Cu体系单相FCC高熵合金中，利用可行性分类器在采集函数中概率性惩罚可能失败的候选成分，成功探索了位于相稳定性边界的高性能合金区域，发现了两个性能迥异的成分区间，并验证了约束最优解位于有效约束边界（active constraint boundaries）的KKT条件预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在约束合金优化中，性能潜力最高的成分往往位于相稳定性边界（phase stability boundary），但该区域实验失败风险也最高，传统硬过滤（hard filtering）方法会完全排除这类高潜力区域，亟需一种能够兼顾性能与可行性风险的方法。

Method: 采用风险感知贝叶斯优化（risk-aware Bayesian optimization）框架，将学习的可行性分类器（feasibility classifier）直接集成到多目标采集函数（multi-objective acquisition function）中，对可能导致实验失败的候选成分进行概率性惩罚，同时保留对高绩效边界成分的访问权。

Result: 从约27,000个经CALPHAD筛选的候选成分中，经过三轮闭环迭代合成48种合金（覆盖0.12%的可行空间），发现两个成分区间：富V、富Ni的高强度区（UTS达~1480 MPa，延伸率50%）和含Mn的高延展区（UTS/YS达4.20，延伸率>50%）。V同时驱动屈服强度（r=0.84）和σ相形成（r=0.54）；在24 at.% V处，三种最强合金与三种σ相失效共享同一成分点。最强性能合金集中在V≥20 at.%、Ni≥36 at.%的狭窄区域内（约100/27,074个可行候选），随机采样概率P≈6.5×10⁻⁶。

Conclusion: V在合金中扮演双重角色——同时提升强度并诱导σ相失效，这与约束最优解位于有效约束边界（active constraint boundaries）的KKT条件（Karush-Kuhn-Tucker conditions）预测一致，验证了可行性感知采集（feasibility-aware acquisition）的必要性：硬过滤会完全排除该高潜力区域。

Abstract: In constrained alloy optimization, the compositions with the highest performance potential often reside at the boundary of phase stability -- where the risk of experimental failure is also highest. This work demonstrates this principle through a risk-aware Bayesian optimization campaign on single-phase FCC high-entropy alloys in the Al-V-Cr-Mn-Fe-Co-Ni-Cu system. A learned feasibility classifier, integrated directly into the multi-objective acquisition function, probabilistically penalizes candidates likely to produce failed experiments while preserving access to high-performing boundary compositions. From approximately 27,000 CALPHAD-screened candidates, 48 alloys were synthesized over three closed-loop iterations targeting five objectives (yield strength, UTS/YS ratio, strain at UTS, dynamic-to-quasi-static hardness ratio, and simulated depth of penetration), exploring 0.12\% of the feasible space. Two compositional regimes emerged: a V-rich, Ni-rich high-strength regime (UTS up to ${\sim}1480$~MPa at 50% elongation) and a Mn-containing high-ductility regime (UTS/YS up to 4.20 at $>$50% elongation). Among feasible alloys, vanadium simultaneously drives yield strength ($r = 0.84$) and sigma-phase formation ($r = 0.54$ with infeasibility); at V = 24~at.%, the three strongest alloys and three sigma failures share the same compositional point. Additionally, the strongest performing alloys cluster in a narrow region of compositional space (V $\geq$ 20 at.%, Ni $\geq$ 36 at.%), representing ${\sim}100$ of $27,074$ feasible candidates -- a probability of $P \approx 6.5 \times 10^{-6}$ under random sampling. This dual role -- consistent with the KKT prediction that constrained optima lie on active constraint boundaries -- required feasibility-aware acquisition to access; hard filtering would have excluded this region entirely.

### [10] [PtyRANNOSAUR: Ptychography with Robust Artificial Neural Networks Optimized for Sub-Angstrom Accuracy and Ultrafast Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27587)
*Kieran Loehr,Rahim Raja,Xiaochuan Ding,Jeffrey Huang,Gillian Nolan,Sang hyun Bae,Bryan K. Clark,Pinshane Y. Huang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电子叠层成像（electron ptychography）重构方法计算速度慢，难以满足近实时（near-live）重构需求，且对超参数调优敏感。

Method: 采用卷积自编码器（convolutional autoencoders）将4D-扫描透射电子显微镜（4D-scanning transmission electron microscopy, 4D-STEM）数据映射为2维相位图像。模型在大规模晶体结构数据库上训练，可针对加速电压、会聚角（convergence angle）、离焦量（defocus）和样品厚度等实验参数进行定制，无需超参数微调，并能处理空间部分相干（spatial partial coherence）、多次散射（multiple scattering）和扫描位置误差（scan position errors）。

Result: 在实验与模拟数据上，PtyRANNOSAUR能够准确重构多种材料体系的原子结构，分辨率可达0.5 Å以下，与最优迭代重构方法相当，计算速度提升10–100倍。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了近实时、高水平的电子叠层成像重构，为数据驱动的原子尺度成像提供了高效可行的新途径。

Abstract: We present PtyRANNOSAUR, a data-driven neural network code that reconstructs atomic resolution electron ptychography data in seconds, 10-100x faster than standard methods. PtyRANNOSAUR uses convolutional autoencoders to map 4D-scanning transmission electron microscopy data to 2D phase images. Each model is trained on a large database of crystal structures and is tailored for a range of experimental parameters, such as accelerating voltage, convergence angle, defocus, and sample thickness. This approach yields high quality reconstructions without requiring any fine-tuning of hyperparameters. In addition, the code handles spatial partial coherence, multiple scattering, and scan position errors, which are critical for state-of-the-art electron ptychography reconstructions. By testing PtyRANNOSAUR on experimental and simulated data, we show that the neural networks accurately reconstruct atomic structures of a broad range of materials systems and can achieve high resolutions of $<0.5$ Å, comparable to the best iterative reconstructions of the same data. These advances enable near-live, state-of-the-art electron ptychography reconstructions.

Abstract: Resonators are a key component in modern communications and computing. Here, we utilize prototypical dielectric-ferroelectric SrTiO3/PbTiO3 superlattices to robustly design periodic ferroelectric nano-scale domains. Complex polar textures in these superlattices lead to emergent piezoelectric properties that also result in millimeter-wave resonances, which are predicted by second principles methods and confirmed by direct measurement. The principles investigated in this work suggest a new modality for ferroelectrics in the design of millimeter-wave electronics.

*Yitao Jiao,Zhenhao Fan,Dawei Wang,Hai-Feng Li*

Conclusion: 熵工程是提升无铅铁电陶瓷（lead-free ferroelectric ceramics）击穿强度和储能性能的有效途径，为高性能介电电容器的开发提供了新思路。

Abstract: Dielectric capacitors are promising for pulsed power applications, but the energy storage performance of lead-free bulk ceramics is often limited by low breakdown strength and large ferroelectric hysteresis. Herein, a high entropy perovskite oxide BaTi0.2Zr0.2Sn0.2Hf0.2Nb0.1Sc0.1O3 was introduced into the BF-BT matrix to develop lead free high entropy ferroelectric ceramics. Multicomponent B-site substitution induces lattice distortion, enhanced pseudocubic characteristics, relaxor behavior, and grain refinement. These effects suppress polarization hysteresis and electrical conduction, resulting in a significant increase in breakdown strength. A maximum breakdown strength of 840 kV/cm1 and a recoverable energy density of 10.55 J/cm3 were achieved. Entropy-induced microstructural heterogeneity promotes a more uniform electric-field distribution and delays dielectric breakdown. This work demonstrates entropy engineering as an effective route to achieving high breakdown strength and superior energy-storage performance in lead-free ferroelectric ceramics.

### [14] [CoTAR: Topology and Atomic State Reconstruction in Condensed Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27636)
*Hodaka Mori,Yu Miyazaki,Takechika Kikkawa*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出CoTAR——一种混合图神经网络（GNN）与隐马尔可夫模型（HMM）的框架，能够从原子种类、坐标和总电荷中重建分子拓扑、形式电荷和未配对电子，在128个凝聚态系统上实现了高精度，并将通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIP）轨迹的有效快照率从38.6%提升至84.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIP）虽能实现近第一性原理精度的凝聚相分子动力学（MD）模拟，但其缺乏显式分子拓扑，限制了基于键的分析以及与经典力场的衔接。

Method: CoTAR框架将图神经网络（GNN）与隐马尔可夫模型（HMM）相结合，在近邻图上进行消息传递，并引入范德华先验、化学约束和时间平滑机制。

Result: 在128个非反应性、拓扑保持的凝聚相系统中，CoTAR在经典MD数据上的键序加权F1分数达到0.906；在uMLIP轨迹上，少样本微调将有效快照率从38.6%提升至84.7%。HMM平滑将系统级MD模拟可行性从83.6%提升至85.9%。

Conclusion: CoTAR为凝聚相uMLIP轨迹的基于键分析提供了一个实用框架。

Abstract: Universal machine learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) enable condensed-phase molecular dynamics (MD) simulations with near-first-principles accuracy, but their lack of explicit molecular topology limits bond-aware analysis and reconnection to classical force fields. Here, we present CoTAR, a hybrid graph neural network (GNN)--hidden Markov model (HMM) framework that reconstructs molecular topology, formal charges, and unpaired electrons from atomic species, coordinates, and total charge by combining message passing on a proximity graph with a van der Waals prior, chemical constraints, and temporal smoothing. Across 128 nonreactive, topology-preserving condensed-phase systems, CoTAR achieved a bond-order-weighted F1 score of 0.906 on classical-MD data; for uMLIP trajectories, few-shot fine-tuning improved the valid-snapshot rate from 38.6\% to 84.7\%. The reconstructed topologies also supported downstream classical MD simulations, and HMM smoothing improved system-level MD simulation feasibility from 83.6\% to 85.9\%, indicating that CoTAR provides a practical framework for bond-aware analysis of condensed-phase uMLIP trajectories.

*D. Y. Park,S. Park,Yongmin Kim,N. Myoung,Z. Yang,Y. Kohama,Y. H. Matsuda*

TL;DR: 本研究通过圆偏振磁致光致发光测量，在高达50 T的脉冲磁场中研究了二维手性钙钛矿R-和S-(C4H9NH3)2PbI4对映体，发现其具有强圆偏振发射偏好、反常的激子跃迁红移以及磁场增强发光等现象，并用Rashba自旋劈裂（Rashba spin-splitting）和极化子形成（polaron formation）进行了解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维手性钙钛矿（two-dimensional chiral perovskites）在强磁场下的光学性质，揭示其手性结构与激发态自旋/能带结构之间的耦合机制。

Method: 在4.2 K温度下，对R-和S-(C4H9NH3)2PbI4对映体施加高达50 T的脉冲磁场，进行圆偏振磁致光致发光（circularly polarized magneto-photoluminescence, MPL）测量。

Result: (1) R型优先发射右旋圆偏振光（RC通道），强度比I_RC/I_LC = 10:1，S型则偏好左旋，且该偏好不受磁场影响；(2) 激子跃迁能量随磁场增加出现反常红移（anomalous redshift），与无手性钙钛矿的正常抗磁蓝移相反，且R型主导RC通道中在7.6 T以下存在非单调的初始蓝移；(3) PL峰位对磁场方向反转完全不变，符合Rashba效应导致亮激子与邻近m_x=0暗态混合的预期；(4) 磁场导致PL强度增加和线宽变窄，归因于回旋轨道收缩抑制了无序散射。

Conclusion: 二维手性钙钛矿在强磁场下的反常光学行为可通过Rashba自旋劈裂（Rashba spin-splitting）和极化子形成（polaron formation）框架得到合理解释，揭示了手性晶格与激子自旋-轨道耦合之间的深层关联。

Abstract: We report circularly polarized magneto-photoluminescence (MPL) measurements on the enantiomeric pair of two-dimensional chiral perovskites R- and S-(C4H9NH3)2PbI4 in pulsed magnetic fields up to 50 T at 4.2 K. The R-form exhibits strong preferential emission into the RC channel (I_RC/I_LC = 10:1), with the S-form showing the opposite sense, robust against the applied field. Three key observations are reported: (i) an anomalous redshift of all exciton transition energies with increasing field-contrasting with the normal diamagnetic blueshift of achiral perovskites-with a non-monotonic initial blueshift to 7.6 T in the dominant RC channel of the R-form; (ii) complete invariance of PL peak positions upon reversal of the field direction, consistent with Rashba-induced mixing of the bright exciton with a nearby m_x = 0 dark state; and (iii) field-induced increase in PL intensity and narrowing of the linewidth, attributed to suppression of disorder scattering as the cyclotron orbit contracts. These results are interpreted in the framework of Rashba spin-splitting and polaron formation in the chiral two-dimensional perovskite lattice.

</details>


### [16] [Amorphous Fe-Sn nanofilms for anomalous-Nernst heat-flux sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27716)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 系统控制成分（composition）和厚度（thickness）制备纳米厚非晶Fe-Sn薄膜；使用X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction, XRD）和穆斯堡尔谱（Mössbauer spectroscopy）表征结构；在刚性基底和柔性聚合物基底（flexible polymer substrates）上测试性能。

Result: 优化后的非晶Fe-Sn纳米薄膜结合了大反常能斯特响应与低热导率，热通量灵敏度（heat-flux sensitivity）达0.37 um/A，超过已报道的非晶磁性薄膜和代表性晶体拓扑磁体（crystalline topological magnets）。该灵敏度在柔性聚合物基底上可复现。

Conclusion: 非晶Fe-Sn纳米薄膜为反常能斯特热通量传感提供了一种材料平台，并提出了基于局域结构控制（local-structure control）和热导率降低（thermal-conductivity reduction）的材料设计路线。

Abstract: Amorphous magnetic films are promising for anomalous-Nernst heat-flux sensing because their low thermal conductivity can enhance the temperature gradient generated by an applied heat flux. However, amorphization often degrades electronic transport and thermoelectric properties, making it challenging to obtain a large anomalous Nernst response in structurally disordered films. Here, we demonstrate nanometer-thick amorphous Fe-Sn films as high-sensitivity anomalous-Nernst heat-flux sensing materials. By systematically controlling composition and thickness, we find that amorphous Fe-Sn nanofilms combine a large anomalous Nernst response with low thermal conductivity, resulting in a heat-flux sensitivity of 0.37 um/A. This value exceeds the sensitivities reported for both amorphous magnetic thin films and representative crystalline topological magnets. X-ray diffraction and Mossbauer spectroscopy show that the optimized films lack long-range crystallinity while retaining local Fe-Sn environments, suggesting that short-range atomic order contributes to the anomalous Nernst response in the amorphous matrix. The sensitivity is also reproduced on flexible polymer substrates, indicating compatibility with mechanically compliant device architectures. These results establish amorphous Fe-Sn nanofilms as a platform for anomalous-Nernst heat-flux sensing and provide a materials design route based on local-structure control and thermal-conductivity reduction.

### [17] [Vacancy-mediated nitrogen diffusion and aggregation via high-fluence electron beam irradiation in HPHT synthesized diamond crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27723)
*Chikara Shinei,Yuta Masuyama,Jun Chen,Hiroshi. Abe,Masashi Miyakawa,Takashi Taniguchi,Takeshi Ohshima,Tokuyuki Teraji*

TL;DR: 本研究通过室温电子束辐照（EBI）和退火处理，在含氮高压高温金刚石中实现取代氮向NV色心的转化。低辐照注量下，Ns0浓度下降、NV0和NV-浓度上升，转化过程占主导；高辐照注量下，各类缺陷浓度均下降，形成H3中心等未知含氮缺陷，且H3中心的形成温度（约1375°C）低于文献报道值（>1600°C），归因于空位介导的氮扩散与聚集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对氮掺杂的高压高温（HPHT）金刚石晶体进行室温电子束辐照（EBI）和后续退火处理，通过改变辐照注量，监测中性取代氮（Ns0）、NV0、NV-及Ns+等缺陷浓度的变化，并在高注量区观察H3中心（氮与空位的聚集缺陷）的形成行为。

Result: 低辐照注量区：Ns0浓度下降，NV0和NV-浓度上升，且Ns0减少量与总NV增加量相当。高辐照注量区：NV0、NV-、Ns0和Ns+浓度均随注量增加而下降，表明形成了未知的含氮缺陷。H3中心在高注量下形成，但其形成退火温度为1375±25°C，显著低于文献报道的1600°C以上。

Conclusion: 低注量下从Ns0到NV0和NV-的转化是主导的缺陷形成过程。高注量下H3中心在较低温度下形成，归因于空位介导的氮扩散与聚集（vacancy-mediated nitrogen diffusion and aggregation）机制。

Abstract: The negatively charged nitrogen vacancy (NV-) center in diamonds is promising point defect for highly sensitive quantum sensing. The formation of high-density NV- centers is essential for improving sensitivity. We performed room-temperature electron beam irradiation (EBI) and annealing on nitrogen-doped high-pressure high-temperature diamond crystals to convert substitutional nitrogen into NV centers. In the low-fluence region of EBI, neutral substitutional nitrogen (Ns0) concentration decreased and NV0 and NV- center concentration increased with increasing EBI fluence. The decrease in Ns0 concentration was comparable to the increase in total NV center concentration; thus, the conversion from Ns0 to NV0 and NV- centers is a dominant defect formation process. In a high-fluence region, NV0 and NV- center and Ns0 and Ns+ concentrations decreased with increasing EBI fluence, indicating the formation of unknown nitrogen-related defects such as the H3 center, which is a nitrogen and vacancy aggregation defect. Although H3 centers were observed at high EBI fluence, their forming annealing temperature of 1375 +- 25 degrees Celsius was lower than the typically reported temperatures over 1600 degrees Celsius. We attribute this low-temperature formation to vacancy-mediated nitrogen diffusion and aggregation.

### [18] [Three-dimensional visualization of threading dislocation in GaN by polarized-light microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27744)
*Yukari Ishikawa,Kisara Matsumoto,Kazuki Ohnishi,Yongzhao Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用偏振光显微镜（polarized-light microscopy）配合准直LED照明进行高通量三维成像，结合同步辐射X射线形貌术验证位错迹线几何与伯格斯矢量方向的关系。

Result: 穿透位错表现出与焦深相关的面内位移，由此可观察其三维倾斜行为；具有相同面内伯格斯矢量分量的位错显示出相似的迹线几何和倾斜方向；位错相对c轴倾斜约3.3°，方向垂直于伯格斯矢量。

Conclusion: 该技术提供了一种简单、无损且可用于大面积GaN晶圆三维位错表征的方法，位错倾斜行为暗示生长过程中存在攀移介导的应变弛豫机制。

Abstract: We demonstrate high-throughput three-dimensional imaging of threading dislocations in ammonothermal GaN wafers using polarized-light microscopy with collimated LED illumination. Threading dislocations exhibited focal-depth-dependent in-plane shifts, enabling visualization of their three-dimensional inclination behavior over large areas. Synchrotron radiation X-ray topography indicated that dislocations with identical in-plane Burgers vector components tended to exhibit similar trace geometries and inclination directions. The threading dislocations were found to be tilted by approximately 3.3° from the c-axis in directions perpendicular to their Burgers vectors, indicating climb-mediated motion associated with strain relaxation during crystal growth. These results demonstrate a simple nondestructive approach for large-area three-dimensional characterization of dislocations in GaN wafers.

### [19] [Single-Crystalline Al/Ge Heterostructure with an Atomically Sharp Commensurate Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27854)
*Jian-Huan Wang,Ding-Ming Huang,Han Gao,Yuan Yao,H. Q. Xu,Jian-Jun Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）在Ge(111)衬底上成功实现了单晶Al(111)的外延生长，获得了原子级平整且尖锐的界面，并观察到7-Al/5-Ge的共格外延关系，将晶格失配从28.4%降至约0.1%。研究发现界面形成存在约0.3 nm的临界厚度，低于该厚度时Al以随机团簇形式成核，随后演变为二维岛状结构并最终形成连续薄膜。优化生长参数后，获得了表面均方根粗糙度约0.16 nm、厚度仅2 nm的超平坦超薄Al膜，为拓扑量子态研究提供了有前景的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）技术在Ge(111)衬底上外延生长单晶Al(111)薄膜。通过控制生长参数，研究Al初始成核与生长的动态过程，并利用多种表征手段分析界面结构、表面形貌及薄膜连续性。

Result: 实现了单晶Al(111)在Ge(111)上的外延生长，界面处存在7-Al/5-Ge的共格（commensurate）外延关系，将固有晶格失配从28.4%大幅降低至约0.1%。界面形成存在约0.3 nm的临界厚度，低于该厚度时Al以随机团簇成核，随后转变为二维岛状结构，最终发展为连续薄膜。优化生长后获得表面均方根粗糙度约0.16 nm、厚度仅2 nm的超平坦超薄Al连续薄膜。

Conclusion: 所制备的外延Al-Ge异质结构具有原子级平整表面和尖锐界面，为研究拓扑量子态（topological quantum states）提供了有前景的材料平台。

Abstract: A key challenge in developing Al/Ge heterostructures for quantum applications is Al-Ge interdiffusion. This process is facilitated by grain boundaries in polycrystalline films, which degrades interface quality and impairs device performance and reliability. Here, we present epitaxial growth of single-crystalline Al(111) on Ge(111) by molecular beam epitaxy, achieving an atomically flat and sharp interface. At the interface, a commensurate 7-Al-lattice/5-Ge-lattice epitaxial relationship is observed, which dramatically reduces the intrinsic lattice mismatch from 28.4% to about 0.1%. Interestingly, this well-ordered interface does not form below a critical thickness of 0.3 nm. Instead, Al initially nucleates as random clusters, which then transform into two-dimensional (2D) islands and, as Al deposition further increases, eventually develop into a continuous film. By optimizing the growth parameters, we have achieved an ultra-flat Al film with a surface root-mean-square roughness of about 0.16 nm and an ultra-thin continuous film with thickness of only 2 nm. These epitaxially grown Al-Ge heterostructures, with their atomically flat surfaces and sharp interfaces, provide a promising platform for studying topological quantum states.

### [20] [Unlocking Cryogenic Energy Storage by Constructing Dipole Glass with Unit-cell-level Polar Disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27887)
*Yangyang Si,Denan Li,Yijie Li,Changsheng Chen,Jingxuan Li,Chao Zhou,Hao Xiong,Tianfu Zhang,Wenjin Liao,Zhongqi Ren,Huaicheng Yuan,Dong Li,Jing-Kai Qin,Cheng-Yan Xu,Ye Zhu,Yunlong Tang,Sujit Das,Jieun Kim,Junling Wang,Hao Pan,Fei Li,Zhen Chen,Shi Liu,Zuhuang Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过在反铁电-顺电（antiferroelectric-paraelectric）相界附近的Pb0.6Sr0.4ZrO3薄膜中设计单胞尺度的无序偶极玻璃态（dipole-glass state），实现了在4 K低温下效率>88%、能量密度211 J/cm³的超高性能，为低温介电电容器（cryogenic dielectric capacitors）提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低温储能（cryogenic energy storage）对深空探测、量子计算等前沿技术至关重要，但传统电化学储能系统在约230 K以下因离子迁移冻结而失效。弛豫基（relaxor-based）介电电容器虽在室温下高效，但极低温下极性纳米畴（polar nanodomains）的冻结/生长导致滞后损耗（hysteresis losses）恶化，限制了应用。

Method: 在反铁电-顺电相界（antiferroelectric-paraelectric phase boundary）附近，通过组分设计在Pb0.6Sr0.4ZrO3薄膜中构建单胞尺度（unit-cell-level）无序偶极玻璃态，利用反铁电衍生的偶极玻璃引入增强的单胞级偶极相互作用复杂性，抑制长程铁电序（long-range ferroelectric order）。

Result: 实现了低至4 K的超低滞后运行，效率>88%，在9 MV/cm电场下达到创纪录的211 J/cm³能量密度，且具有超过10^8次充放电循环的稳定性和微秒级充放电能力。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了用于低温介电电容器的偶极玻璃范式（dipole-glass paradigm），为前沿纳米电子学（nanoelectronics）中的高效储能系统开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Cryogenic energy storage is vital for frontier technologies including deep-space exploration and quantum computing, yet conventional electrochemical energy systems fail below ~230 K due to frozen ion migration. While relaxor-based dielectric capacitors provide high efficiency at room temperature, the intrinsic freezing/growth of polar nanodomains at extended cryogenic regime limits their applications with deteriorated hysteresis losses. Here, we realize superior cryogenic energy-storage performance by designing unit-cell-level disordered dipole-glass state in Pb0.6Sr0.4ZrO3 thin films with composition near antiferroelectric-paraelectric phase boundary. The antiferroelectric-derived dipole-glass introduces enhanced unit-cell-level complexity of dipole interaction that suppresses long-range ferroelectric order. This enables ultralow-hysteresis operation (efficiency > 88%) down to 4 K, delivering record-high energy density (211 J/cm^3) at 9 MV/cm, stability over 10^8 charge/discharge cycles and microsecond-scale charge/discharge capability. This work establishes a dipole-glass paradigm for cryogenic dielectric capacitors, opening a new avenue to highly-efficient energy-storage systems with broad applications in frontier nanoelectronics.

</details>


### [21] [Symmetry-Selective Strain Control of Spin-Momentum Locking and Spin Transport in Two-Dimensional Pentagonal Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27896)
*ShuaiYu Wang,Sheng Chen,Xiao-Ping Li,Lei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于对称性分析构建了二维五边形交变磁体（altermagnet）的应变解析框架，识别出94种稳定交变磁体候选材料，并将其分为三类应变响应类型，展示了铁弹、剪切和单轴应变对自旋分裂与输运特性的不同调控效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）具有依赖动量的非相对论性自旋劈裂（spin splitting），其自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking, SML）可通过实空间对称操作调控。当前缺乏系统性的应变框架来分类和预测不同应变对SML的影响。

Method: 构建了基于对称性的应变解析框架，分类单轴应变（uniaxial strain）和剪切应变（shear strain）张量对SML的三种影响：保持、重构或消除。结合第一性原理筛选（first-principles screening），从3330种材料中识别出94种稳定的交变磁体候选材料，覆盖正交晶系所有type-III自旋Laue群（spin Laue groups）。

Result: 94种候选材料被分为三类应变响应类型：Type-I保持SML；Type-II通过部分对称性破缺重构SML但保留关键交变磁性特征；Type-III彻底破坏SML。代表性材料中，铁弹α-CoS₂表现出可铁弹切换的SML并反转非对角自旋电导率符号；剪切应变α-CoP₂发生g波到d波SML重构，激活非对角自旋电导率；单轴应变FeSSe实现应变选择的自旋-谷输运。

Conclusion: 该工作为二维正交交变磁体中应变控制的输运提供了理论框架和材料指导。

Abstract: Altermagnets are compensated magnets featuring momentum-dependent nonrelativistic spin splitting generated by nontrivial operations connecting opposite-spin sublattices. A direct symmetry-based route to control this spin splitting is to modify the real-space operations that define the altermagnetic spin-momentum locking (SML). Here, we develop a strain-resolved symmetry framework for two-dimensional pentagonal altermagnets, classifying whether uniaxial and shear strain tensors preserve, reconstruct, or eliminate the SML. Using the above criterion combined with first-principles screening, we identify 94 stable altermagnetic candidates from 3330 materials. These candidates cover all type-III spin Laue groups of orthorhombic lattices and are classified into three strain-response types: Type-I preserves the SML; Type-II reconstructs the SML through partial symmetry breaking while retaining essential altermagnetic features; and Type-III destroys the altermagnetic SML. Representative materials further demonstrate this classification: ferroelastic $α$-CoS$_2$ exhibits ferroelastically switchable SML and reverses the sign of the off-diagonal spin conductivity; shear-strained \(α\)-CoP\(_2\) undergoes a \(g\)- to \(d\)-wave reconstruction of the SML, activating off-diagonal spin conductivity; and uniaxially strained FeSSe realizes strain-selected spin-valley transport. This work provides theoretical and material guidance for strain-controlled transport in two-dimensional orthorhombic altermagnets.

</details>


### [22] [In situ synchrotron X-ray diffraction study of flash austenitization and process design insights in medium-Manganese steels for energy applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28072)
*Bowen Zou,Mathias Zapf,Thea Kannenberg,Daniel Schneider,Yixu Wang,Xiao Shen,Ulrich Prahl,Wenwen Song*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过原位同步辐射X射线衍射（in situ synchrotron X-ray diffraction）结合膨胀测量法（dilatometry），系统量化了中锰钢（Medium Mn steel）在快速奥氏体化（flash austenitization）条件下，温度和初始微观组织对奥氏体化动力学（austenitization kinetics）的影响，发现快速加热本身不足以实现完全奥氏体化，需要短时等温保持，且动力学行为对温度的敏感性随保温阶段不同而变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中锰钢因其多相微观组织和可调控的奥氏体稳定性，在能源相关基础设施中具有应用前景。快速奥氏体化可在限制粗化和成分均匀化的前提下快速形成奥氏体，但其短时相变动力学（short-time transformation kinetics）尚未被充分量化，缺乏系统的实验数据支持工艺优化。

Method: 以Fe-6Mn-1.5Si-1Cr-0.3Mo-0.05Nb-0.2C (wt.%)中锰钢为对象，通过奥氏体回复处理（austenite reversion treatment, ART）制备两种初始微观组织，以100°C/s的速率加热至850°C、900°C或950°C后进行等温保持，并采用膨胀测量法集成的原位同步辐射X射线衍射进行实时表征。

Result: 快速加热即使在慢速加热测定的参考Ac3温度以上也无法实现完全奥氏体化；完全奥氏体化（以bcc相分数f_α ≤ 1 wt.%定义）需要短时等温保持，所需时间从850°C下的约8秒降至950°C下的约2秒；奥氏体化后期阶段对温度的敏感性低于早期阶段；初始ART状态主要影响起始奥氏体分数，但在较高FA温度下两种状态的动力学趋势相近。

Conclusion: 中锰钢的快速奥氏体化并非仅由升温过程完成，后续短时等温保持至关重要；FA温度对动力学的影响存在阶段性差异；初始微观组织的影响在高温下趋于弱化，为工艺调控提供了定量依据。

Abstract: Medium Mn steels (MMnSs) are promising candidates for energy-related infrastructure because their multiphase microstructures and austenite stability can be tailored to improve failure resistance under demanding service conditions. Flash austenitization (FA) provides a rapid route to form austenite while limiting prior austenite grain coarsening and substitutional solute homogenization, but the related short-time transformation kinetics remain insufficiently quantified. In the present work, the effects of FA temperature and initial microstructure on austenitization kinetics were investigated in an Fe-6Mn-1.5Si-1Cr-0.3Mo-0.05Nb-0.2C (wt.%) MMnS using dilatometry-integrated in situ synchrotron X-ray diffraction. Two initial microstructures produced by austenite reversion treatment (ART) were heated at 100 degrees C/s to 850 degrees C, 900 degrees C, or 950 degrees C and then held isothermally. Rapid heating alone is insufficient for full austenitization, even above the reference Ac3 temperature determined under slow heating. Full austenitization, defined by bcc fraction (f_alpha) <= 1 wt.%, requires short holding, decreasing from about 8 s at 850 degrees C to about 2 s at 950 degrees C. The final stage of austenitization is less sensitive to FA temperature than the early holding stage. The initial ART state mainly shifts the starting austenite fraction, whereas both states show comparable kinetic trends at higher FA temperatures.

</details>


### [23] [Room-temperature magnon-phonon transduction in high-damping Co/Pt structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28073)
*Gauravkumar Patel,Takuma Sato,Maximilian Frenzel,Prakriti P. Joshi,Ruslan Salikhov,Ievgeniia Korniienko,Dominik Legut,Olav Hellwig,Sebastian F. Maehrlein,Kilian Lenz,Jürgen Lindner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用精心设计的磁性-非磁性异质结构（Co/Pt），使定域剪切驻波声子与铁磁共振磁子发生共振耦合，并通过实验和理论建模验证了能量与角动量的交换，为CMOS兼容材料中的量子换能器提供了理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子通信与信息处理受益于不同准粒子（quasi-particle）之间的耦合，磁弹性材料（magnetoelastic materials）天然支持磁子（magnon）与声子（phonon）之间的直接耦合，有望实现无需磁性材料的远程磁信息传输。然而，如何高效、可控地实现这一耦合是当前的关键挑战。

Method: 采用具有Pt种子层的Co薄膜磁性-非磁性异质结构，该结构同时充当剪切驻波（standing shear waves）的谐振腔，使选择性声子与磁子产生共振。结合理论建模与超快相干声子谱学（ultra-fast coherent phonon spectroscopy）识别参与耦合的横声学声子。

Result: 声子共振的铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）谱线展宽且幅度降低，标志着能量与角动量的交换。识别出耦合声子为Co/Pt复合结构中的剪切驻波。材料具有高晶体质量与大的磁弹性耦合常数（magnetoelastic coupling constant），这是高效磁子-声子耦合的前提。

Conclusion: 在CMOS兼容材料中实现了磁子-声子共振增强耦合，为未来量子换能器（quantum transducer）提供了理想的材料平台。

Abstract: Quantum communication and information processing strongly benefit from the coupling between different quasi-particles, offering complementary advantages. Magnetoelastic materials inherently allow for direct coupling between magnetization dynamics and quantized lattice vibrations, called phonons. Near the ferromagnetic resonances, phonons may thus trade energy and angular momentum with uniformly precessing magnetization, called magnons, and enable transduction of information from magnetic to phononic modes, thereby paving the way for long-range transport of magnetic information without the need of magnetic material. Here, we employ tailored magnetic-nonmagnetic heterostructures, which simultaneously act as cavities for standing shear waves, to bring selective phonons and magnons into resonance. These Co films with Pt seed layers show extended linewidth and reduced amplitude of the phonon-resonant FMR lines, providing a hallmark of energy and angular momentum exchange. Complementarily, by theoretical modeling and ultra-fast coherent phonon spectroscopy, we identify the responsible transverse acoustic phonons as standing shear waves in the combined Co and Pt structure. We find a high crystal quality in conjunction with a large magnetoelastic coupling constant as a prerequisite for efficient magnon-phonon coupling of this type. Such resonant enhancement of magnon-phonon coupling in CMOS-compatible material provides an ideal material platform for future quantum transducers.

</details>


### [24] [Tuning the optoelectronic properties of wide bandgap perovskites: Data-driven insights from combinatorial synthesis and high-throughput experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28093)
*Alexander Wieczorek,Sergey Tsarev,Nathan Rodkey,Oleksandr Pshyk,Stefanie Frick,Maksym V. Kovalenko,Sebastian Siol*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文建立了一种基于顺序物理气相沉积（physical vapor deposition）的组合工作流，可在Cs-Pb-Br-Cl四元空间中独立调控阳离子和阴离子组分，通过高通量筛选揭示了宽带隙钙钛矿（wide-bandgap perovskite）的高光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）产率与特定Cs/Pb比例（1.05–1.20）及高能光学跃迁之间的关联，并公开了完整的多模态数据集以加速数据驱动的材料发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宽带隙铅卤钙钛矿（wide-bandgap lead halide perovskites, LHPs）的发现与优化受限于可扩展性差的溶液基工作流程，且其庞大的组分参数空间为材料优化带来了额外挑战，亟需建立一种可独立调控组分的高通量筛选方法。

Method: 研究基于顺序物理气相沉积（sequential physical vapor deposition）构建了集成化组合工作流，实现对阳离子（Cs/Pb）和阴离子（Br/Cl）组分的独立调控；在超过500个样品兴趣区域上应用自动化结构、组分和光学表征，快速筛选四元Cs-Pb-Br-Cl组分空间。

Result: 筛选确定了宽带隙钙钛矿的实用Cs/Pb窗口为1.05–1.20，该范围内观测到较高的光致发光（PL）产率；进一步分析数据发现，一种高能光学跃迁（high-energy optical transition）可作为高PL产率的稳健判定指标。

Conclusion: 本文将高PL效率的组分起源的机理洞察与全集成的高通量筛选框架相结合，并公开了完整的多模态数据集（multi-modal dataset），为加速宽带隙钙钛矿的数据驱动发现提供了广泛可获取的基准。

Abstract: The discovery and optimization of wide-bandgap lead halide perovskites (LHPs) is hindered by solution-based workflows with limited scalability. Large compositional parameter spaces present an additional challenge for materials optimization. Here, we establish an integrated, combinatorial workflow based on sequential physical vapor deposition that enables independent tuning of cation (Cs/Pb) and anion (Br/Cl) compositions. Applying automated structural, compositional, and optical characterizations across >500 samples regions of interest are rapidly screened in the quaternary Cs-Pb-Br-Cl space. From the screening, we establish a practical Cs/Pb window of 1.05-1.20 for wide bandgap perovskites, within which elevated PL yields were observed. Through in-depth analysis of the data set, we uncover a high-energy optical transition as a robust determinant for high PL yields. By combining mechanistic insight into the compositional origins of high PL efficiency with a fully integrated, high-throughput screening framework, and by openly releasing the complete multi-modal dataset, this work provides a broadly accessible benchmark to accelerate data-driven discovery of wide-bandgap perovskites.

### [25] [Uniaxial compression of crystalline HCP titanium: an atomistic modelling study of size effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28155)
*Fatemeh Safari,Konstantinos Konstantinou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，系统探究了模型尺寸和应变速率对压缩状态下α-钛（alpha-titanium）力学响应的影响。结果发现弹性性质对尺寸与应变速率不敏感，而塑性变形阶段表现出显著的尺寸效应；系统尺寸与应变速率之间存在强耦合关系，共同决定了模拟的变形行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解钛的形变行为既关乎工业应用的技术进步，也是从基础层面掌握相关合金力学性能的关键。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟，变化系统尺寸（跨越四个数量级，最大达3200万原子）和应变速率（低至10^8 s^-1），研究α-钛晶体模型在压缩下的力学响应。

Result: 弹性性质不依赖系统尺寸与应变速率；塑性变形阶段出现明显尺寸效应——增大系统尺寸可降低应力波动、使结构演化更均匀、并稳定位错（dislocation）活动；降低应变速率需要更大的系统尺寸才能实现平衡与结构稳定。

Conclusion: 系统尺寸与应变速率之间存在强耦合效应，二者共同决定了压缩晶体材料的模拟变形行为。

Abstract: Understanding the deformation behaviour of titanium is important not only for technological advances associated with industrially-relevant applications, but also essential to achieve a fundamental understanding of the mechanical properties of the relevant alloys. In this computational study, molecular-dynamics simulations are employed to ascertain the impact of model size on the mechanical response of alpha-titanium under compression. The deformation behaviour of the crystalline models is investigated as a function of different system sizes (varied by four orders of magnitude, up to 32 million atoms), and strain rates (down to 10^8 s^-1). The results show that the elastic properties remain independent of both system size and strain rate, whereas marked size effects emerge during plastic deformation. Increasing the system size of the titanium model reduces stress fluctuations, results in more homogeneous structural evolution, and stabilizes dislocation activity. Decreasing the applied strain rate requires correspondingly a larger system size to achieve equilibration and to ensure a stable behaviour for the simulated structure. The modelling results demonstrate that system size and strain rate are strongly coupled, and their combined effect governs the simulated deformation behaviour of the compressed crystalline material.

### [26] [Moiré Phonons and Emergent Exciton-Phonon Coupling in a Moiré Heterobilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28185)
*Can B. Uzundal,Woochang Kim,Zhiyuan Cui,Yuxuan Wei,Zheyu Lu,Qixin Feng,Francis L. Hong,Indrajit Maity,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Manish Jain,Mit H. Naik,Yoseob Yoon,Michael F. Crommie,Steven G. Louie,Feng Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在WS2/WSe2异质双层中实验发现了莫尔声子与莫尔激子之间具有层选择性的新颖耦合，并通过太赫兹声子换能器、驱动振子模型和第一性原理计算揭示了三种莫尔声子共振及其耦合机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）已成为调控范德华异质结构中电子和光学性质的新平台，但其对激子-声子耦合（exciton-phonon coupling）的影响仍 largely unexplored，因此本文旨在探索这一未解决的关键问题。

Method: 采用宽带太赫兹声子换能器（broadband terahertz phonon transducer）相干激发莫尔声子（moiré phonons），通过其共振扰动激子态来探测耦合；结合驱动振子模型（driven oscillator model）提取动力学参数，并辅以第一性原理计算（first principles calculations）进行理论验证。

Result: 实验观察到莫尔超晶格以层选择性（layer-selective manner）内在修饰了激子-声子耦合；驱动振子模型揭示了三种莫尔声子共振，它们与莫尔激子具有不同的耦合特征；第一性原理计算表明莫尔原胞中存在多种具有强杂化面内和面外振动的莫尔声子模式，并识别出实验中观测到的三种莫尔声子及其特征耦合。

Conclusion: 研究证明了莫尔超晶格能层选择性地调控激子-声子耦合，为理解莫尔体系中声子与激子的相互作用提供了新机制，并为基于莫尔超晶格的光电和声子工程开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Moiré superlattices have emerged as a new platform for engineering electronic and optical properties in van der Waals heterostructures, enabling control over correlated and excitonic phenomena. Yet the impact of moiré superlattices on exciton-phonon coupling remains largely unexplored. Here we demonstrate emergent, layer-selective coupling between moiré phonons and moiré excitons in angle-aligned WS2/WSe2 heterobilayers. Using a broadband terahertz phonon transducer, we coherently launch moiré phonons that resonantly perturb the excitonic states. We show that the exciton-phonon coupling is intrinsically modified by the moiré superlattice in a layer-selective manner. A driven oscillator model captures the dynamics, revealing three moiré phonon resonances with distinct coupling to the moiré excitons. First principles calculations show that many moiré phonon modes can arise with distinct strongly hybridized in-plane and out-of-plane vibrations in the moiré unit cells. The calculations further identify the three experimentally observed moiré phonons and their emergent characteristic coupling to the moiré excitons.

### [27] [Observing Massive Scattering from Null Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27421)
*Walker Melton,Kyrill Michaelsen,Romain Ruzziconi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过软引力子辐射研究了大质量散射振幅信息如何被传递到零无穷远（null infinity）的晚期极限，发现Bondi质量面（Bondi mass aspect）可作为大质量出射辐射的探测器算符，并建立了Bondi质量面的关联函数与散射截面的加权和之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有平直时空全息方案（如天球全息（celestial holography）或卡罗尔全息（Carrollian holography））难以描述含大质量外态的散射过程，因为大质量粒子渐近于类时无穷远（timelike infinity）而非零无穷远。本研究旨在通过软引力子辐射，探索大质量散射振幅信息如何在零无穷远晚期极限被携带，以弥补上述局限。

Method: 采用类时无穷远与零无穷远边界之间的连续性条件，论证Bondi质量面在$\mathscr{I}^+_+$上的晚期极限可作为大质量出射辐射的探测器算符；进一步将Bondi质量面的in-in关联函数与散射截面的加权和建立联系；最后将Bondi质量面解释为卡罗尔应力张量（Carrollian stress-tensor）分量，并利用Ward恒等式（Ward identities）约束其二点关联函数。

Result: 建立了Bondi质量面在零无穷远晚期极限处与大质量散射过程信息之间的联系：它天然充当大质量出射辐射的探测器算符，且其in-in关联函数可表示为散射截面的加权和。

Conclusion: 研究表明，零无穷远处（$\mathscr{I}$）的观测者可在晚期时间提取关于大质量散射过程的信息，这为将大质量态纳入平直时空全息框架提供了新的理论路径。

Abstract: Because massive particles asymptote to timelike rather than null infinity, current flat space holographic proposals such as celestial or Carrollian holography struggle to describe scattering processes with massive external states. We take a step toward addressing this limitation by studying how information about massive scattering amplitudes is carried to the late-time limit of null infinity by soft graviton radiation. We show that continuity between the boundaries of timelike and null infinity implies that the late-time limit of the Bondi mass aspect naturally acts as a detector operator for massive outgoing radiation. We further relate in-in correlation functions of the Bondi mass aspect at $\mathscr{I}^+_+$ to weighted sums of scattering cross sections, implying that an observer at $\mathscr{I}$ can extract information about massive scattering processes at late times. Finally, we interpret the Bondi mass aspect as a Carrollian stress-tensor component, and study Ward identities to constrain its two-point functions.

</details>

Method: 针对Fermat型多项式，证明以自由场表达的Calabi–Yau顶点算子（vertex operators）对应于$\mathcal{N}{=}2$最小模型（minimal models）的初级场（primary fields）之积；利用该对应关系验证自由场构造的模不变性，并将其推广至Berglund–Hübsch型Calabi–Yau轨形，导出完整顶点算子需满足的条件。

Result: 成功建立了自由场构造与最小模型构造之间的对应关系；验证了自由场构造的模不变性；将该构造扩展至Berglund–Hübsch型Calabi–Yau轨形，并得到与最小模型构造平行的顶点算子条件。

Conclusion: 自由场构造与最小模型构造在Calabi–Yau紧致化中具有一致性，且自由场构造可自然推广至轨形情形，为进一步研究杂化弦论的模性质提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We establish a correspondence between the free-field construction and the minimal-model construction of the Calabi--Yau sector of the four-dimensional heterotic string compactified on Berglund--Hübsch type Calabi--Yau manifolds and their orbifolds. For Fermat-type polynomials the Calabi--Yau vertex operators expressed in terms of free fields are shown to correspond to products of primary fields of $\mathcal{N}{=}2$ minimal models. Using this correspondence we verify modular invariance of the free-field construction and extend it to Berglund--Hübsch Calabi--Yau orbifolds, deriving the conditions on complete vertex operators that parallel those of the minimal-model construction.

### [29] [Soft QED as Open Quantum System: Infrared Cancellation and Soft-Shell Coarse Graining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27498)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将量子电动力学（QED）中未解析的软光子扇区形式化为开放量子系统（open quantum system），通过约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）描述系统与环境（未解析软光子）的纠缠，并展示该框架在红外有限性、软光子定理及林德布拉德演化（Lindblad evolution）等方面与完整QED的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准QED中软光子的红外发散（infrared divergence）问题在概率计算中尚缺乏统一的开放量子系统框架。作者旨在通过将未解析的软光子视为环境，提出一种新的形式化方法，以系统地处理实虚软光子项的求和与红外有限性，并建立与Lindblad演化的联系。

Method: 将已解析的带电粒子和硬光子定义为系统，未解析的软光子定义为环境，基于约化密度矩阵构建开放量子系统描述。利用施温格-凯尔迪什（Schwinger-Keldysh, SK）形式将未解析的虚项与实项纳入双轮廓展开（doubled-contour expansion）。通过Kraus算符（Kraus operators）和影响泛函（influence functional）的等历史恒等式（equal-history identity）实现软光子演化的幺正规范化，并推导出尺度参数化的Lindblad演化。

Result: 在单圈层次上，虚软光子与实软光子携带具有相反符号的相同在壳Eikonal核（on-shell eikonal kernel）。开放量子系统框架与完整QED在相同可观测量、微扰阶、费曼图和相空间下给出相同的红外有限项。软光子演化是由散射流（scattering current）驱动的幺正相干态位移（unitary coherent-state displacement）。含尺度参数的Lindblad演化在固定硬支空间（fixed hard-branch space）上实现，其有限壳映射为完全正幺正舒尔通道（completely positive unital Schur channel），在尖锐尺度不变的leading-soft区为全正可分的退相半群（dephasing semigroup）。

Conclusion: 该开放量子系统框架优雅地组织了QED概率计算，自动实现了红外有限性。所得到的对数可见度斜率（logarithmic visibility slope）和单调纯度损失（monotonic purity loss）是约化态描述的非对角预测。相同的受控位移膨胀（controlled-displacement dilation）还给出了Sudakov概率、泊松软光子多重数（Poisson soft-photon multiplicities）及轫致辐射数谱（bremsstrahlung number spectrum）。

Abstract: I formulate unresolved soft-photon sector of QED as open quantum system. Resolved charged particles and hard photons form the system, unresolved soft photons form the environment, and basic object is the reduced density matrix. A resolved outcome $f$ of multiple hard particles and photons has probability $P_{f}(i) =\sum_n|\langle f,n|S|i,0\rangle|^2=\langle i|F_f|i\rangle$, with Kraus operators $K_n= {}_{\rm soft} \langle n|S|0 \rangle_{\rm soft}$ and effect $F_f=\sum_nK_n^\daggerΠ_fK_n$. The SK formulation places unresolved virtual and real terms in one doubled-contour expansion. At one loop they carry the same on-shell eikonal kernel with opposite signs. This elegantly organizes the QED probability: for the same observable, perturbative order, diagrams, and phase space, the OQS gives the same infrared-finite terms as the full-QED. The soft-photon evolution is a unitary coherent-state displacement driven by the scattering current. The equal-history identity of influence functional exactly normalizes this soft evolution; together with the soft-photon theorem it removes the IR divergent leading-soft factor from inclusive probability. I also derive explicit leading-soft QED realization of scale-parametrized Lindblad evolution on a fixed hard-branch space. Tracing an infinitesimal soft-photon shell produces diagonal jump operators whose entries are fixed by the corresponding eikonal emission amplitudes. The finite-shell map is a completely positive unital Schur channel and, in the sharp scale-invariant leading-soft regime, a dephasing semigroup of a completely-positive-divisible scale flow. The resulting logarithmic visibility slope and monotonic purity loss are off-diagonal predictions of the reduced-state description. The same controlled-displacement dilation gives the Sudakov probability, Poisson soft-photon multiplicities, and the bremsstrahlung number spectrum.

</details>


### [30] [Gravitational wave scattering at $\mathcal{O}(G^4)$: Murua construction and elliptics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27544)
*Yilber Fabian Bautista,Mathias Driesse,Kays Haddad,Gustav Uhre Jakobsen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用世界线量子场论（worldline quantum field theory）形式，计算了引力波与无自旋点粒子在牛顿常数四阶（$\mathcal{O}(G^4)$）上的散射振幅。通过引入含Murua系数的主积分分解，避免了振幅向Magnusian转换所需的切割减法（cut subtraction），并将结果与黑洞微扰理论匹配，证明点粒子世界线量子场论能准确描述史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black holes）至$\mathcal{O}(G^4)$。此外，在该阶次下，动量空间中首次出现了椭圆函数（elliptic functions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在精确计算引力波与点粒子在牛顿常数四阶上的散射振幅，并验证点粒子世界线量子场论能否准确描述史瓦西黑洞的散射行为。

Method: 采用世界线量子场论（worldline quantum field theory）形式进行计算；利用含Murua系数的主积分分解，绕过传统方法中所需的切割减法（cut subtraction），将散射振幅直接转换为Magnusian，进而映射到分波空间（partial wave space）中的散射相移（scattering phase shift）。

Result: 计算得到$\mathcal{O}(G^4)$阶的散射振幅，并与黑洞微扰理论（black hole perturbation theory）的预测相匹配，证明点粒子世界线量子场论能准确描述史瓦西黑洞至该阶次；在该阶次下，动量空间首次出现椭圆函数（elliptic functions）。

Conclusion: 点粒子世界线量子场论在$\mathcal{O}(G^4)$阶上能够准确描述史瓦西黑洞的引力波散射特性；文中发展的含Murua系数的积分分解方法有效简化了计算流程。

Abstract: We compute the amplitude for the scattering of a gravitational wave off of a spinless point particle at fourth order in Newton's constant, using the worldline quantum field theory formalism. A decomposition of our master integrals incorporating Murua coefficients allows us to entirely bypass the cut subtraction needed to convert the scattering amplitude into the Magnusian, the latter being desirable as it maps directly onto the scattering phase shift in partial wave space. This is then matched to the prediction from black hole perturbation theory, proving that point-particle worldline quantum field theory accurately describes Schwarzschild black holes up to $\mathcal{O}(G^4)$. Elliptic functions appear in momentum space for the first time for this process at this order.

### [31] [CIPro Package: Complete Intersections in Products of Projective Spaces and Line Bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27588)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: CIPro 是一个 Mathematica 软件包，用于构建和分析乘积射影空间中的完全交集及其上的线丛，能够计算陈类（Chern classes）、Hilbert 级数（Hilbert series）、GV 不变量（GV invariants）和对称性（symmetries）等几何性质，以及线丛的上同调群（cohomology groups），并整合了文献中的完全交集 Calabi-Yau 三/四重态数据集。该工具主要服务于弦论紧致化（string compactifications）中的几何计算，尤其适用于 Heterotic 和 Type II 构造中的 Calabi-Yau 几何，部分功能亦可推广至 F-理论中的几乎 Fano 基（almost Fano bases）等非 Calabi-Yau 情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为弦论紧致化中日益复杂的完全交集（complete intersections）几何计算需求提供统一的软件工具，并将分散在文献中的相关数据集整合到单一系统中，以降低重复计算成本并提升可重复性。

Method: 基于 Mathematica 环境开发软件包 CIPro，实现完全交集及其上线丛多种几何与拓扑性质的自动化计算，并集成文献中已有的完全交集 Calabi-Yau 三/四重态数据集。

Result: 该包可计算完全交集的陈类、Hilbert 级数、GV 不变量和对称性，以及线丛的上同调群；整合了文献中已有的完全交集 Calabi-Yau 三/四重态数据集。

Conclusion: CIPro 为弦论紧致化中的几何计算提供了实用工具，尤其适用于 Heterotic 和 Type II 构造中的 Calabi-Yau 几何，其部分功能也适用于 F-理论中的几乎 Fano 基等非 Calabi-Yau 情形。

Abstract: CIPro is a Mathematica package for constructing and analyzing complete intersections in products of projective spaces and line bundles over such varieties. It computes properties of complete intersections, such as Chern classes, Hilbert series, GV invariants and symmetries, as well as properties of line bundles on complete intersections, including their cohomology groups. The package also consolidates a number of data sets available in the literature into a single system, including the lists of complete intersection Calabi-Yau three- and four-folds. This short tutorial introduces the package, provides a brief discussion of some of the mathematical background underlying its computations, and gives a series of examples to illustrate its use. These tools are of utility for many computations in string compactifications, especially for Calabi-Yau geometries appearing in Heterotic and Type II constructions. Many tools apply beyond the Calabi-Yau context, including for example, almost Fano bases in F-theory.

### [32] [Classification of Killing Horizons in D=11 Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27843)
*Jan Gutowski,Chettha Saelim,Martin Wolf*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在十一维超引力（11D supergravity）中，对具有闭合空间截面的超对称退化 Killing 视界（supersymmetric degenerate Killing horizons）进行分类，证明此类解可分为两类，并分别揭示了它们的几何结构与超对称性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超引力理论中，Killing 视界是理解黑洞解与超对称性之间关系的重要结构。此前研究多集中于近视界极限（near-horizon limit），本文旨在脱离该极限，对十一维超引力中超对称退化 Killing 视界进行系统分类。

Method: 通过引入 Gaussian 零坐标系（Gaussian null coordinate system），根据 Killing 旋量（Killing spinor）在视界上的光锥手性（lightcone chirality）将解划分为两类：第一类中负光锥手性分量非零，第二类中该分量为零。随后对两类解分别进行等距等价性和旋量 Lie 导数的分析。

Result: 第一类解与超对称近视界几何（supersymmetric near-horizon geometries）等距等价。第二类解中，生成视界的 Killing 向量对应的旋量 Lie 导数（spinorial Lie derivative）为零；且当超对称数目大于 13 时，该类解退化为 pp-波（pp-waves）。

Conclusion: 超对称退化 Killing 视界在十一维超引力中仅存在两类截然不同的结构，其分类完全由视界上 Killing 旋量的光锥手性决定。

Abstract: We initiate the classification of supersymmetric degenerate Killing horizons, with closed spatial cross section, away from the near-horizon limit in D=11 supergravity. We prove that all such solutions fall into two distinct classes, depending on lightcone chirality with respect to a Gaussian null coordinate system. For the first class of solutions, the negative lightcone chirality part of the Killing spinor is non-zero on the Killing horizon, and we prove that all such solutions are isometric to supersymmetric near-horizon geometries. In the second class, the negative lightcone chirality part of the Killing spinor vanishes on the Killing horizon. In this case, we prove that the spinorial Lie derivative of the Killing spinor with respect to the Killing vector which generates the Killing horizon vanishes, and that all such solutions with more than 13 supersymmetries are pp-waves.

TL;DR: 本文研究了超对称λ-变形下的AdS₃×S³×T⁴超弦理论，计算了光锥规范下的玻色子树级世界sheet S矩阵。研究发现，当0≤λ<1时，由于非弹性散射过程的非平凡抵消，世界sheet散射与可积性（integrability）兼容；而当λ→1时，S矩阵变得病态，表明该极限未能完全捕捉T-对偶理论的世界sheet动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超对称λ-变形下AdS₃×S³×T⁴超弦理论的可积性（integrability）性质，并检验λ→1极限是否能够完整描述非阿贝尔T-对偶（non-Abelian T-dual）几何的世界sheet动力学。

Method: 采用光锥规范（light-cone gauge），对超对称λ-变形的AdS₃×S³×T⁴超弦理论进行微扰计算，得到玻色子树级世界sheet S矩阵，并分析散射过程的弹性与非弹性特征。

Result: 在0≤λ<1的通用参数范围内，非弹性散射过程发生非平凡抵消，使世界sheet散射与可积性兼容；当λ→1时，S矩阵失去良好定义，尽管该极限在解析延拓意义下可复现非阿贝尔T-对偶几何。

Conclusion: λ→1极限并不能完全捕捉T-对偶理论的世界sheet动力学，暗示该极限在描述完整动力学时存在局限性。

Abstract: We consider the supersymmetric $λ$-deformation of $\text{AdS}_3 \times \text{S}^3 \times \text{T}^4$ superstrings and compute its perturbative bosonic tree-level worldsheet S matrix in the light-cone gauge. For generic values of $0 \leq λ< 1$, we show that the worldsheet scattering remains compatible with integrability due to a non-trivial cancellation of non-elastic scattering processes. By contrast, the S matrix becomes ill-defined for $λ\to 1$, despite the fact that this limit reproduces the non-Abelian T-dual geometry up to an analytic continuation. This suggests that the $λ\to 1$ limit does not capture the full worldsheet dynamics of the T-dual theory.

### [34] [A UV-Finite Ryu-Takayanagi Relation from Relative Entropy in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27915)
*Albert Much,Philipp Dorau,Leonardo Sangaletti,Rainer Verch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在AdS₃/CFT₂对偶中，以相对熵（relative entropy）替代发散的冯·诺依曼纠缠熵，建立了一个紫外有限的Ryu-Takayanagi关系。通过将手征相对熵的精确结果适配到菱形区域，边界相对熵被表达为Schwarzian泛函，进而通过Fefferman-Graham字典与Bañados几何的渐近数据对应；三维引力的刚性将这一边界对应推广至体时空。在线性微扰下，相对熵等于RT测地线长度变化除以4G_N。该构造仅依赖于Bisognano-Wichmann/Borchers定理和全息字典，为RT关系提供了算子代数层面的紫外有限对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的Ryu-Takayanagi公式依赖于紫外发散的冯·诺依曼纠缠熵，在量子场论中需要正规化。本文旨在利用相对熵这一紫外有限（UV-finite）的量，在AdS₃/CFT₂中重新建立RT关系，从而提供一个算子代数（operator-algebraic）意义上更干净的理论框架。

Method: 作者将Hollands关于手征相对熵（chiral relative entropy）的精确结果适配到菱形区域（diamond region），将边界真空与相干态之间的相对熵表达为Schwarzian泛函。利用Fefferman-Graham字典将该泛函与Bañados几何的渐近数据对应，并借助三维引力的刚性将这一边界对应唯一地延拓至整个体时空。最后，在线性微扰下计算相对熵与RT测地线长度变化之间的关系。

Result: 在线性微扰（linear order in the metric perturbation）下，边界相对熵等于体时空RT测地线长度变化除以4G_N，即δS_rel = δL_RT / (4G_N)。该结果不依赖于紫外截断，且完全基于Bisognano-Wichmann/Borchers定理与全息字典。

Conclusion: 本文在AdS₃/CFT₂对偶中建立了相对熵版本的Ryu-Takayanagi关系，为全息纠缠熵提供了一种紫外有限、算子代数化的对应物。该构造不依赖纠缠熵的正规化，展示了相对熵作为全息对偶中更基本物理量的潜力。

Abstract: We establish a Ryu-Takayanagi (RT) relation in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ using \emph{relative entropy} as the central object, in place of the ultraviolet-divergent von Neumann entanglement entropy. Adapting Hollands' exact result for the chiral relative entropy to a diamond region, we express the boundary relative entropy between the vacuum and a coherent state as a Schwarzian functional, which the Fefferman-Graham dictionary identifies with the asymptotic data of a Bañados geometry; the rigidity of three-dimensional gravity promotes this boundary identification to the bulk. To linear order in the metric perturbation, the relative entropy then equals the variation of the RT geodesic length divided by $4G_N$. The construction rests only on the Bisognano-Wichmann/Borchers theorem and the holographic dictionary, giving a UV-finite, operator-algebraic counterpart to the RT relation.

### [35] [The two-dimensional disordered $O(N)$ sigma model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27925)
*Martí Berenguer,Felix M. Haehl,Elisa Tabor*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个二维 O(N) 非线性 sigma 模型，其中包含随机高斯 p-体相互作用。该模型结合了二维玻色子 SYK 型量子场论的结构与非线性 sigma 模型的稳定球面约束。在大 N 极限下，推导了环面上的 Schwinger-Dyson 方程，并通过解析近似和数值方法分析了其解。结果发现其相图与一维量子球面 p-自旋模型定性相似，包括低温下向自旋玻璃相的转变，该相由有限的爱德华-安德森序参量（Edwards-Anderson order parameter）表征，且两点函数的动力学部分呈现近似标度（scaling）行为。这些结果为研究无序二维相对论性场论中的近似共形行为（conformal behavior）和玻璃态物理（glassy physics）提供了一个可操作的分析框架。

Result: 获得的相图在定性上与一维量子球面 p-自旋模型的相图相似：低温下体系进入自旋玻璃相（spin glass phase），该相由有限的爱德华-安德森序参量（Edwards-Anderson order parameter）刻画；同时，两点函数中的动力学部分展现出近似的标度（scaling）行为。

Conclusion: 该模型为研究带有无序的二维相对论性场论中的近似共形行为（approximate conformal behavior）和玻璃态物理（glassy physics）提供了一个可操作的理论环境，具有普适性和可扩展性。未来有望借助该模型进一步探索无序系统中维度与共形对称性破缺之间的相互作用。

Abstract: We introduce a two-dimensional $O(N)$ nonlinear sigma model with random Gaussian $p$-body interactions. The model combines the structure of a two-dimensional bosonic SYK-type quantum field theory with the stabilizing spherical constraint of the nonlinear sigma model. At large $N$ we derive the Schwinger-Dyson equations on a torus and analyze the solutions using both analytical approximations and numerical methods. We find a phase diagram qualitatively similar to that of the one-dimensional quantum spherical $p$-spin model, including a low-temperature transition to a spin glass phase. This phase is characterized by a finite Edwards-Anderson order parameter, while the dynamical part of the two-point function displays an approximate scaling regime. These results provide a tractable setting for studying approximate conformal behavior and glassy physics in a two-dimensional relativistic field theory with disorder.

### [36] [$\texttt{SMaSH}$ : Simplify Massive Spinor Helicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27928)
*Aakash Kumar,Arnab Rudra,Rahul Shaw*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 SMaSH，一个基于 Mathematica 的软件包，用于在四维时空（four spacetime dimensions）中执行旋量螺旋度（spinor helicity）计算。该软件包支持有质量旋量螺旋度计算、无质量和离壳变量处理，并集成了预设振幅与传播子、高能极限实现、离散 C/P/T 变换检测、接触项计算及规范不变性（gauge invariance）检查等功能，还可通过 RAMBO 算法生成 n 点散射的数值运动学。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在 Mathematica 环境下实现旋量螺旋度形式体系（spinor helicity formalism），包含：有质量/无质量/离壳旋量螺旋度变量；基于 arXiv:1709.04891 的预设三点振幅与传播子；高能极限（high energy limit）约化；离散 C、P、T 变换检查；接触项（contact term）计算与规范不变性强制施加功能；以及利用 RAMBO 算法为任意 n 点散射生成实数和复数数值运动学（numerical kinematics）。

Result: 软件包支持 Weinberg 最小振幅（Weinberg minimal amplitudes）的计算，并具备 Schouten 化简、Clifford 代数操作、旋量螺旋度与洛伦兹矢量（Lorentz vector）互转、旋量标量微分及螺旋度缩放（helicity scaling）等基础操作。

Conclusion: SMaSH 是一个全面的旋量螺旋度计算工具，填补了有质量粒子显式小群指标处理方面的空白，并为高能物理散射幅（scattering amplitude）的微扰计算（perturbative computation）提供了自动化的数值与符号操作环境。

Abstract: We present $\texttt{SMaSH}$, a $\texttt{Mathematica}$ package to do spinor helicity computations in four spacetime dimensions $\href{https://github.com/aakash-kmr/SMaSH}{\text{(github)}}$. It can handle massive spinor helicity computations with explicit little group indices which is a novel feature. It can also handle massless as well as off-shell spinor helicity variables. It is designed to compute perturbative computations; it comes with predefined three point amplitudes and propagators for any masses and spins (arXiv:1709.04891). It can implement the high energy limit over an expression, check the discrete $\tt{C,P,T}$ transformations, compute contact terms and impose gauge invariance for any scattering process. We have shown the usage of such functions for computing gauge invariant Weinberg minimal amplitudes (arXiv:2506:12431, arXiv:2504:06343).
  The package can also generate both real and complex numerical kinematics for any $n$-point scattering for arbitrary masses and energy scales by implementing the $\tt{RAMBO}$ algorithm. It is also rich with basic spinor helicity manipulations like Schouten simplification, Clifford algebra manipulation, conversion between spinor helicity and Lorentz vectors, derivative w.r.t. spinors and their scalars, helicity scaling etc.

</details>


### [37] [Quantum black hole cohomologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27955)
*Seok Kim,Seongmin Kim,Siyul Lee,Jiyoo Park*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过研究SU(2)理论中BPS AdS黑洞微态的经典上同调（cohomologies）在1-loop修正下的提升（lift）现象，发现最轻的意外上同调（fortuitous cohomology）及其“毛状”（hairy）版本未被提升，而许多更重的“核心”（core）意外上同调被提升，并论证经典上同调在Cardy极限下的熵比严格保护态的指标熵（indicial entropy）至少大约1.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BPS AdS黑洞的量子性质（quantum natures）一直停留在猜想层面，近期在SO(7)理论中发现经典黑洞意外上同调会被1-loop修正提升，本研究旨在检验这一提升现象是否普遍存在于SU(2)理论中，并量化其熵效应。

Method: 论文以最大超杨-米尔斯理论（maximal super-Yang-Mills theories）的经典上同调为出发点，在SU(2)理论框架下系统分析不同意外上同调在1-loop修正下的提升行为，将对象区分为“毛状”版本与“核心”版本进行分类考察。

Result: 在SU(2)理论中，最轻的意外上同调及其“毛状”版本未被1-loop修正提升，而许多更重的“核心”意外上同调确实被提升；经典上同调在Cardy极限下的熵比严格保护态的指标熵至少高出约1.2%。

Conclusion: 提升现象在SU(2)理论中同样存在，但并非所有经典上同调都被修正，轻量级与毛状版本保持不受提升，而核心较重版本则被修正；经典上同调的系统熵贡献在渐近极限下具有可量化的超额。

Abstract: Microstates of BPS AdS black holes have been studied from the classical cohomologies of the maximal super-Yang-Mills theories, but their quantum natures have been conjectural. It was recently found that a classical black hole (fortuitous) cohomology in the $SO(7)$ theory is lifted by 1-loop corrections. We show that such lifts also happen in the $SU(2)$ theory, presenting both lifted/unlifted examples. In particular, the lightest fortuitous cohomology and its `hairy' versions are unlifted, while many heavier `core' fortuitous ones are lifted. We argue that the entropy of classical cohomologies in the Cardy limit is larger than the indicial entropy of strictly protected states by at least $\approx 1.2 \%$.

### [38] [Planar loop integrands from cuts in $D$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28052)
*Fan Zhu,Song He,Zhenqi Han*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在任意有色理论中，从D维广义幺正割（generalized unitarity cuts）直接重构平面圈被积函数（planar loop integrands）的公式，通过Möbius逆变换（Möbius-inversion formula）将组合学与树级振幅（tree amplitudes）分离，并给出了纯杨-米尔斯理论（pure Yang–Mills theory）及最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论（maximally supersymmetric Yang–Mills theory）中的闭式结果与数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有圈被积函数重构方法依赖特定理论的树级输入，组合结构与动力学信息耦合紧密。本文旨在将这两者系统性地分离，建立一种仅依赖于D维广义幺正割的通用重构框架，适用于任意有色理论。

Method: 方法核心是将L圈n点色序振幅的被积函数表示为所有可容许无量纲标量图（admissible non-scaleless scalar graphs）的求和，每项由对应的D维割（cut）贡献；系数由细化偏序集（refinement poset）上的通用Möbius逆变换公式（或等价地，关联复形的欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）减一）给出。计算所需割由拼接D维树级振幅并对内部胶子态求和生成。

Result: 在纯杨-米尔斯理论中给出了圈被积函数的闭式公式；在两圈五点（two-loop five-point）情形下与已知被积函数数据及积分-约化（integration-by-parts reduction）后的螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）一致；进一步生成了两圈六点（two-loop six-point）和三圈四点（three-loop four-point）的紧凑割组织化数据；在最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论中，气泡（bubble）和三角（triangle）子图的缺失显著简化了相关割偏序集。

Conclusion: 所提框架成功将圈被积函数的组合结构与动力学贡献解耦，并通过多个非平凡算例（包括两圈五点、两圈六点、三圈四点）验证了方法的正确性与可扩展性。

Abstract: We present a direct reconstruction formula for planar loop integrands from $D$-dimensional generalized unitarity cuts in any colored theory. The reconstruction combinatorics is separated from the theory-dependent tree amplitudes entering the cuts: for the $L$-loop $n$-point color-ordered amplitude, the integrand is expressed as a sum over admissible non-scaleless scalar graphs dressed by corresponding cuts in $D$ dimensions; the coefficients are given by the universal Möbius-inversion formula of the refinement poset, or equivalently one minus the Euler characteristics of associated complexes.
  As an application we write down closed-formulas for loop integrands in pure Yang--Mills theory, where the required cuts are generated by gluing $D$-dimensional tree amplitudes and summing over internal gluon states. We also use the two-loop five-point case as a validation, comparing with known integrand data and after integration-by-parts reduction, with known integrated helicity amplitudes. The same framework also produces compact cut-organized data for larger examples, including the two-loop six-point and three-loop four-point cases. We also describe the corresponding simplification in maximally supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory, where the absence of bubble and triangle subgraphs reduces the relevant cut poset substantially.

Abstract: We construct simple analytical solutions of the RG equations for the running couplings α_s and y_{top} in the asymptotic regime. These solutions have an explicit form, contain only logarithms and no special functions, and subsequently sum up the leading, subleading, etc logarithms in all orders of PT. While the effect of y_{top} on the running of α_s happens to be negligible, the role of α_s on the running of y_{top} is essential, the account of higher orders gives a noticeable contribution.

*Juno Kwon,Rak-Kyeong Seong*

Method: 对于父代膜砖模型对应的环面 Calabi-Yau 4 维流形 M，分析阿贝尔轨形群 Gamma 在 M 生成元上的作用如何诱导出手征场（chiral fields）、费米场（Fermi fields）以及 J-项和 E-项上的作用；通过要求轨形化后的模型与 J-和 E-项关联的闭合路径及它们乘积形成的手征环（chiral cycles）保持一致，导出轨形作用的 Calabi-Yau 条件，并得到轨形化后 J-和 E-项的显式公式。

Result: 成功将构造应用于 Q^{1,1,1} 和 D_3 对应的膜砖模型，得到了相应的 2d (0,2) 箭图规范理论（quiver gauge theories）族，并给出了计数不同阿贝尔轨形的生成函数显式表达式。
