Abstract: We present a systematic procedure for constructing brane brick models corresponding to abelian orbifolds of toric Calabi-Yau 4-folds, extending the orbifold construction beyond the well-studied case of abelian orbifolds of C^4. Given a parent brane brick model corresponding to a toric Calabi-Yau 4-fold M, we show that the action of an abelian orbifold group Gamma on the generators of M induces an action on the chiral and Fermi fields as well as the J- and E-terms of the associated 2d (0,2) supersymmetric gauge theory. The requirement that the orbifolded brane brick model remains consistent with the closed paths associated with the J- and E-terms, together with the chiral cycles formed by their products, precisely reproduces the Calabi-Yau condition on the orbifold action. This procedure yields an explicit formula for the J- and E-terms of the orbifolded brane brick model in terms of those of the parent theory. We apply our construction to the brane brick models corresponding to Q^{1,1,1} and D_3, and present the resulting families of 2d (0,2) quiver gauge theories. ### [41] [Configurational Temperature in Matrix Models and Random Matrix Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28148)
*Anosh Joseph,Vinod Mamale*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了相互作用矩阵模型和高斯随机矩阵系综中的组态温度估计量（configurational temperature estimator），该估计量源自精确的Schwinger-Dyson恒等式，并通过作用量的梯度和Hessian矩阵表达。在Gross-Witten-Wadia模型、四势阱双阱矩阵模型以及高斯正交、酉和辛系综中，该估计量均在统计误差内满足β_config=1。通过将估计量分解为各向同性和各向异性部分，发现有限N修正满足β_iso−1≃−β_aniso的近似关系，并展示了该估计量作为蒙特卡洛模拟灵敏诊断手段的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索组态温度估计量在相互作用矩阵模型和高斯随机矩阵系综中的行为，并验证其满足精确Schwinger-Dyson恒等式的程度，同时挖掘该估计量在数值模拟中的诊断价值。

Method: 基于精确Schwinger-Dyson恒等式推导出组态温度估计量，并将其表达为作用量的梯度（gradient）和Hessian矩阵的形式。将该估计量分解为各向同性部分（isotropic part）和各向异性部分（anisotropic part），分别分析有限N修正。

Result: 在Gross-Witten-Wadia模型、四势阱双阱矩阵模型以及高斯正交系综（GOE）、酉系综（GUE）和辛系综（GSE）中，组态温度估计量均在统计不确定度内满足β_config=1。各向同性部分与各向异性部分的有限N修正满足近似关系β_iso−1≃−β_aniso。

Conclusion: 组态温度估计量在多种矩阵模型中精确满足Schwinger-Dyson恒等式，其分解后的各向同性与各向异性部分揭示了有限N修正的互补结构。该估计量可作为蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）中一种灵敏的诊断工具。

Abstract: We investigate the configurational temperature estimator in interacting matrix models and Gaussian random-matrix ensembles. The estimator follows from an exact Schwinger--Dyson identity and may be expressed in terms of the gradient and Hessian of the action. We study the Gross--Witten--Wadia model, a quartic double-well matrix model, and the Gaussian Orthogonal, Unitary, and Symplectic Ensembles. In all cases, the estimator satisfies the exact Schwinger--Dyson identity, $β_{\rm config} = 1$, within statistical uncertainties. Separating the estimator into isotropic and anisotropic parts, we find that the leading finite-$N$ corrections satisfy the approximate relation $β_{\rm iso} - 1 \simeq - β_{\rm aniso}$. We also show that the configurational temperature estimator provides a sensitive diagnostic of Monte Carlo simulations.

### [42] [Large Quantum Gravity Fluctuations of BTZ Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28160)
*Ben Freivogel,Upamanyu Moitra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在三维反德西特时空（AdS3）中，通过明确定义的协议计算黑洞视界的量子涨落，定义了视界的“量子宽度”，并通过全息对偶将其与边界关联函数联系起来。在微扰量子引力框架下，发现该量子宽度典型量级为 $(G_\mathrm{N} L_{\mathrm{AdS}}^3)^{1/4}$，参量上远大于普朗克尺度，且在紫外区对数发散。该结果为微扰量子引力中规范不变的涨落远大于普朗克尺度提供了迄今最严格的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞视界的量子涨落，旨在理解量子引力效应在视界尺度上的表现，并检验视界涨落是否可能远大于普朗克尺度这一非平凡问题。

Method: 定义了一个精确的协议来计算视界涨落，并定义了相应的“量子宽度”；利用全息对偶（holography）将视界涨落与边界关联函数（boundary correlation functions）联系起来；在微扰量子引力（perturbative quantum gravity）框架下进行计算。

Result: 量子宽度的典型量级为 $(G_\mathrm{N} L_{\mathrm{AdS}}^3)^{1/4}$，参量上远大于普朗克尺度；该宽度依赖于测量尺度，在紫外（UV）区域呈对数发散。

Conclusion: 研究结果为微扰量子引力中视界存在规范不变且远大于普朗克尺度的量子涨落提供了迄今最严格的证据。

Abstract: We study the quantum fluctuations of the black hole horizon in three-dimensional Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime. We define a precise protocol to calculate the horizon fluctuations and define a corresponding ``quantum width'' of the horizon. We relate the horizon fluctuations to boundary correlation functions via holography. Working in perturbative quantum gravity, we find that the quantum width is typically of order $(G_\mathrm{N} L_{\mathrm{AdS}}^3 )^{1/4}$, which is parametrically larger than the Planck scale. In detail, the quantum width depends on the scale at which it is measured, diverging logarithmically in the UV. Our results give the most rigorous evidence to date of gauge-invariant fluctuations at scales much larger than the Planck scale within perturbative quantum gravity.

### [43] [Non-primary square roots in massive gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28208)
*Alexey Golovnev*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者通过理论分析，重新审视dRGT有质量引力和双引力理论中矩阵平方根的定义与性质，区分了主平方根与非主平方根在协变性上的表现，并引入微扰论和解析性（analyticity）分析。

Abstract: Non-linear dRGT massive and bimetric gravities are complicated theories constructed in terms of square roots of matrices. Apart from the technical issues of successfully working with such square roots, there is also a problem of their non-uniqueness. There are claims in the literature that one should better use the principal root. This is a very reasonable conclusion. However, the motivation they give for it is that otherwise there would be non-primary square roots violating the general covariance. In this paper, I would like to show that, if properly understood, the non-primary square roots are also perfectly covariant. At the same time, I recall the relatively old observation that the real problem with such square roots lies in perturbation theory around them. In terms of matrices, it simply does not exist. In terms of the elementary symmetric polynomials used in the Lagrangian density, it is not analytic. Moreover, the non-principal square roots are more prone to getting into the complex domain.

### [44] [Quantum anomalies from three-point on-shell bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28193)
*Hiren Kakkad,Rémy Larue,Alexander Ochirov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用三点壳上（on-shell）技术对量子反常（quantum anomalies）进行自举（bootstrap）分析，仅需经典对称性（classical symmetry）和有效作用量（effective action）的对称性作为输入，无需显式构造作用量形式。该方法使用无质量螺旋旋量（massless helicity spinors）及离散对称性C、P、T的壳上表示，确定了Weyl反常、手征反常（整体与定域）、微分同胚反常和洛伦兹反常，直至实常数前因子，并恢复了规范反常抵消条件，同时发现Weyl反常不应包含Pontryagin密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子反常的计算通常依赖显式的路径积分（path integral）或费曼图（Feynman diagrams）方法，过程繁琐且缺乏系统性。本文旨在发展一种仅基于壳上（on-shell）技术与对称性分析的更简洁、通用的反常自举（bootstrap）框架，以规避对具体作用量形式的依赖。

Method: 方法的核心是在三点（three-point）振幅层次上应用壳上技术。输入条件仅包括：（1）可能被反常破坏的局域或整体经典对称性；（2）有效作用量（effective action）所具备的对称性。具体技术手段包括使用无质量螺旋旋量（massless helicity spinors）以及离散变换C、P、T的壳上表示。

Result: 该方法成功确定了Weyl反常、手征反常（chiral anomaly，包括整体和定域）、微分同胚反常（diffeomorphism anomaly）和洛伦兹反常（Lorentz anomaly），结果精确到实常数前因子（real constant prefactors）。研究还恢复了规范反常抵消条件（gauge-anomaly cancellation conditions），并额外发现Weyl反常不应涉及Pontryagin密度。

Conclusion: 壳上自举方法为分析量子反常提供了一种不依赖于显式拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）或路径积分（path integral）的有效途径。该结果验证了方法本身的可行性，并为后续将自举技术拓展到更复杂的反常问题（如引力反常或更高点振幅）奠定了基础。

Abstract: We bootstrap quantum anomalies using on-shell techniques in the simplest setting: at three points. The necessary field-theoretic input includes the local or global classical symmetry, which the anomaly may break, and the symmetries of the effective action -- though not its explicit form. We use massless helicity spinors together with an on-shell representation of the discrete C, P, and T transformations. Our approach determines the Weyl, chiral (global and local), diffeomorphism, and Lorentz anomalies up to real constant prefactors. In particular, we recover gauge-anomaly cancelation conditions, as well as find that the Weyl anomaly should not involve Pontryagin densities.

### [45] [Higher dimensional quantum Hall effect and the analog of $W_\infty$-algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28219)
*Dimitra Karabali,V. P. Nair*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过拓扑论证（topological arguments）揭示了高维量子霍尔效应（higher dimensional quantum Hall effect）中的阿贝尔（Abelian）与非阿贝尔（nonabelian）规范变换与 W∞ 变换之间的类比关系，并利用降序程序（descent procedure）中的双上循环（two-cocycle）和体-边界反常抵消（bulk-boundary anomaly cancellation）推导了边缘模（edge modes）上的对易子反常（commutator anomaly）及扩展代数。体作用量（bulk actions）通过 Dolbeault 指数定理（Dolbeault index theorem）构造，所得代数与现有边缘模计算结果一致，并比较了二维与更高维下变换性质的异同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高维量子霍尔效应中规范变换与 W∞ 变换之间的深层结构联系，并利用纯拓扑方法推导边缘模上的反常代数，从而统一理解不同维度下的这类变换行为。

Method: 采用拓扑论证方法，利用反常的降序程序中的双上循环以及体-边界作用量之间的反常抵消机制；体作用量通过 Dolbeault 指数定理统一构造。

Result: 建立了阿贝尔/非阿贝尔规范变换与 W∞ 变换在高维量子霍尔效应中的类比关系；推导了边缘模上对易子反常及扩展代数，结果与已有边缘模显式计算一致。

Conclusion: 所提出的拓扑方法为构造高维量子霍尔效应中的体作用量及分析边缘反常代数提供了统一框架，并揭示了二维与更高维之间变换性质的相似性与差异。

Abstract: We show that Abelian and nonabelian gauge transformations are the analog of $W_\infty$ transformations for higher dimensional quantum Hall effect. The commutator anomaly and the extended algebra of such transformations on the edge modes of a droplet are obtained by purely topological arguments, basically utilizing the two-cocycle in the descent procedure for anomalies and using the fact that there is anomaly cancellation between the bulk and boundary actions. The method relies on the fact that bulk actions are easily constructed in general using the Dolbeault index theorem. The resulting algebras are shown to agree with explicit edge mode calculations for cases where they are available. We also comment on the similarities and differences in the nature of these transformations between two and higher dimensions.

</details>


### [46] [Multi--black holes in Bertotti--Robinson spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28232)
*Hideo Furugori,Jun-ichi Sakamoto,Shinya Tomizawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用可积西格玛模型中的单值矩阵（monodromy-matrix）形式，在 Bertotti–Robinson 时空背景下构造了一类描述多黑洞的精确解，包括 Majumdar–Papapetrou 型与 Israel–Wilson–Perjés 型解，并证明了该框架的系统性与推广能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平凡背景（如 Bertotti–Robinson 时空）中构造多黑洞精确解是经典广义相对论中的重要问题；现有方法缺乏系统性框架，本文旨在利用可积结构填补这一空白。

Method: 从极端的 Reissner–Nordström 黑洞出发，推导对应的陪集（coset）矩阵与单值矩阵，利用其幂零（nilpotent）代数结构实现单值矩阵的显式分解；通过在单值矩阵中引入多极点，推广至多中心构型，并进一步考虑更一般的幂零元以涵盖稳态及 Israel–Wilson–Perjés 型解。

Result: 构造了具有 Bertotti–Robinson 渐近行为的 Majumdar–Papapetrou 型多黑洞解，每一中心对应一个具有 AdS₂ × S² 近极端几何（near-horizon geometry）的规则极端黑洞；此外将框架推广至稳态 Bertotti–Robinson 时空及更广的 Israel–Wilson–Perjés 型解。

Conclusion: 单值矩阵方法为非平凡背景下的多黑洞解构造提供了强大且系统的框架，并为更一般构型的研究指出了有前景的路径。

Abstract: We construct a new class of exact solutions describing multi-black holes in the Bertotti--Robinson spacetime, using the monodromy-matrix formalism associated with integrable sigma models. Starting from the extremal Reissner--Nordström black hole in the Bertotti--Robinson background, we derive the corresponding coset and monodromy matrices and show that they are governed by nilpotent algebraic structures. This property enables an explicit factorization of the monodromy matrix, allowing for a systematic reconstruction of the underlying gravitational solutions. We extend this construction to multi-center configurations by introducing multiple poles in the monodromy matrix, leading to Majumdar--Papapetrou--type solutions with Bertotti--Robinson asymptotics. Each center is shown to correspond to a regular extremal black hole with an $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times S^2$ near-horizon geometry, and the asymptotic end likewise approaches a Bertotti--Robinson geometry. We further generalize the framework to stationary configurations in the Bertotti--Robinson spacetime, as well as to a broader class of Israel--Wilson--Perjés-type solutions, by considering more general nilpotent elements. Our results demonstrate that the monodromy-matrix approach provides a powerful and systematic framework for constructing multi-black hole solutions in nontrivial backgrounds, and suggest a promising route toward more general configurations.

</details>


### [47] [Gravitational Compton scattering at the fourth post-Minkowskian order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28239)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算更高后闵可夫斯基阶（post-Minkowskian order）的引力康普顿散射过程是理解引力波散射相移及验证理论框架一致性的关键步骤，现有结果尚未覆盖$\mathcal{O}(G^4)$阶。

Method: 采用世界线量子场论（Worldline Quantum Field Theory）框架，计算了$\mathcal{O}(G^4)$阶的经典引力康普顿振幅。

Result: 成功获得了第四后闵可夫斯基阶的经典引力康普顿振幅及相应的$N$-矩阵元，后者给出了同阶的引力波散射相移。

Conclusion: 计算结果与黑洞微扰理论（black-hole perturbation theory）一致，验证了所得振幅的正确性。

Abstract: We compute the classical gravitational Compton amplitude at the fourth post-Minkowskian order, $\mathcal{O}(G^4)$, within the Worldline Quantum Field Theory framework. We derive the associated $N$-matrix element, which provides the gravitational-wave scattering phase shift at the same order. As a nontrivial check, we show that our result agrees with black-hole perturbation theory.

### [48] [Quantum Fluctuations of the Black Hole Horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28243)
*Ben Freivogel,Antony Speranza,Erik Verlinde*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在量子引力（quantum gravity）框架下，定义并计算了经典黑洞视界（event horizon）的“量子宽度（quantum width）”，发现该宽度依赖于探测探针的分辨率，且在特定参数条件下可远大于普朗克尺度（Planck scale）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典黑洞具有尖锐的事件视界，但在量子力学（quantum mechanics）中视界应存在量子涨落（quantum fluctuation）。Marolf 提出的“量子宽度”概念缺乏明确的可观测定义，本文旨在通过物理实验方案给出可计算的定义。

Method: 通过一个物理实验来定义量子宽度：考察从向内传播的光线（ingoing light ray）发出的信号能够逃逸到无穷远的最后时刻。在微扰量子引力（perturbative quantum gravity）框架下，对球对称黑洞（spherically symmetric black hole）进行计算。

Result: 计算表明，量子宽度依赖于探测探针的分辨率（resolution of the probe），且通常远大于普朗克尺度。以四维史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）为例，在特定参数区间内，大小为 $σ_\perp$ 的一块视界区域，其量子宽度约为 $\sqrt{l_P r_s^2/σ_\perp}$。

Conclusion: 黑洞视界的量子宽度并非普朗克尺度的固定量，而是与探测分辨率相关的可观测量，这一结论对量子引力（quantum gravity）中的黑洞物理研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: Classical black holes have sharply defined event horizons, but quantum mechanically the horizon acquires a quantum uncertainty, called the `quantum width' by Marolf. We propose a definition of the quantum width by a physical experiment involving the last moment a signal emitted from an ingoing light ray can escape to infinity. Calculations of this observable for spherically symmetric black holes in perturbative quantum gravity reveal that the quantum width depends on the resolution of the probe, and is often much larger than the Planck scale. For example, for Schwarzschild black holes in four dimensions in a particular regime of parameters, a piece of the horizon of size $σ_\perp$ has quantum width roughly $\sqrt{l_P r_s^2/σ_\perp}$.

</details>


### [49] [Spinor-helicity formalism for continuous-spin particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28245)
*Thomas Basile,Xavier Bekaert,Felipe Figueroa,Evgeny Skvortsov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用单个双分量旋量提出了一种连续自旋粒子（CSP）的新形式体系，使得振幅计算得以简化，并揭示了CSP振幅与有质量粒子振幅的无穷自旋极限、黑洞散射中的指数因子以及自对偶理论中共线振幅之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为连续自旋粒子（continuous-spin particles, CSP）建立一套更简洁、易于计算振幅的形式体系，以弥补现有方法在振幅构造上的不足。

Method: 借助单个双分量旋量（two-component spinor）构建渐近态，通过固定齐次度（homogeneity degree）分解自然导出螺旋度（helicity）态；将CSP振幅视为有质量粒子振幅的无穷自旋极限（infinite-spin limit），并类比黑洞散射中某种普适因子的指数化（exponentiation）行为。

Result: 发现了非平凡的CSP共线振幅（collinear amplitudes），其中共线分数（collinear fractions）受表征不同CSP的量纲参数（dimensionful parameter）约束；验证了振幅中的指数化普适因子与黑洞散射的类比成立。

Conclusion: 提出了一种基于旋量的CSP新表述，统一了CSP振幅与有质量粒子极限、黑洞散射及自对偶（self-dual）理论中共线振幅之间的多种联系，为CSP散射振幅研究提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We propose a new formulation of continuous-spin particles (CSP) with the help of a single two-component spinor to build asymptotic states. This formulation allows to write down amplitudes in a straightforward way, similar to the massless spinor-helicity approach. The helicity states naturally emerge upon decomposing into components of a fixed homogeneity degree. We show that CSP amplitudes can be understood as the infinite-spin limit of amplitudes of massive particles and, similarly to the scattering of black holes, a certain universal factor exponentiates. In analogy with the recent discovery of collinear amplitudes in self-dual theories, we find nontrivial CSP collinear amplitudes where the collinear fractions are constrained by the dimensionful parameter characterising the various continuous-spin particles.

</details>


### [50] [The cosmology of long range Yukawa interactions in general backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28246)
*Guillem Dom`enech,Panagiotis Giannadakis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文推广了早期宇宙中费米子与轻标量场耦合的研究，在恒定状态方程宇宙学背景下考虑一般的标量场依赖耦合，识别出标度（scaling）和渐近（asymptotic）两种主要动力学机制，并证明标度机制源于标量-费米子作用量的近似标度不变性（scale invariance），在晚期渐近为共形不变性（conformal invariance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙中的长程力可能导致早期结构形成乃至原初黑洞（primordial black holes）的产生，但此前对费米子与轻标量场耦合的研究局限于特定形式，缺乏对一般耦合情况的系统理解。

Method: 在恒定状态方程（equation of state）宇宙学背景下，将标量场依赖的耦合推广到一般形式，通过分析标量场动力学行为划分不同演化机制，并利用作用量的近似对称性解释标度行为的起源。

Result: 识别出两种动力学机制：标度机制中标量场在费米子质量为零的点附近振荡，标量与费米子能量密度比值近似恒定；渐近机制中系统演化至费米子恢复裸质量（bare mass）的构型。标度机制源于作用量的近似标度不变性，晚期进一步成为近似共形不变性。

Conclusion: 该工作为系统研究该系统中扰动增长（growth of perturbations）提供了第一步理论框架，有助于理解早期宇宙的结构形成机制。

Abstract: Long-range forces in the early universe may lead to early structure formation and, perhaps, to primordial black holes. We generalise previous studies of fermions coupled to a light scalar field by considering general scalar-field-dependent couplings in cosmological backgrounds with a constant equation of state. We identify two broad regimes: a scaling regime, in which the scalar field oscillates around a point of vanishing fermion mass, and an asymptotic regime, in which the field evolves toward configurations where the fermions recover their bare mass. We show that the scaling regime arises from an approximate scale invariance in the scalar-fermion action, which becomes an approximate conformal invariance at late times. In the scaling regime, the ratio between the scalar and fermion energy densities is approximately constant. Our work provides a first step toward a general study of the growth of perturbations in this system.

</details>


### [51] [Surface Water Wave Scattering and the Hydrotope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28280)
*Nima Arkani-Hamed,Francesco Calisto,Nail Ussembayev,W. Wayne Zhao,Zihan Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用高能物理方法，推导了深水表面重力波在经典树图水平的散射振幅，在一维水平散射和双负波数（two-negative-wavenumber）扇区内得到了n波散射的闭合公式，其振幅可解释为一种称为“水拓扑（hydrotope）”的多面体体积，统一并推广了Lvov（1997）的五波振幅结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于深水表面重力波散射的计算存在未解决的疑难，Lvov（1997）的五波振幅结果尚缺乏统一框架。本研究旨在利用高能物理中的散射振幅方法，为n波散射建立一般性解析公式，以解决该问题。

Method: 采用高能物理中的经典树图（tree-level）散射振幅方法，研究一维水平方向上的深水表面重力波散射；聚焦于“两负波数”（two-negative-wavenumber）扇区，通过分析不同运动学区域中“腔室”（chambers）的符号模式，将散射振幅表示为一种由超平面切割的经典多面体——水拓扑（hydrotope）的体积。

Result: 在一维水平散射和双负波数扇区内，获得了n波散射的闭合公式（closed formula）。该公式由一个运动学前因子（kinematic prefactor）与一个多面体体积的乘积构成，其中多面体称为“水拓扑”；该公式最初在“最简单”运动学腔室中以单项表达式被发现，最终推广至所有腔室。

Conclusion: 该结果解答了Lvov（1997）五波振幅计算中遗留的疑难，将其统一推广至任意波数（任意n值）情形，展示了高能物理方法在经典波动散射问题中的有效性。

Abstract: We study the classical tree-level scattering amplitudes of deep-water surface gravity waves using the methods of high-energy physics. For scattering in one horizontal dimension and in the two-negative-wavenumber sector we obtain a closed formula for $n$-wave scattering. Up to a kinematic prefactor, the amplitude is the volume of a classic polytope -- a box sliced by a hyperplane, which we dub the hydrotope, whose purpose in life is simply to organize the sign patterns of the "chambers" characterizing all the different regions of the two-minus kinematic space. The general formula was discovered by Claude Opus 4.6 working under our guidance, beginning with our earlier discovery of a one-term expression valid in the "simplest" kinematic chamber. Our results resolve the puzzle raised by Y.V. Lvov's 1997 computation of the five-wave amplitudes, unifying and extending it to all multiplicities.

</details>

### [52] [Eigenvalue Statistics of Random Quantum Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27809)
*Mingpu Jiang,Jianhui Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限维参数依赖随机哈密顿量中量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor, QGT）的本征值统计，获得了N=2和N=3情况的精确解析结果，并提出了适用于任意N和D的有限维QGT本征值统计描述框架，通过数值模拟验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何张量（QGT）在凝聚态物理、拓扑相和量子相变中具有广泛应用，其本征值能够刻画随机量子几何的尺度、各向异性和有效秩，超越了迹（trace）等标量量；然而，QGT本征值的统计性质尚缺乏系统研究。

Method: 针对有限维参数依赖的随机哈密顿量（random Hamiltonian），推导了N=2和N=3情形的QGT本征值统计精确解析结果；并构建了一个适用于任意N和参数空间维度D的有限维QGT本征值统计描述（finite-N, arbitrary-D description），通过数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 获得了N=2和N=3两个非平凡情形的精确解析结果，其中N=3已展现出真实的形状涨落（shape fluctuations）；提出的有限N、任意D描述框架与数值模拟结果一致。

Conclusion: 该研究为有限维无序和混沌系统中的随机量子几何（random quantum geometry）提供了精确基准（exact benchmarks）和实用框架。

Abstract: The quantum geometric tensor is a fundamental property of quantum states, with broad applications in condensed matter physics, topological phases, and quantum phase transitions. The eigenvalues characterize the scale, anisotropy, and effective rank of random quantum geometry, going beyond scalar quantities such as the trace. Here we study the eigenvalue statistics of the quantum geometric tensor in finite-dimensional parameter-dependent random Hamiltonians. We obtain exact analytical results for the first two nontrivial cases, $N=2$ and $N=3$, with $N=3$ already showing genuine shape fluctuations. We further propose a finite-$N$, arbitrary-$D$ description of QGT eigenvalue statistics and verify it by numerical simulations. Our results provide exact benchmarks and a practical framework for random quantum geometry in finite-dimensional disordered and chaotic systems.

### [53] [A stochastic model of a nuclear reactor with directed percolation. Overjump and maximum power](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27874)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在重尾分布描述中子链长度的条件下，核反应堆系统的随机风险行为，旨在估计超过临界阈值的波动概率以及功率定律跳跃分布下的风险界限。

Method: 采用随机风险模型进行模拟，分析中子链长度服从帕累托分布的反应堆行为；计算超过临界阈值的波动概率；估计幂律分布跳跃的风险界限；并考虑实际反应堆的有限尺寸以及对截断列维过程（truncated Lévy process）的自相关函数进行分析。

Result: 获得了反应堆功率最大值、首次达到最大值的时刻以及超调量分布等泛函；建立了形状参数与反应堆物理常数之间的关系，以及形状参数与噪声谱和物理常数之间的关系；给出了截断列维过程的自相关函数与其与中子通量监测设备频率滤波器之间的关系。

Conclusion: 随机风险模型能够有效描述重尾分布下的核反应堆行为，所得关系将概率模型的形状参数与反应堆的物理常数、噪声谱及监测设备特性联系起来，为反应堆安全分析提供了理论依据。

Abstract: A stochastic risk model is applied to simulating the behavior of a nuclear reactor in a situation where the neutron chain length is described by a distribution with heavy "tails," such as the Pareto distribution. Probabilities of a fluctuation exceeding a critical threshold are obtained, and risk bounds for power-law distributions of jumps are estimated. Functionals of the reactor power maximum, the instant of first reaching the maximum, and the distribution of the overjump magnitude are considered. A relationship between the shape parameter and the physical constants of reactors is obtained, as well as the relationship with the noise spectrum and physical constants. The finite dimensions of a real reactor are taken into account. The autocorrelation function of the truncated Lévy process and its relationship with the frequency filters of the neutron flux monitoring equipment are considered.

</details>


### [54] [Phase structure of the Random Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28103)
*Alessio Giorlandino,Eric De Giuli,Sebastian Goldt*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究揭示随机语言模型（Random Language Model, RLM）在双极限标度下存在一系列相变层次，并建立了与随机能量模型（Random Energy Model）的联系，导出与大型语言模型（LLM）中Heaps定律和上下文长度标度一致的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上下文无关文法（context-free grammar）是人类语言层级结构的最小模型，但随机语言模型（RLM）从无序输出到结构化文本的相变位置与性质此前尚不明确。

Method: 采用双极限标度（double-scaling limit），即文法温度 $\tildeε_d \to 0$ 且隐藏符号数 $N \to \infty$，固定参数 $x = \tildeε_d \log N$；通过识别RLM与随机能量模型（Random Energy Model）之间的等价关系进行分析，并采用半退火近似（semi-annealed approximation）导出标度律。

Result: 发现一系列相变：符号间关联涌现、单符号边际分布（single-symbol marginals）变为非均匀、规则使用在玻璃相（glassy phase）中冻结。半退火近似导出的规则使用、熵和能量的非平凡标度律与Heaps定律（Heaps' law）及大型语言模型（large language model, LLM）中的上下文长度标度（context-length scaling）一致。

Conclusion: RLM在双极限标度下展现出层次化的相变结构，其与随机能量模型的联系为理解语言模型的统计力学行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Context-free grammars are minimal models of hierarchical structure in human language, generating structured text from recursive production rules. The Random Language Model (RLM) [De Giuli, PRL 2019], an ensemble of such grammars with random rule weights, exhibits a cross-over from gibberish-like output to structured text as a function of a "temperature", but the location and nature of this transition remained unclear. Here, we show that the RLM exhibits a hierarchy of phase transitions in a double-scaling limit where the grammar temperature $\tildeε_d \to 0$ and the number of hidden symbols $N \to \infty$ at fixed $x = \tildeε_d \log N$. By identifying the relation between RLM and the Random Energy Model, we identify a series of transitions where correlations between symbols emerge, single-symbol marginals become non-uniform, and rule use freezes in a glassy phase. A semi-annealed approximation yields nontrivial scaling laws for rule usage, entropy, and energy, consistent with Heaps' law and context-length scaling observed in large language models.

</details>


### [55] [Scaling limit of the Random Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28105)
*Eric De Giuli*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文在标度极限（scaling limit）下建立了随机语言模型（RLM）的定量理论，揭示了在临界值 $x_c=1/8$ 处的凝聚相变（condensation transition）和 $x=1/2$ 处的熵减少特征尺度，推导了规则数量、熵等可观测量在不同标度区间的标度律（scaling law），并解决了关于热力学相变存在性的先前争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对随机语言模型（Random Language Model, RLM）——一种基于随机上下文无关文法（stochastic context-free grammar）的整体——是否存在热力学相变（thermodynamic transition）存在歧义，且缺乏对有限语料库长度和大隐藏符号数量下模型行为的定量理解。

Method: 在隐藏符号数量 $N \to \infty$ 且文法温度 $\tildeε_d \to 0$ 的标度极限下，固定参数 $x = {\tildeε}_d \log N$，基于规则使用模式（rule-usage patterns）的大偏差原理（large-deviation principle）实现对模型的可控描述；并通过半退火近似（semi-annealed approximation）将问题映射到一类具有非平凡组合结构的随机能量模型（Random Energy Model）。

Result: RLM 在临界值 $x_c = 1/8$ 处存在凝聚相变，低于此值时规则使用发生集中且语言统计量依赖于语料库长度；在 $x = 1/2$ 处出现熵从最大值减少的起始特征尺度。推导了不同规则数量、熵等可观测量的显式标度律，识别出由文法规模、语料库长度和温度共同控制的标度区、饱和区和临界区。

Conclusion: 该理论解释了热力学相变的存在争议，并将缓慢趋近大 $N$ 极限归因于对 $\log N$ 的依赖。提供了一个统一框架，显示语言的普适统计特性可从生成文法的典型实现中涌现，对自然语言统计和大语言模型（large language models）行为具有启示意义。

Abstract: We develop a quantitative theory of the Random Language Model (RLM), an ensemble of stochastic context-free grammars, in a scaling limit where the number of hidden symbols $N \to \infty$ while the grammar temperature $\tildeε_d \to 0$ at fixed $x = {\tildeε}_d \log N$. In this limit, the model admits a controlled description based on a large-deviation principle over rule-usage patterns. A semi-annealed approximation maps the problem to a class of Random Energy Models with nontrivial combinatorics.
  We show that the RLM exhibits a condensation transition at a critical value $x_c=1/8$, below which rule usage concentrates and language statistics acquire a nontrivial dependence on corpus length. A second characteristic scale at $x=1/2$ marks the onset of entropy reduction from its maximal value. Across these regimes, we derive explicit scaling laws for the number of distinct rules, entropy, and related observables, identifying distinct scaling, saturation, and critical regimes controlled by the interplay of grammar size, corpus length, and temperature.
  The theory resolves previous ambiguities regarding the existence of a thermodynamic transition and explains the slow approach to the large-$N$ limit as a consequence of the dependence on $\log N$. It further provides a unified framework in which universal statistical properties of language emerge from typical realizations of generative grammars, with implications for both natural language statistics and the behavior of large language models.

</details>


### [56] [Classical versus quantum Anderson localization in disordered systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28262)
*Stefano Mossa,Giancarlo Ruocco,Walter Schirmacher*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本论文通过比较标量经典波（在质量和力常数无序下）与电子紧束缚模型（在对角和非对角无序下），揭示了经典波体系与标准电子安德森模型之间不存在直接的数学对应关系。经典波体系属于一种受约束的无序类别，其中声学求和规则（acoustic sum rule）关联了对角和非对角矩阵元。在统一的本征值框架下，论文确定了四种无序类别的局域化相图，发现经典波系统与非对角无序电子系统类似，局域态仅出现在带边附近，而扩展态在强无序下仍可在谱中心存在；同时，声学求和规则导致了与电子系统根本不同的局域化拓扑结构。特别是质量无序相图与基于传统势方法的以往结果存在定性差异，并在上带边附近揭示了一个扩展局域化区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究常将经典波局域化映射为带对角无序的电子安德森模型，但这种映射的数学合理性未被严格检验。澄清这一映射的有效性，并建立经典波体系与电子无序模型的正确比较框架，对理解三维光子与声学介质中的安德森局域化（Anderson localization）至关重要。

Method: 论文从数学上比较了质量无序和力常数无序的标量经典波与对角和非对角无序的电子紧束缚模型，指出经典波系统应采用正确的模量型（modulus-type）表述，而非传统势能型（potential-type）映射。随后在统一的本征值框架下，利用互补的谱诊断（spectral diagnostics）、本征向量诊断（eigenvector diagnostics）和能级统计诊断（level-statistics diagnostics）来确定所有四种无序类别的局域化相图。

Result: 经典波系统与电子非对角无序系统共享一个关键定性特征：局域态仅出现在带边附近，而扩展态在强无序下仍能在谱中心区域存在。然而，声学求和规则导致经典波系统的局域化拓扑结构（localization topologies）与对角和非对角无序电子系统均存在根本差异。在质量无序情形下，得到的相图与传统势方法的结果定性不同，并在上带边附近发现了一个扩展局域化区间（extended localized regime）。

Conclusion: 经典波体系构成一个独立的受约束无序类别，不能简单地映射为标准电子安德森模型。研究结果为量子与经典波系统中的局域化提供了统一视角，并为在三维光子与声学介质中实现安德森局域化提供了新的条件认知。

Abstract: We investigate Anderson localization in three-dimensional disordered systems by comparing scalar classical waves with mass and force-constant disorder to electronic tight-binding models with diagonal and off-diagonal disorder. We show that the commonly employed mapping between classical-wave localization and the electronic Anderson model with diagonal disorder is not mathematically justified. Instead, the correct modulus-type formulation reveals that classical-wave systems constitute a distinct constrained disorder class, in which the acoustic sum rule correlates diagonal and off-diagonal matrix elements and prevents any direct correspondence with the standard electronic disorder models. Within a unified eigenvalue framework, we determine localization phase diagrams for all four disorder classes using complementary spectral, eigenvector, and level-statistics diagnostics. We find that classical-wave systems share a key qualitative feature with electronic off-diagonal disorder: localized states occur only near a band edge, while extended states persist in the central part of the spectrum even at strong disorder. At the same time, the acoustic sum rule produces localization topologies that differ fundamentally from both diagonal- and off-diagonal-disorder electronic systems. In particular, for mass disorder we obtain a phase diagram that differs qualitatively from previous results based on the conventional potential-type approach and reveals an extended localized regime near the upper band edge. Our results establish a unified perspective on localization in quantum and classical wave systems and provide new insight into the conditions under which Anderson localization may occur in three-dimensional photonic and acoustic media.

</details>


### [57] [Stationary point complexity via minimal supersymmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28298)
*Jaron Kent-Dobias*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种4指标超对称（4-index supersymmetric）表示方法，通过自发超对称破缺（spontaneous supersymmetry breaking）自然地处理Kac-Rice公式中Hessian矩阵行列式的绝对值问题，将复杂度问题简化为五个序参量（order parameters），并应用于感知机（perceptron）和Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型等平均场随机景观（mean-field random landscapes）的退火复杂度（annealed complexity）计算，同时自然地推广至淬火复杂度（quenched complexity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在利用Kac-Rice公式计算平均场随机景观中驻点（stationary points）统计量时，Hessian矩阵行列式的绝对值是一个长期存在的技术障碍。忽略绝对值虽然能产生优雅的2指标超对称表示，但常常导致不正确的结果。因此，需要一种新方法自然且正确地处理该绝对值问题。

Method: 作者提出了一种扩展的4指标超对称表示方法，通过沿特定超空间方向的自发超对称破缺自然地引入Hessian行列式的绝对值。假设没有额外的对称性破缺，问题可约化为五个序参量，这些序参量对应于由自发超对称破缺算符生成的超空间算符代数（superspace operator algebra）的元素。

Result: 将序参量与驻点的几何和谱性质相关联，证明超对称破缺序参量对应于Hessian矩阵在零特征值处的谱密度（spectral density）。将该形式应用于感知机和Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型，成功计算了退火复杂度。该框架可自然推广至淬火复杂度，其中每个序参量对应一个副本矩阵（replica matrix）。

Conclusion: 所发展的4指标超对称表示方法有效解决了平均场随机景观中驻点统计计算中长期存在的绝对值技术难题，提供了一个统一的框架，可同时处理退火和淬火复杂度问题。

Abstract: The statistics of stationary points are a powerful way to understand mean-field random landscapes, and the Kac--Rice formula is a general way to compute them. A longstanding technical barrier to these calculations is the presence of the absolute value of the determinant of the Hessian. Neglecting the absolute value produces an elegant 2-index supersymmetric representation of the problem, but is often incorrect. We develop an expanded 4-index supersymmetric representation of the complexity problem which incorporates the absolute value naturally via spontaneous supersymmetry breaking along a particular superspace direction. Positing that no additional symmetry breaking occurs implies the reduction to five order parameters corresponding to elements of a superspace operator algebra generated by the spontaneously SUSY-breaking operator. We relate the order parameters to the geometry and spectra of stationary points, showing that the SUSY-breaking order parameter corresponds to the spectral density of the Hessian at zero eigenvalue. We give examples of this formalism applied to calculate the annealed complexity of several models, including the perceptron and the Sherrington--Kirkpatrick model. The framework is naturally extended to quenched complexity, where each order parameter corresponds to a replica matrix.

</details>

### [58] [Machine learning fully hadronic events with spectral functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27420)
*Mohammad Mahdi Altakach,Hadi Hassan,Sabine Kraml,Kazuki Sakurai,Haitham Zaraket*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用两点关联谱函数（two-point correlation spectral function）作为强子对撞机上全强子事件机器学习分析的输入特征，该特征与喷注多重数（jet multiplicity）无关且编码了事件信息。以胶微子对产生（gluino-pair production）衰变到顶夸克对加中性微子信号为例，结合谱函数的神经网络（dense neural network）相比ATLAS现有分析在胶微子质量（gluino-mass）探测范围上提升了约150 GeV，相比仅使用喷注运动学（jet kinematics）的神经网络提升了约250 GeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强子对撞机中全强子事件的特征化面临挑战：硬过程信号喷注（signal jets）与任意数量的初态辐射（ISR）和末态辐射（FSR）喷注混杂，产生大量组合本底（combinatorial background）。同时，机器学习分析要求固定维度的输入特征，但量子色动力学（QCD）辐射导致事件间喷注多重数（jet multiplicity）波动，现有方法难以处理该问题。

Method: 将两点关联谱函数（two-point correlation spectral function）作为机器学习分析的输入特征。该函数将事件的横动量（transverse-momentum）数据映射为关于角距离（angular distance）的一维函数，在模去对撞等距性（collider isometries）和喷注排列（jet permutations）后编码事件信息，且其定义与喷注多重数无关。

Result: 以胶微子对产生（gluino-pair production）并衰变至 t t-bar 加中性微子的全强子终态为基准，利用 139 fb⁻¹ 的 13 TeV pp 对撞数据，基于谱函数特征的密集神经网络（dense neural network）将胶微子质量（gluino-mass）的预期探测范围相比近期ATLAS分析提升了约150 GeV，相比仅使用喷注运动学（jet kinematics）的同一网络提升了约250 GeV。

Conclusion: 两点关联谱函数能有效解决喷注多重数可变性带来的固定维度输入问题，显著提升全强子事件中超出标准模型新物理信号的机器学习分析性能。

Abstract: Characterising fully hadronic events is a difficult task at hadron colliders. Signal jets from the hard process are mingled with an arbitrary number of ISR and FSR jets, leading to a large combinatorial background. This also poses a challenge for machine-learning analyses, where the number of input features is fixed while the jet multiplicity fluctuates from event to event due to QCD radiation. In this work, we explore the use of the two-point correlation spectral function as an input feature for machine-learning analyses of such events. The spectral function maps the transverse-momentum data of an event into a one-dimensional function of the angular distance, encoding the event information modulo collider isometries and jet permutations, and is defined independently of the jet multiplicity. As a concrete benchmark we apply the method to discriminate gluino-pair production followed by $\tilde{g} \to t \bar{t} \tildeχ_1^0$ against the fully hadronic $t \bar{t}$ background. With $139~{\rm fb}^{-1}$ of $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV $pp$ collision data, a dense neural network supplied with spectral-function features improves the expected reach in gluino-mass by roughly 150 GeV relative to a recent ATLAS analysis, and by roughly 250 GeV relative to the same network trained on jet kinematics alone.

</details>


### [59] [Collider Probes of Dark Energy Microphysics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27441)
*Chaitanya Bashyam,Alfredo Gurrola,Andres Florez,Cristian Rodriguez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用高能对撞机（如LHC）上超越标准模型（BSM）中介子共振的测量来探测暗能量微观物理，通过构建有效场论框架，将动力学暗能量标量场与2HDM+$a$模型中的赝标量中介子耦合，使对撞机观测量（如衰变宽度、分支比和运动学结构）对暗能量涨落声速敏感，从而建立一种从最小尺度（对撞机）到最大尺度（宇宙加速）的新的探测试验范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗能量的物理起源是现代物理学最深远的开放问题之一；当前宇宙学观测虽能约束状态方程参数$w$，但无法揭示暗能量的微观物理，因为许多不同的理论模型可以再现相同的膨胀历史。暗能量扰动声速是区分这些模型的关键量，但现有天体物理观测对此基本无约束，亟需新的探測手段。

Method: 构建一个统一的低能有效场论（effective-field-theory, EFT）框架，其中动力学暗能量标量场通过对称性驱动的导数相互作用（derivative interactions）与2HDM+$a$模型中的赝标量中介子耦合。这些相互作用会导致中介子不可见衰变（invisible decays）并改变其在暗能量背景中的传播特性，从而在对撞机上产生可测量的共振属性畸变。

Result: 中介子的衰变宽度、分支比和运动学结构变得对暗能量涨落的传播性质（尤其是声速（sound speed））敏感。因此，对撞机观测量可以直接且互补地探测暗能量微观物理，有潜力区分那些仅通过宇宙学无法区分的理论模型。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了高能对撞机实验探测宇宙加速物理的新范式，揭示了自然界最小尺度与最大尺度之间的联系，开辟了一条揭示暗能量基本起源的新型实验路径。

Abstract: The physical origin of dark energy remains one of the most profound open questions in modern physics. Although cosmological observations tightly constrain the equation of state parameter $w$, this information alone does not reveal the underlying microphysics, as many distinct theoretical models can reproduce the same expansion history. A key discriminator among these models is the sound speed of dark energy perturbations, yet this quantity remains largely unconstrained by current astrophysical observations. In this work, we propose a fundamentally new approach: using collider measurements of beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) mediator resonances as a probe of dark energy microphysics. We construct a unified effective-field-theory framework in which a dynamical dark energy scalar is coupled, through symmetry-motivated derivative interactions, to a pseudoscalar mediator in the 2HDM+$a$ model. These interactions naturally induce invisible decays and modify the propagation of the BSM mediator in a dark energy background, leading to measurable distortions of resonance properties at colliders such as the LHC. We show that the decay widths, branching ratios, and kinematic structure of the mediator resonance become sensitive to the propagation properties of dark energy fluctuations, in particular the sound speed. As a result, collider observables provide a direct and complementary handle on dark energy microphysics, with the potential to distinguish between models that are otherwise indistinguishable through cosmology alone. Our results establish a new paradigm in which high-energy collider experiments can probe the physics of cosmic acceleration, revealing a connection between the smallest and largest scales in nature and opening a novel experimental pathway to uncover the fundamental origin of dark energy.

</details>


### [60] [$t \bar{t}$ production as a window to invisible new physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27613)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于MadGraph5_aMC@NLO简化暗物质模型生成$pp \rightarrow t\bar{t}Y_i$（$i=0,1$）信号样本，中介子质量固定为5 GeV，仅考虑$t\bar{t}$系统的双轻子（dileptonic）末态，通过运动学拟合（kinematic fit）进行重建，并包含所有相关标准模型（SM）本底。

Result: 该分析对轻自旋-1中介子具有灵敏度，CP敏感的角度观测量（CP-sensitive angular observables）能够在矢量（vector）、轴矢量（axial-vector）、标量和赝标量场景之间提供区分能力。

Conclusion: $t\bar{t}$末态不仅可用于搜寻不可见粒子，还能在发现后对其自旋和宇称（parity）性质进行表征。

Abstract: We present a phenomenological study where we probe the sensitivity to invisible dark matter (DM) mediators produced in association with a $t\bar{t}$ pair at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). Building on previous work focused on scalar mediators, we extend the analysis to include spin-1 mediators, $Y_1$, with both vector and axial-vector couplings to top quarks. The mediator mass is fixed to 5 GeV. Signal samples of $pp \rightarrow t\bar{t}Y_i$ ($i = 0, 1$) are generated using a MadGraph5_aMC@NLO simplified DM model. Only dileptonic final states of the $t\bar{t}$ system are considered, and the reconstruction is performed through a kinematic fit without explicitly reconstructing the invisible mediator. All relevant Standard Model backgrounds are included. We consider several exclusion scenarios to assess the sensitivity to the presence of a spin-1 mediator, as well as the ability to distinguish a pure vector or axial-vector mediator from alternative hypotheses with different spin and CP properties. We find that the analysis is sensitive to light spin-1 mediators and that CP-sensitive angular observables provide discrimination power between vector, axial-vector, scalar and pseudoscalar scenarios. These results highlight the potential of $t\bar{t}$ final states not only to search for invisible particles, but also to characterize their spin and parity properties in case of discovery.

### [61] [Quantum Correlations in the Decay of $B^0$ meson and Entanglement Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28034)
*Divya Sharma,Vaibhav Rawoot,Sudip Kumar Haldar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对B⁰介子衰变为两个矢量介子（构成双qutrit系统）过程中的量子关联进行了唯象学研究，利用纠缠熵等量子纠缠度量分析了衰变动力学中的量子特性，发现纠缠度量与衰变分支比之间存在关联，且相角对纠缠熵有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高能粒子物理过程中量子关联的表征方法，并检验纠缠度量（entanglement measures）能否为B⁰介子衰变动力学提供新的物理洞察。

Method: 采用纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）和Rényi熵（Rényi entropy）作为量子关联度量，基于LHCb、ATLAS和Belle合作组的极化振幅与相对相位的实验测量数据，计算并对比不同衰变道的Hartley熵、von Neumann熵、碰撞熵（collision entropy）和最小熵（min-entropy）以及线性熵（linear entropy）、I-concurrence、tangle、 negativity、对数负性（logarithmic negativity）、Schmidt系数与Schmidt秩等多种纠缠度量。

Result: 纠缠熵对相角（phase）具有强依赖性；von Neumann熵与衰变分支比（branching fraction）之间存在关联，揭示了弱相互作用和强相互作用在产生量子纠缠中的作用；不同Rényi阶数下的熵值表现出差异化的行为。

Conclusion: 纠缠度量能够为高能粒子物理中的衰变动力学提供有价值的洞察，有望成为理解量子关联的重要工具。

Abstract: We present a phenomenological study of quantum correlations in the decay of $B^0$ mesons into a system of two vector mesons. The decay of the $B^0$ meson into two vector mesons constitutes a bipartite system of two qutrits. The entanglement entropy is used as a measure of quantum correlations in the system of decaying particles. We study the variation of the Rényi entropy with Rényi order ($α$) for the decay channels $B_s^0 \rightarrow φ\, φ$, $B_d^0 \rightarrow J/ψ\, K^{*}(892)^0$, $B_d^0 \rightarrow φ\, K^{*}(892)^0$ and $B_s^0 \rightarrow J/ψ\, φ$ and discuss the significance of entanglement entropy at different Rényi order regimes. The LHCb, ATLAS and Belle collaborations experimental measurements of complex polarization amplitudes and relative phases are used as input for our analysis. A comparison of entanglement entropy for all the $B^0$ meson decay processes, with both vanishing and non-vanishing phases, reveals a strong phase dependence of the entropy. We further present the results of Hartley entropy (Max-Entropy), von Neumann entropy, collision entropy, and min-entropy, each corresponding to different values and limits of the Rényi order. The comparison between the branching fractions of the decay processes and the von Neumann entropy shows a connection between entanglement and decay dynamics, indicating the role of weak and strong interaction in generating quantum entanglement. In addition, we evaluate several other entanglement measures, including linear entropy, I-concurrence, tangle, negativity, logarithmic negativity, Schmidt coefficients, and Schmidt rank for different $B^0$ meson decay processes. Our study demonstrates that entanglement measures provide useful insights into the underlying decay dynamics and may serve as important tools for understanding quantum correlations in high-energy particle physics processes.

</details>

*Matteo Cerutti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 基于神经网络参数化，首次在N³LL精度下同时分析Drell-Yan和半单举深度非弹性散射数据，提取了非极化横动量依赖部分子分布（unpolarized TMD PDFs）。发现加入SIDIS数据使分布变宽、不确定度介于仅DY提取与传统模型之间，展示了神经网络方法降低模型依赖性的潜力。

Abstract: A first global analysis of unpolarized Transverse-Momentum-Dependent (TMD) distributions based on a neural-network (NN) parametrization is presented. Drell-Yan (DY) and semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering (SIDIS) data are simultaneously included at next-to-next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic (N$^3$LL) accuracy. The results indicate that the inclusion of SIDIS data leads to broader unpolarized TMD PDFs compared to a DY-only NN extraction. The associated uncertainties are reduced with respect to the DY-only case, while remaining larger than the ones obtained using traditional models. These results demonstrate the potential of flexible NN parametrizations in reducing model dependence and provide guidance for future high-precision measurements at Jefferson Lab and the Electron-Ion Collider.

### [63] [Bootstrapping two-loop six-gluon amplitudes in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27801)
*Sérgio Carrôlo,Dmitry Chicherin,Johannes M. Henn,Qinglin Yang,Yang Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一套程序，将规范理论散射振幅中的最大超越性（maximally transcendental）项作为实际计算工具，利用四维主导奇点（leading singularities）和壳上图（on-shell diagrams）确定平面QCD振幅的有理系数，结合符号自举（symbol bootstrap）首次计算了平面双圈六胶子振幅的最大权重符号（maximal-weight symbol），并得到新的两圈三重共线（triple-collinear）和双软（double-soft）分裂函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，Lipatov及其合作者指出，规范理论散射振幅中最大超越性（即最复杂）的项最接近于最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论。本文的动机是将这一观察转化为实用的计算工具，以求解平面QCD中高圈振幅的最大超越性部分。

Method: 该方法包括：(1) 利用四维主导奇点（leading singularities）和壳上图（on-shell diagrams）对平面QCD振幅中最高权重特殊函数的有理系数进行分类和评估，得到显式共形不变的旋量-螺旋度（spinor-helicity）表达式；(2) 结合最近建立的六粒子两圈函数空间（two-loop six-particle function space）进行符号自举（symbol bootstrap），通过物理一致性条件约束确定振幅的最大权重符号。

Result: 首次得到了平面QCD中两圈六胶子振幅的最大权重符号，首先针对${-}{-}{+}{+}{+}{+}$螺旋度构型，然后推广到所有最大螺旋度违反（MHV）构型。答案由物理一致性条件唯一确定，所需字母表（alphabet）仅含137个符号字母（symbol letters）。作为副产品，得到了此前未知的两圈三重共线和双软分裂函数。

Conclusion: 该程序提供了一种实用的计算方法，将最大超越性项与超对称理论联系起来的观察转化为具体的计算工具。结果展示了符号自举在QCD振幅计算中的有效性，并概述了该方法未来可能拓展的方向。

Abstract: The maximally transcendental, or most complicated, terms of gauge-theory scattering amplitudes have long been singled out, following Lipatov and collaborators, as those parts of a QCD amplitude that most closely mirror maximally supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory. We report on a programme that turns this observation into a practical computational tool. We show that the rational prefactors multiplying the highest-weight special functions of planar QCD amplitudes are governed by four-dimensional leading singularities, which can be classified and evaluated using on-shell diagrams. The resulting prefactors are manifestly conformally invariant and admit compact spinor-helicity expressions that hold for arbitrary multiplicity. Combining this input with the recently established two-loop six-particle function space, we set up a symbol bootstrap and determine, for the first time, the maximal-weight symbol of the planar two-loop six-gluon amplitude in massless QCD, first for the ${-}{-}{+}{+}{+}{+}$ helicity configuration and subsequently for all MHV configurations. The answer is fixed uniquely by physical consistency conditions, requires a reduced alphabet of only $137$ symbol letters, and yields as a byproduct previously unknown two-loop triple-collinear and double-soft splitting functions. We summarise the method and the results, and outline the directions they open up.

</details>


### [64] [Dense and Cold Magnetized Quark Matter: A Review of Magnetic-Field-Independent Regularization and the Medium Separation Scheme](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28111)
*Francisco X. Azeredo,Dyana C. Duarte,Ricardo L. S. Farias,Bruno S. Lopes,João A. R. S. Prado,William R. Tavares*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了在有效量子色动力学模型（尤其是Nambu-Jona-Lasinio模型）中，处理磁化致密夸克物质的正则化方案——磁场无关正则化（MFIR）与介质分离方案（MSS），证明该框架能消除非物理伪影，且在强磁场与高化学势下超导能隙保持有限，不出现零温正常相转变，从而为致密星与重离子碰撞中的极端条件物质提供更稳健的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非可重整化框架（如Nambu-Jona-Lasinio模型）中，紫外发散的处理至关重要；传统正则化方案在磁化和致密环境下可能引入非物理伪影。该综述旨在对比并统一两种正则化方案，以消除这些伪影，获得对极端条件下强相互作用物质的物理自洽描述。

Method: 系统回顾了磁场无关正则化（MFIR）与介质分离方案（MSS）两种正则化方法，并在统一框架下分析冷致密夸克物质的热力学，包括色超导相。MFIR将发散真空贡献与有限磁场相关项分离，MSS则将分离扩展到介质部分，确保仅对真空量进行正则化。

Result: 在该统一框架下，超导能隙在大化学势下保持有限，即使在强磁场存在时也是如此；与传统正则化方案的结果不同，未发现零温下向正常相的转变。该方法消除了虚假振荡及其他非物理伪影。

Conclusion: 真空贡献与介质贡献的恰当分离至关重要，该方案为处于致密星和重离子碰撞相关极端条件下的强相互作用物质提供了更稳健、物理自洽的描述。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive review of regularization schemes for magnetized dense quark matter within effective models of quantum chromodynamics, focusing on the Magnetic-Field-Independent Regularization (MFIR) and the Medium Separation Scheme (MSS) at finite chemical potential and magnetic field. In nonrenormalizable frameworks such as the Nambu-Jona-Lasinio model, the treatment of ultraviolet divergences is crucial, particularly in magnetized and dense environments where conventional regularization procedures may introduce unphysical artifacts. We show that MFIR consistently isolates divergent vacuum contributions from finite magnetic-field-dependent terms, while MSS extends this separation to the medium sector, ensuring that only vacuum quantities are regularized. Within this unified framework, we analyze the thermodynamics of cold and dense quark matter, including color-superconducting phases, and demonstrate that the superconducting gap remains finite at large chemical potentials, even in the presence of strong magnetic fields. In contrast to results obtained with traditional regularization schemes, we find no evidence for a transition to a normal phase at zero temperature, highlighting the importance of a proper separation between vacuum and medium contributions. These results eliminate spurious oscillations and other nonphysical artifacts, leading to a more robust and physically consistent description of strongly interacting matter under extreme conditions relevant to compact stars and heavy-ion collisions.

### [66] [Real poles with opposite-sign residues in the non-perturbative quark propagator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28212)
*R. Alkofer,M. N. Ferreira,A. S. Miramontes,J. M. Morgado,J. Papavassiliou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 通过将标准能隙方程（gap equation）与非微扰夸克-胶子顶点（quark-gluon vertex）动态耦合，研究Landau规范下夸克传播子（quark propagator）的解析结构。结果表明，在亚GeV类时动量区域，适当包含底层动力学会导致一对实极点（real poles），符号相反的留数（residues），且未发现复共轭极点（complex conjugate poles）。该行为由三个主导顶点形状因子（vertex form factors）共同调控，可产生350 MeV的组分夸克质量（constituent quark mass）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准夸克能隙方程在广泛使用的近似下常产生复共轭极点，这类极点存在概念性缺陷（conceptual shortcomings）。本文旨在通过动态耦合完整的夸克-胶子顶点，重新考察夸克传播子在非微扰区域的真实解析结构，以解决上述理论不一致性。

Method: 采用完整的顶点基（full vertex basis），将标准能隙方程与非微扰夸克-胶子顶点进行动态耦合（dynamically coupling）。通过逐步调节三个主导顶点形状因子的强度，分析它们各自及协同作用对夸克传播子解析结构的影响。

Result: 在亚GeV类时动量区域，夸克传播子呈现一对符号相反的实极点，而非广泛使用的近似中出现的复共轭极点。这一解析结构由三个顶点形状因子主导：树图分量（tree-level component）、反常色磁矩（anomalous chromomagnetic moment）以及一个被命名为“自旋-动量曲率”（spin-momentum curvature）的分量。三者协同作用将低能极点稳定在实轴上，并产生约350 MeV的组分夸克质量。

Conclusion: 该实极点结构避免了复共轭极点带来的概念问题，同时与色禁闭（color confinement）中关于正性破坏（positivity violation）的要求完全兼容。这为理解夸克传播子在非微扰能区的行为提供了更自洽的解析图像。

Abstract: We investigate the analytic structure of the quark propagator in the Landau gauge by dynamically coupling the standard gap equation to the non-perturbative quark-gluon vertex. Employing the full vertex basis, we demonstrate that for sub-GeV time-like momenta, the proper inclusion of the underlying dynamics leads to a pair of real poles with opposite-sign residues. In particular, in stark contradistinction to the results obtained in widely used approximations, we see no sign of complex conjugate poles. This distinctive analytic structure evades conceptual shortcomings frequently associated with complex conjugate poles while remaining fully compatible with the aspects of color confinement related to positivity violation. Crucially, this novel behavior is governed by a dominant triplet of vertex form factors: the tree-level component, the anomalous chromomagnetic moment, and a component we label as "spin-momentum curvature". By gradually tuning the individual strengths of these components, we demonstrate that while they contribute in distinct ways to the quark propagator, their joint action is vital for stabilizing the system. Together, they place the low-lying poles onto the real axis while producing a robust constituent quark mass of $350$ MeV.

</details>


### [67] [Particle Production from Inhomogeneities: the off-shell side of gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28297)
*Michele Redi,Andrea Tesi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了早期宇宙中引力非均匀性导致的粒子产生机制，建立了暗物质产生与引力波信号之间的现象学联系，并表明在亚视界尺度上，该过程可简化为引力散射，从而拓展了标准热浴引力冻结机制至非热和非平衡源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究早期宇宙亚视界尺度（sub-horizon scales）上引力非均匀性（gravitational inhomogeneities）引起的粒子产生过程，并揭示其与引力波信号之间的潜在联系。

Method: 推导出粒子产生与标量、矢量和张量度规扰动（metric perturbation）的应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）的非等时两点关联函数（unequal-time two-point function）之间的一般表达式，并通过分析该关联函数在时间型支撑（time-like support）和光型支撑（light-like support）上的行为建立联系。

Result: 粒子产额可探测关联函数的时间型支撑；在张量情况下，同一关联函数在光型支撑上的行为控制引力波发射。结果表明，在亚视界尺度上，非均匀度规背景下的粒子产生实际上可简化为引力散射（gravitational scattering），从而直接联系到标准模型热浴的引力冻结机制（gravitational freeze-in），并扩展到非热和非平衡源。该机制可有效填充引力耦合的暗扇区（dark sectors），尤其是扰动在暴胀（inflation）后不久产生时。

Conclusion: 建立了暗物质产生与随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）振幅之间的定量关系，允许将暗物质质量与引力波信号相关联，并为一阶相变（first order phase transitions）等过程中的标量和张量扰动产生粒子提供了具体分析框架。

Abstract: We continue the study of particle production from gravitational inhomogeneities in the early Universe. Focusing on sources active on sub-horizon scales, we derive general expressions relating particle production to the unequal-time two-point function of the stress-energy tensor sourcing scalar, vector and tensor metric perturbations. The resulting particle yield probes the time-like support of this correlator, and in the tensor case the same object controls gravitational wave emission when evaluated on the light-like support. This establishes a phenomenological link between dark matter production and gravitational wave signals, allowing the dark matter mass to be related to the amplitude of the stochastic gravitational wave background. Our results show that, on sub-horizon scales, particle production from inhomogeneous metric backgrounds practically reduces to gravitational scattering. This directly connects the formalism to gravitational freeze-in from the Standard Model thermal bath, while extending it to non-thermal and out of equilibrium sources. We apply the formalism to first order phase transitions and discuss the associated production from scalar and tensor perturbations. The mechanism can efficiently populate gravitationally coupled dark sectors, especially when the perturbations are generated shortly after inflation.

</details>

### [68] [Collection, characterization, and precision measurement of levitated charged nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27478)
*B. E. Kane,Joyce Coppock,Sunghyun Kim,Sarah Westgate*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用电喷雾发射（electrospray emission）生成并收集粒子；通过热运动直接成像（direct imaging of thermal motion）快速表征粒子；将粒子从收集阱转移至独立的分析阱（analysis trap）以实现更高真空与更低噪声；在高真空（p≈10^{-8} Torr）分析阱中对捕获粒子振荡幅度进行恒温控制（thermostatic control），进而长期精密测量振荡频率以推导电荷质量比（Q/M）。

Abstract: We describe apparatus and experimental procedures for high stability precision measurements of levitated nanoscale particles confined in an ion trap in high vacuum. We discuss methods for particle generation and collection using electrospray emission, for rapid characterization by direct imaging of thermal motion, and for transfer of the particle from the trap where it is collected to a separate analysis trap in order to achieve better vacuum and lower noise. In the analysis trap at high vacuum (pressure $p\simeq10^{-8}$ Torr), we employ thermostatic control of the trapped particle oscillation amplitudes, allowing long-term, precision measurements of oscillation frequencies, from which the charge to mass ratio ($Q/M$) can be deduced. Under these conditions, we achieve $Q/M$ measurement precision approaching $10^{-5}$. This sensitivity will enable, for example, investigations of the surface chemistry of $μ$m-scale levitated materials in ultra-high vacuum environments.

### [69] [Multiphoton Fingerprints of Altermagnetic Spin Splittings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27548)
*Sayed Ali Akbar Ghorashi,Andrew M. Rappe*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了多光子吸收作为平面交变磁体（altermagnets）的偏振分辨非线性光学探针，发现交变磁自旋分裂的角谐波（angular harmonic）决定了最低阶对称选择性光学吸收的阶数，并建立了区分d波、g波和i波交变磁自旋分裂的非线性光谱学层级关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为平面交变磁体（planar altermagnets）寻找超越线性响应（linear response）的直接光学指纹，以区分不同阶次（d波、g波、i波）的交变磁自旋分裂（altermagnetic spin splitting）。

Method: 采用偏振分辨的多光子吸收（polarization-resolved multiphoton absorption）作为非线性光学探针，系统研究不同阶次交变磁序（d波、g波、i波）下的光学响应，分析跃迁矩阵元（transition matrix element）中直接n光子贡献的缺失条件及其对吸收率的频率标度律（frequency scaling）的影响。

Result: 交变磁自旋分裂的角谐波（angular harmonic）决定了最低阶对称选择性光学吸收：d波序对应双光子吸收（two-photon absorption），g波序对应四光子吸收（four-photon absorption），i波序对应六光子吸收（six-photon absorption）。每种情况下存在一个与交变磁纹理的对称谐波锁定的偏振通道，其中直接n光子贡献缺失，改变了吸收率的频率标度律。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一个区分d波、g波和i波交变磁自旋分裂的非线性光谱学层级关系（hierarchy of nonlinear spectroscopic signatures），为超越线性响应识别交变磁体的对称性提供了直接光学指纹。

Abstract: We systematically investigate multiphoton absorption as a polarization-resolved nonlinear optical probe of planar altermagnets (ALMs). We show that the angular harmonic of the altermagnetic spin splitting fixes the lowest optical absorption at which a symmetry-selective response appears: two-photon absorption for $d$-wave order, four-photon absorption for $g$-wave order, and six-photon absorption for $i$-wave order. In each case, there exists a polarization channel locked to the symmetry harmonic of the altermagnetic texture in which the direct $n$-photon contribution to the transition matrix element is absent. This changes the frequency scaling of the absorption rate relative to other polarization channels and provides a direct optical fingerprint of the underlying altermagnetic harmonic. Our results establish a hierarchy of nonlinear spectroscopic signatures that distinguishes $d$-, $g$-, and $i$-wave altermagnetic spin splittings beyond linear response.

</details>


### [70] [Confined exciton polaron in MoS$_2$ on twisted-hBN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27770)
*Garima Gupta,Mayank Chhaperwal,Pankaj Kumar,Pushkar Dasika,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Archana Raja,Kausik Majumdar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验反驳了三子（trion）形成的简单静电图像，发现即使在电场阻止电荷自发重排的条件下，仍观测到带电激子发射的量子化特征。作者提出利用激子极化子（exciton polaron）的多体图像解释这一悖论，从而为区分三子与激子极化子提供了明确方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统静电图像认为三子（trion）由额外电荷诱导激子（exciton）极化并使之结合而成，但外电场（electric field）可能阻止这种电荷自发重排，从而抑制三子形成。本文旨在实验检验该假设是否成立。

Method: 在AA堆叠的扭曲六方氮化硼（t-hBN）界面印刻铁电畴（ferroelectric domains），并将其置于单层MoS₂下方，利用畴壁附近的空间变化面内电场（in-plane electric field）同时实现二维激子的局域与极化，以及自由载流子的耗尽。

Result: 观测到大幅量子化激子劈裂（quantized exciton splitting），证实激子在畴壁中被强局域。尽管极化激子的电子侧因约束势被迫靠近累积自由电子的畴区，理论上应阻止任何三子形成，但仍观察到量子化带电激子发射（quantized charged exciton emission），其能级劈裂模式与量子化激子的能级劈裂一致。

Conclusion: 该悖论无法用三子的简单静电图像解释，而需诉诸激子极化子（exciton polaron）的多体图像：导带空穴（conduction band hole）通过吸引力与极化激子及电子费米海（electron Fermi sea）结合。这一结果为明确区分三子与激子极化子提供了决定性方法。

Abstract: The simple electrostatic picture of a trion is that of an excess charge inducing an exciton polarization and binding closer (farther) to the hole (electron) side of it. Trion formation can be forbidden when such spontaneous rearrangement of charges is not allowed by the application of external perturbation, such as electric field. Here we test this hypothesis experimentally using a non-monotonic electric field. We realize this scenario by imprinting the ferroelectric domains at the AA-stacked twisted-hBN (t-hBN) interface onto a monolayer of MoS2 placed over it. The spatially varying in-plane electric field around the domain wall serves the dual purpose of (a) confining and polarizing the 2D exciton in the domain wall, and (b) depleting the free charge carriers from the domain wall. We observe a large quantized exciton splitting confirming strong exciton confinement in the domain wall. Forced by the confining potential, the electron side of the polarized exciton lies closer to the domain with accumulated free electrons, which should ideally prevent any trion formation. Contrary to the laid hypothesis, we observe signatures of quantized charged exciton emission, with an inter-level splitting that mimics the level-splitting of the quantized excitons. This paradox is explained using the many-body picture of exciton polaron, where a conduction band hole attractively binds the polarized exciton and the electron Fermi sea. The results provide a definitive way to unambiguously discern exciton polaron from trion.

</details>


### [71] [Non-Newtonian two-dimensional electron fluid in magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27788)
*P. S. Alekseev,M. A. Semina*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由局部焦耳加热（local Joule heating）导致的二维（2D）电子流体非牛顿行为（non-Newtonian behavior）机制，通过构建并求解类泊肃叶流（Poiseuille-like flow）几何下的流体动力学方程，发现电子剪切粘度（shear viscosity）是速度梯度的非单调函数，从而形成胀流型（dilatant）或假塑型（pseudoplastic）流体，并指出该非牛顿非线性效应是超高质量GaAs量子阱中观察到的非平凡微分磁阻（differential magnetoresistance）的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释二维电子流体在高电流下表现出的非平凡微分磁阻这一实验结果，并揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 构建并求解包含流体力学速度（hydrodynamic velocity）和相应温度分布（temperature profile）的流体动力学方程，针对类泊肃叶流几何进行分析。

Result: 电子剪切粘度是速度梯度的非单调函数，二维电子形成非牛顿流体（胀流型或假塑型），且该非牛顿非线性由局部焦耳加热引起。

Conclusion: 在高电流下，超高质量GaAs量子阱中的二维电子流体确实表现为非牛顿电子流体，其非平凡微分磁阻可由局部焦耳加热导致的非牛顿非线性解释。

Abstract: We predict a mechanism for the non-Newtonian behavior of a two-dimensional (2D) electron fluid due to the local Joule heating of electrons. Within this mechanism, the electron shear viscosity is a non-monotonic function of the velocity gradient. This means that 2D electrons form an unusual non-Newtonian fluid, either dilatant or pseudoplastic, depending on the flow regime. We construct and solve the hydrodynamic equations for a hydrodynamic velocity and a corresponding temperature profile for a Poiseuille-like flow geometry. We demonstrate that the considered non-Newtonian non-linearity induced by the local heating is apparently responsible for the nontrivial differential magnetoresistance observed for 2D electrons in ultra-high-quality GaAs quantum wells, so we conclude that a 2D non-Newtonian electron fluid is realized in these systems at high currents.

</details>


### [72] [Exceptional Points as Manifestations of Topological-Charge Breakdown in a Non-Hermitian Skyrmion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27810)
*Kejun Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究非厄米（non-Hermitian）磁性系统中斯格明子（skyrmion）拓扑保护的变化，发现原本单一的拓扑荷在非厄米系统中分裂为两个不同的荷，并在奇异点（exceptional point）处发生拓扑保护的分离，类似于因果响应函数在奇异点处的解析性破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，磁性斯格明子的整数拓扑荷（topological charge）被认为是拓扑保护（topological protection）的标志。论文试图回答：当磁体系引入平衡增益/损耗或PT对称各向异性而成为非厄米系统时，这种拓扑保护会发生怎样的变化。

Method: 通过构造非厄米斯格明子的双正交（biorthogonal）左右态框架，分别计算基于右态（right state）的拓扑荷和基于双正交左右对（biorthogonal left-right pair）的拓扑荷，分析它们在非赫米特变形下的行为，并研究局部生成元（local generator）奇异点处场的发散特征。

Result: 非厄米斯格明子携带两个不同的拓扑荷：仅由右态构建的荷在PT流下表现为目标球面上的吉尔伯特型弛豫（Gilbert-type relaxation），具有同伦保护（homotopy-protected）性质；而由双正交左右对构建的荷为复数，增益/损耗开启后即失去量子化（quantization），并在斯格明子赤道环上的奇异点处发散崩溃。

Conclusion: 在非厄米动力学下，斯格明子的拓扑保护不再是单一陈述：它会在奇异点处分裂。这种实空间拓扑奇异点与因果响应函数在奇异点处的解析性破坏相对应，二者是同一非厄米简并（non-Hermitian degeneracy）的不同表现。

Abstract: The integer topological charge of a magnetic skyrmion is the standard emblem of topological protection. We ask what happens to that protection when the magnet is made non-Hermitian, with balanced gain and loss or a PT-symmetric anisotropy. A non-Hermitian skyrmion turns out to carry two charges that coincide in the Hermitian limit but part ways under deformation. The charge built from the right state alone is homotopy-protected: the PT flow reduces exactly to a Gilbert-type relaxation on the target sphere, so it cannot change under smooth evolution. The charge built from the biorthogonal left-right pair is complex, loses quantization as soon as the gain/loss is turned on, and breaks down at the exceptional point of the local generator -- a ring on the skyrmion's equator, where the biorthogonal Bloch field itself diverges. Topological protection of a skyrmion is therefore not a single statement once the dynamics is non-Hermitian: it splits at an exceptional point. This is the real-space topological counterpart of the analyticity breakdown a causal response function suffers at an exceptional point, both being manifestations of the same non-Hermitian degeneracy.

</details>


### [73] [Theory of Electron Spin Resonance Scanning Tunneling Microscopy: The First Decade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27830)
*Saba Taherpour,Denis Janković,Hoang-Anh Le,Jose Reina-Galvez,Christoph Wolf*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文综述了扫描隧道显微镜中电子自旋共振（ESR-STM）技术的最新进展，讨论了电场驱动自旋共振的机制（包括海森堡交换、近藤散射和安德森杂质模型），并通过理论预测与实验观测的对比验证了电子关联、自旋交换和多体效应对ESR-STM信号的影响。此外，还介绍了相干多自旋控制、耦合电子-核自旋系统以及核自旋驱动与极化等前沿应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ESR-STM技术使得在原子尺度上研究表面磁性杂质的电子跃迁成为可能，并能以全电学方法实现自旋的光谱探测与相干操控，无需外加振荡磁场。本文旨在系统回顾该领域的最新进展，阐明电场驱动自旋共振的物理机制，并探索其在量子计算和自旋操控中的潜在应用。

Method: 综述了基于海森堡交换（Heisenberg exchange）、近藤散射（Kondo scattering）和安德森杂质模型（Anderson impurity model）的电场驱动自旋共振机制；通过理论预测与实验观测的对比，验证电子关联（electronic correlations）、自旋交换（spin exchange）和多体效应（many-body effects）在ESR-STM信号中的表现。

Result: 理论预测与实验观测一致，表明电子关联、自旋交换和多体效应在ESR-STM信号中具有可观测的特征。在相干自旋控制方面，ESR-STM能够实现扫描隧道显微镜（STM）结中的多自旋相干操控，支持多量子比特（multi-qubit）操作。此外，在耦合电子-核自旋系统中，实现了超精细分辨的ESR光谱（hyperfine-resolved ESR spectroscopy）以及核自旋的驱动与极化。

Conclusion: ESR-STM技术为原子尺度的自旋操控与量子比特操作提供了全电学的有效途径。未来有望在相干多自旋控制和耦合电子-核自旋系统方面发挥关键作用，推动基于自旋的量子信息处理与原子尺度自旋物理的发展。

Abstract: Electron spin resonance in scanning tunneling microscopy enabled the study of electronic transitions of magnetic impurities on surfaces at the atomic scale. This ESR-STM technique allows to spectroscopically probe and coherently manipulate spins using an all-electrical method without oscillating external magnetic driving fields. Here, we aim to review recent advancements in ESR-STM. We will discuss possible fundamental mechanisms by which the electric field drives spin resonance based on Heisenberg exchange, Kondo scattering, and Anderson impurity models. We validate theoretical predictions against experimental observations, to understand how electronic correlations, spin exchange, and many-body effects manifest in ESR-STM signals. After reviewing coherent spin control in the STM junction, we discuss potential applications of the ESR-STM method for coherent multi-spin control which enables multiple-qubit operations. Finally, we address recent developments in coupled electron-nuclear spin systems, including hyperfine-resolved ESR spectroscopy, and the driving and polarization of nuclear spins in ESR-STM.

</details>


### [74] [Open Nanoacoustic Resonators Based on SrTiO$_3$/YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-x}$ Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27945)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用STO/YBCO超晶格作为声学分布式布拉格反射器（distributed Bragg reflector），结合金属Ni换能器产生相干声子，通过时域布里渊散射（time-domain Brillouin scattering）进行超快光学激发与探测，并利用转移矩阵（transfer-matrix）计算声学反射率和模分布。

Result: 瞬态反射率测量显示了受限的声学动力学行为以及明确的腔共振特征，且实验结果与转移矩阵计算在声学反射率和模分布上一致。

Abstract: We report the design and experimental demonstration of an open nanophononic cavity based on a hybrid oxide superlattice composed of SrTiO$_3$ (STO) and YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-x}$ (YBCO), combined with a metallic Ni transducer for coherent phonon generation. The STO/YBCO periodic stack acts as an acoustic distributed Bragg reflector supporting confined longitudinal acoustic phonons in the sub-THz regime, while the Ni layer enables efficient ultrafast optical excitation and detection by time-domain Brillouin scattering. Transient reflectivity measurements reveal confined acoustic dynamics and a well-defined cavity resonance, in agreement with transfer-matrix calculations of acoustic reflectivity and mode profiles. These results demonstrate phonon confinement in multifunctional oxide heterostructures and establish complex oxide superlattices as a platform for hybrid nano-acoustic resonators and ultrafast phonon control of correlated electronic phases.

### [75] [Hidden valley dynamics behind vanishing circular polarization in moiré excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27963)
*Yuto Urano,Lata Chouhan,Nurul Fariha Ahmad,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Daichi Kozawa,Ryo Kitaura*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过时间分辨光致发光光谱揭示，过渡金属二硫族化物异质结中摩尔超晶格激子的时间积分圆偏振极化率近乎为零，并非源于快速的谷弛豫，而是由两个具有相反光学选择规则和不同有效衰减/去极化速率的发射通道（类A和类B）动态补偿所致。该隐藏的谷动力学行为可通过静电场连续调控，表明时间积分极化测量在多通道谷发射体中会产生假阴性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测量通常探测时间积分的谷极化（valley polarization），导致零极化状态的动力学起源一直不清楚。本文旨在阐明过渡金属二硫族化物（transition-metal dichalcogenide）异质结中电可调摩尔激子（moiré exciton）的近乎为零的稳态谷极化是否一定意味着快速的谷弛豫。

Method: 采用旋性分辨的时间分辨光致发光（helicity-resolved time-resolved photoluminescence）光谱技术，结合双通道模型（two-channel model，包含类A和类B摩尔发射通道）以及二维栅极场映射（gate-field map）方法。

Result: 观察到共旋和反旋圆偏振发射之间存在时间交叉（temporal crossing），表明旋性相反的动力学组分共存并在时间积分后相互抵消。双通道模型可重现该旋性交叉现象，且无需引入单个快速谷弛豫过程。交叉时间随静电调谐（electrostatic tuning）系统性演化，表明隐藏的谷动力学受电控。

Conclusion: 时间积分圆偏振极化率在多通道谷发射体中可能给出谷极化的假阴性指示（false-negative indication），即零稳态极化并不等同于快速谷弛豫；隐藏的谷动力学具有电可控性，为谷电子学（valleytronics）和量子光学应用提供了新的调控维度。

Abstract: Optically addressable valley degrees of freedom in transition-metal dichalcogenide heterostructures provide a powerful platform for valleytronic and quantum-optical functionalities. In moiré superlattices, interlayer excitons inherit valley-contrasting optical selection rules while acquiring long lifetimes, electric dipoles, and site-dependent optical responses. However, because conventional measurements typically probe time-integrated valley polarization, the dynamical origin of vanishing polarization has remained elusive. Here, we show that a nearly zero steady-state valley polarization in electrically tunable moiré excitons does not necessarily indicate fast valley relaxation. Helicity-resolved time-resolved photoluminescence reveals a temporal crossing between co- and cross-circularly polarized emission, indicating that helicity-opposite dynamical components coexist and compensate after time integration. A minimal two-channel model, representing A-like and B-like moiré emission channels with opposite optical selection rules and distinct effective decay/depolarization rates, reproduces the observed helicity crossing without invoking a single rapid valley relaxation process. Furthermore, two-dimensional gate-field maps show that the crossing time evolves systematically with electrostatic tuning, demonstrating that the hidden valley dynamics are electrically controllable. These results show that time-integrated circular polarization can give a false-negative indication of valley polarization in multichannel valley emitters.

</details>


### [76] [Determining Electron Beam Lateral Coherence in a Scanning Electron Microscope Using Electron Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28056)
*Evelijn Akerboom,Fatemeh Kiani,Giulia Tagliabue,Wiebke Albrecht,Joanne Etheridge,F. Javier García de Abajo,Albert Polman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在扫描电子显微镜（SEM）中开发并表征了扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）能力，利用单晶金片和单层石墨烯样品在30 keV加速电压下获得了高质量的选区电子衍射（SAED）图和会聚束电子衍射（CBED）图。通过分析波矢差为0.031/Å的双电子束干涉，提取了电子束直径5%区域内约60%的横向相干度下限，表明该相干性足以在SEM中实现量子相干的电子-光-物质相互作用实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扫描电子显微镜（SEM）中建立并验证扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）能力，以研究电子束（e-beam）在样品平面内的有效横向相干性（lateral coherence），从而拓展SEM在量子相干实验中的应用可能性。

Method: 利用单晶金片和单层石墨烯样品，在30 keV加速电压下获取选区电子衍射（SAED）图和会聚束电子衍射（CBED）图以验证系统能力；借鉴透射电子显微镜（TEM）中的技术测量电子束在SEM样品平面中的横向相干度，通过分析波矢差为0.031/Å的双电子束干涉来提取相干性下限。

Result: 成功获得了高质量的SAED图和CBED图，验证了30 keV下系统探测晶体学信息的能力。通过干涉分析，提取到电子束直径5%区域内约60%的横向相干度下限。

Conclusion: 所测得的相干性数值足以在SEM中支持量子相干的电子-光-物质相互作用（quantum-coherent electron-light-matter interaction）实验。

Abstract: We develop and characterize scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) capabilities within a scanning electron microscope (SEM) to investigate the effective lateral coherence of the electron beam (e-beam) in the specimen plane. Using single-crystalline Au flakes and a sample composed of a monolayer of graphene, we obtain high-quality selected-area electron diffraction (SAED) maps and convergent-beam electron diffraction (CBED) patterns, validating the systems ability to probe crystallographic information at an acceleration voltage of 30 keV. Building on these capabilities, we implement a method, which is adapted from techniques traditionally used in transmission electron microscopy, to measure the degree of lateral coherence of the e-beam in the specimen plane of the SEM. By analyzing interference between electrons with two different wave vectors separated by 0.031 per angstrom, we extract a lower limit for the degree of lateral coherence over 5% of the e-beam diameter of approximately 60%. These coherence values are sufficient to enable quantum-coherent electron-light-matter interaction experiments in the SEM.

</details>


### [77] [Population-Dominated Ergotropy in a Capacitively Coupled Double-Quantum-Dot Battery under 1/f Charge Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28082)
*Khalil Loukhssami,Khadija El Hawary,Sanaa Abaach,Morad El Baz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个电容耦合双量子点（double quantum dot, DQD）量子电池（quantum battery, QB）在失谐电荷噪声下的可提取功存储。通过共振微波调制隧穿耦合通道充电，噪声平均后系统展现出退相干，主导的可提取功以非被动布居分布存储，而噪声会削弱相干振幅和布居转移路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际量子电池在实验环境中不可避免地受到电荷噪声干扰，但现有研究多关注注入能量，对噪声影响下可提取功（ergotropy）的定量分析不足。本文旨在从可提取功的视角建立噪声感知的半导体量子电池充电描述框架。

Method: 将双量子点电池建模为两个具有伊辛型（Ising-type）电容耦合的相互作用电荷量子比特（charge qubits），通过隧穿耦合通道的共振微波调制进行充电；失谐涨落由带限1/f噪声频谱生成经典随机过程来模拟；对每个噪声实现进行幺正演化，再通过系综平均获得退相干效应；分析总遍历功（ergotropy）、布居与相干贡献、能量基布居、被动序违逆诊断及噪声平均态的Jensen-Shannon相干性。

Result: 共振隧穿耦合驱动在相互作用双量子点能谱中选择了主导的E0↔E3布居转移通道；可提取功主要存储在非被动布居分布中，相干作为瞬态动力学资源伴随并支持共振转移；失谐噪声同时削弱了能量基相干振幅和主导布居遍历功所依赖的布居转移路径。

Conclusion: 基于可提取功而非仅注入能量的视角，该框架为半导体量子电池的充电过程提供了噪声感知的描述，揭示了噪声对相干和布居转移的双重抑制机制。

Abstract: We investigate extractable work storage in a capacitively coupled double quantum dot (DQD) quantum battery (QB) subjected to experimentally motivated detuning charge noise. The battery is modeled as two interacting charge qubits with an Ising-type capacitive coupling and is charged by resonant microwave modulation of the tunnel coupling channel. Detuning fluctuations are introduced as classical stochastic processes generated from a band-limited 1/f noise spectrum. For each noise realization, the evolution remains unitary, whereas decoherence and loss of contrast emerge after ensemble averaging. We analyze the total ergotropy, its population and coherent contributions, the energy basis populations, a passive ordering violation diagnostic, and the Jensen-Shannon coherence of the noise-averaged state. The results show that resonant tunnel coupling driving selects a dominant E0 <-> E3 population transfer channel in the interacting DQD spectrum. The dominant extractable work is stored in non-passive population distributions, in agreement with recent population ordering interpretations of ergotropy in QBs, while coherence accompanies and supports the resonant transfer as a transient dynamical resource. Detuning noise reduces the energy basis coherence amplitude and also weakens the population transfer pathway responsible for the dominant population ergotropy. This framework provides a noise-aware description of semiconductor QB charging based on extractable work rather than on injected energy alone.

### [78] [Role of the Casimir force in the capacitive radio-frequency microelectromechanical switches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28195)
*G. L. Klimchitskaya,A. S. Korotkov,V. V. Loboda,V. M. Mostepanenko*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究分析了微机电电容式开关中圆柱形薄膜与底部电极之间由涨落引起的卡西米尔力（Casimir force）的作用。在考虑真实材料特性和表面粗糙度的条件下计算卡西米尔力，并与理想金属光滑表面的理想化结果进行了对比。结果表明，考虑真实材料属性和表面粗糙度对于获得准确的卡西米尔力至关重要；在最短间距下，卡西米尔力可能超过电力；所得结果可用于确定薄膜厚度，以确保微机械开关稳定循环工作所需的弹性恢复力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定涨落诱导的卡西米尔力在微机电电容式开关（microelectromechanical capacitive switches）中圆柱形薄膜与底部电极之间所扮演的角色，以更准确地评估其对开关性能的影响。

Method: 在计算卡西米尔力时同时考虑了薄膜与底部电极材料的真实物性（real material properties）以及表面粗糙度（surface roughness）；并将计算结果与采用理想金属（ideal metal）光滑表面理想化模型所得结果进行了比较。

Result: 考虑真实材料特性和表面粗糙度对于获得正确的卡西米尔力数值至关重要；在最短间距（薄膜与传输线接触时）下，卡西米尔力的大小可能超过电力，具体取决于工作电压（operating voltage）的数值。

Conclusion: 所获得的卡西米尔力数值可用于确定开关薄膜的厚度，从而保证微机械开关在无吸合（pull-in）情况下稳定循环工作所需的弹性恢复力（restoring elastic force）。

Abstract: We determine the role of the fluctuation-induced Casimir force acting between a membrane of cylindrical shape and a bottom electrode in microelectromechanical capacitive switches. For this purpose, the Casimir force is computed taking into account the real properties of both a membrane and a bottom electrode materials with account of surface roughness. The obtained results are compared with those found for the smooth surfaces using the idealization of ideal metal. It is shown that an account of both the real material properties and surface roughness is crucial for obtaining the correct values of the Casimir force. According to our results, at the shortest separations, when the switch membrane is in contact with the transmission line, the magnitudes of the Casimir force may exceed the magnitudes of the electric one depending on the value of the operating voltage. The obtained values of the Casimir force can be used for determining the thickness of the switch membrane, which ensures the necessary magnitude of the restoring elastic force required for a stable cyclic functioning of the micromechanical switch with no pull-in.

### [79] [Interlayer electric multipole Hall effect in twisted multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28205)
*Chengxin Xiao,Cong Xiao,Dawei Zhai,Wang Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了范德华层状材料中由层赝自旋（layer pseudospin）形成的非平凡织构，揭示了在具有时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的体系中仍能产生的层霍尔效应（layer Hall effect, LHE），包括双层中的层间电偶极霍尔效应（interlayer electric dipole Hall effect）以及多层中的电多极霍尔效应（electric multipole Hall effect）和对应的面内磁多极（in-plane magnetic multipole）。文章重点分析了镜像对称扭曲三层结构中的层间电四极霍尔效应（interlayer electric quadrupole Hall effect），并发现小转角下平移调控电流，大转角下可由单界面贡献叠加解释，从而可推广至无明确周期性的多层体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有时间反演对称性的扭曲范德华层状材料中，层赝自旋非平凡织构所导致的层霍尔效应及其物理机制，并建立从双层到多层、从有周期到无周期体系的统一理解框架。

Method: 从分析镜像对称扭曲三层结构中的层间电四极霍尔效应出发，研究不同转角（twist angle）和掺杂条件下的电流行为；在小转角下考察层间平移（interlayer translation）对层霍尔电流的调控，在大角度和低掺杂下将总电流分解为两个独立扭曲界面的贡献之和。

Result: 在小扭转角下，层间平移可以高效调控层霍尔电流的幅值；在大扭转角和低掺杂条件下，总层霍尔电流可近似为两个单独扭曲界面贡献的线性叠加，这一分解方法使大角度扭曲多层结构中各层霍尔电流的求解得以实现，即使系统不具备明确定义的周期性（well-defined periodicity）。

Conclusion: 通过分解为独立界面贡献的策略，可将层分辨霍尔电流的分析从周期性的扭曲双层推广至非周期性的扭曲多层体系，为理解和利用层霍尔效应提供了更普适的理论工具。

Abstract: Electrons in layered van der Waals materials possess a layer pseudospin characterizing their wave-function distribution among layers. In twisted structures, this pseudospin forms nontrivial textures, leading to intriguing phenomena such as the layer Hall effect (LHE), where distinct layer Hall currents flow despite the presence of time-reversal symmetry. In chiral bilayers, LHE manifests as an interlayer electric dipole Hall effect with Hall counterflows and a concomitant in-plane magnetic dipole. Multilayers host richer layer-dependent Hall currents, generating interlayer electric multipole Hall effects and in-plane magnetic multipoles. We start from exploring the interlayer electric quadrupole Hall effect in mirror-symmetric twisted trilayers. At small twist angles, interlayer translation efficiently tunes layer Hall current magnitudes. At large angles and low doping, the currents can be well accounted for by adding the contributions from the two individual twisted interfaces. This decomposition allows obtaining layer-resolved Hall currents in large-angle twisted multilayers even without well-defined periodicity.
