### [80] [Massive scalar fields in eccentric regime: Detectability and constraints from LISA observations of extreme mass-ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27429)
*Tieguang Zi,Shailesh Kumar,Jun-Kun Zhao,Bao-Min Gu,Fu-Wen Shu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了有质量标量场（massive scalar field）对极端质量比旋近（EMRI）系统在偏心轨道下动力学和引力波信号的影响，发现标量辐射可导致显著的引力波相位偏移（dephasing），且偏心度越大效应越明显；同时利用Fisher信息矩阵（FIM）分析表明，LISA探测器可对标量荷（scalar charge）和标量场质量施加有意义的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋近（EMRI）是未来空间引力波（GW）天文台的重要源，可用于检验基本场和广义相对论（GR）的偏离。本文旨在研究有质量标量场对围绕Kerr黑洞的偏心赤道EMRI动力学的影响。

Method: 在绝热旋近（adiabatic treatment）框架下，计算携带标量荷（scalar charge）的恒星质量天体同时发射标量辐射与张量引力波的相对论性流（relativistic fluxes）；通过频域中标量扰动方程求解，利用切比雪夫插值（Chebyshev interpolants）给出流的有效演化；采用Fisher信息矩阵（FIM）分析评估LISA的测量能力。

Result: 有质量标量辐射可产生显著的引力波相位偏移（dephasing），且随轨道偏心度（eccentricity）增大而增强；但标量场质量越大，标量流反而受到抑制。偏心EMRI对标量场质量具有有意义的约束能力。

Conclusion: 偏心EMRI为零质量与有质量标量场情形提供了区分手段，并为在强引力场区域检验标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor theories of gravity）提供了一条有前景的重要途径。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are among the prime sources for future space-borne gravitational wave (GW) observatories and provide a useful setting for testing the presence of fundamental fields and possible deviations from general relativity (GR) in both strong and weak gravity regimes. In this work, we study the effect of a massive scalar field on eccentric equatorial EMRI dynamics around Kerr black holes. Considering that the inspiralling stellar-mass object carries a scalar charge and emits scalar radiation together with tensor GWs, we compute the relevant relativistic fluxes within the adiabatic treatment of the inspiral. With the solution of the scalar perturbation equation in the frequency domain, the resulting fluxes are presented through the Chebyshev interpolants in order to have the efficient inspiral evolution across the parameter space considered. We quantify the impact of scalar field mass and scalar charge on the orbital evolution and GW signal through phase shifts and waveform mismatches relative to both GR and the massless-scalar scenario. We find that massive scalar radiation can generate significant GW dephasing that increases with orbital eccentricity; however, the scalar flux is suppressed as the scalar field mass is becoming larger. Using a Fisher information matrix (FIM) analysis, we estimate the ability of Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) to measure or constrain the scalar charge and scalar field mass. Our results indicate that eccentric EMRIs can place meaningful constraints on massive scalar fields and provide a promising as well as important avenue for testing scalar-tensor extensions of gravity in the region of a strong gravitational field.

</details>


### [81] [Critical collapse of vacuum spacetimes: Nakamura wave initial data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27431)
*Thomas W. Baumgarte,Carsten Gundlach,David Hilditch*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了轴对称真空引力波（axisymmetric vacuum gravitational waves）在坍缩过程中的临界现象（critical phenomena），采用基于Nakamura构造的初始数据，能够将参数微调至黑洞形成临界点略优于以往模拟，观察到近似自相似（approximately self-similar）阈值解中的额外回波（echo），但未发现精确自相似性或唯一的临界解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞形成临界现象中阈值解的结构与性质，特别是针对真空引力波坍缩场景，利用新的初始数据族以更精细地接近黑洞形成的临界点，从而观察更多自相似回波细节，并检验是否存在唯一的临界解。

Method: 采用基于爱因斯坦方程线性波解（linear wave solutions to the Einstein equations）构建的初始数据族，遵循Nakamura构造方法，将波内容编码在外曲率（extrinsic curvature）而非空间曲率（spatial curvature）中，并在满足非线性约束方程（nonlinear constraint equations）时对数据进行“修整”（dressed up），以此进行数值模拟并对参数进行微调至黑洞形成临界点。

Result: 新初始数据族能够将参数精细调节至黑洞形成临界点略优于先前模拟，从而在近似自相似阈值解中观察到并检验了额外一个回波；所有阈值解均表现出近似离散自相似性（approximately discretely self-similar），但自相似性不精确，且未发现唯一临界解的证据。

Conclusion: 模拟结果与以往研究一致：真空引力波坍缩的临界现象中存在近似离散自相似而非精确自相似的阈值解，不存在唯一的临界解；不同阈值解之间具有共同特征，包括沿极轴（poles）与赤道（equator）方向出现交替极大值（alternating maxima）。

Abstract: We report on numerical simulations of critical phenomena in the collapse of axisymmetric vacuum gravitational waves, adopting families of initial data that, to the best of our knowledge, have not been used in this context before. Like Teukolsky waves, the data are based on linear wave solutions to the Einstein equations. We follow Nakamura's construction and encode the wave content in the extrinsic curvature rather than the spatial curvature, which leads to several simplifications when the data are "dressed up" so that they satisfy the nonlinear constraint equations. We are able to fine-tune these data to the onset of black hole formation slightly better than in our previous simulations, allowing us to observe and examine one more echo in the approximately self-similar threshold solution. Our findings are consistent with earlier studies: while we find threshold solutions that are approximately discretely self-similar, the self-similarity is not exact, and we find no evidence for a unique critical solution. We discuss common features between the different threshold solutions, including the appearance of alternating maxima in the direction of the poles and the equator.

</details>


### [82] [Tidal Forces in the Presence of Torsion and Nonmetricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27433)
*Armin van de Venn,Marcelo Netz-Marzola,David Vasak,Jürgen Struckmeier*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了挠率（torsion）和非度规性（nonmetricity）如何修正度规-仿射引力（metric-affine gravity）中的潮汐加速度，推导了推广的偏离方程，并在弱场非相对论极限下分析了后黎曼（post-Riemannian）修正对潮汐张量的贡献，指出潮汐加速度可作为探测后黎曼时空特征的系统性途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索挠率和非度规性在度规-仿射引力理论中对潮汐加速度的具体修正机制，并评估未来通过潮汐测量约束后黎曼时空特征的可能性。

Method: 在度规-仿射几何框架下推导投影偏离方程（projected deviation equation），将其推广至包含挠率和非度规性的情形；在弱场非相对论极限下将潮汐加速度分解为牛顿项（Newtonian contribution）与线性后黎曼修正项；利用不可约洛伦兹分量（irreducible Lorentz components）分解挠率和非度规性，识别其在潮汐张量（tidal tensor）中的对应特征。

Result: 潮汐加速度在弱场非相对论极限下可分离为通常的牛顿贡献和由挠率、非度规性驱动的线性后黎曼修正；通过不可约洛伦兹分解可以区分不同类型的后黎曼贡献在潮汐张量中的特征信号；未来直接的潮汐测量有望转化为对后黎曼潮汐贡献的基准约束（benchmark bounds）。

Conclusion: 潮汐加速度为系统性地探测后黎曼时空特征提供了一条可行途径，未来可通过敏感于仿射联络（affine connection）的探针动力学（probe dynamics）实现直接观测约束。

Abstract: This work investigates how torsion and nonmetricity modify tidal accelerations in metric-affine gravity. We derive a projected deviation equation that generalizes the standard geodesic deviation equation to metric-affine geometry, and apply it to the relative acceleration of neighboring autoparallels in the weak-field, nonrelativistic limit. In this regime, the tidal acceleration separates into the usual Newtonian contribution and linear post-Riemannian corrections sourced by torsion and non-metricity. By decomposing torsion and nonmetricity into their irreducible Lorentz components, we identify the corresponding signatures in the tidal tensor and discuss to what extent these contributions can be distinguished. We then show how future direct tidal measurements could be translated into benchmark bounds on post-Riemannian tidal contributions, assuming probe dynamics sensitive to the affine connection. Our results suggest that the tidal acceleration may provide a systematic route toward probing post-Riemannian spacetime features in the future.

### [83] [Einstein-aether Elliptic Charges and the First Law of Asymptotically AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27437)
*Walter Arata,Moustafa Ismail,Stefano Liberati,Luke Martin,David Mattingly,Giulio Neri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-以太理论（Einstein-aether theory）中，针对静态球对称渐近 AdS 时空中的普适视界（universal horizon），发现了一个由以太加速度（aether acceleration）生成的新对称性，并推导出相应的守恒流与荷。该结果与 Hořava-Lifshitz 引力中的椭圆荷（elliptic charge）机制对偶，澄清了渐近以太对齐（asymptotic aether alignment）在热力学中的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 $c_{14}=0$ 的静态球对称渐近 AdS 扇区中，普适视界的第一定律（first law）在以太与类时 Killing 矢量在无穷远处未对齐时包含一个额外项。该额外项在 Hořava-Lifshitz 引力中已被解释为与 khronon 重参数化（khronon reparameterization）相关的椭圆荷贡献，但在爱因斯坦-以太理论中此前缺乏对应的解释。

Method: 在相同扇区中，作者发现约化作用量（reduced action）存在一个此前未被识别的对称性，由形如 $δu^a=f a^a$ 的无穷小变换生成，其中 $a^a$ 为以太加速度，$f$ 满足椭圆型约束（elliptic constraint）。由此推导出对应的守恒流（conserved current）与荷（charge）。

Result: 推导了与上述对称性关联的守恒流与荷；证明对齐极限（aligned limit）可自然地解释为该以太荷贡献为零的系综（ensemble）。

Conclusion: 该结果为爱因斯坦-以太理论提供了 Hořava-Lifshitz 引力中椭圆荷机制的对应物，并阐明了渐近以太对齐在热力学中的意义。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic role of asymptotic aether alignment for universal horizons in Einstein-aether theory. In the static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically AdS sector with $c_{14}=0$, the known first law for universal horizons contains an additional term whenever the aether is misaligned with the timelike Killing vector at infinity. While this term has recently been interpreted in Hořava--Lifshitz gravity as the contribution of an elliptic charge associated with khronon reparameterizations, no corresponding explanation was available in Einstein-aether theory. We show that, in the same sector, Einstein-aether theory possesses a previously unidentified symmetry of the reduced action, generated by infinitesimal transformations of the form $δu^a=f a^a$, where $a^a$ is the aether acceleration and $f$ obeys an elliptic constraint. We derive the associated current and charge, and show that the aligned limit is naturally interpreted as the ensemble in which this aether-charge contribution vanishes. This provides the Einstein-aether counterpart of the elliptic-charge mechanism in Hořava--Lifshitz gravity and clarifies the thermodynamic significance of asymptotic aether alignment.

</details>


### [84] [The crust of dark-matter admixed neutron stars: bulk properties and torsional oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27456)
*Jiayi Zhang,Hector O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了暗物质混合中子星（dark-matter-admixed neutron stars, DANSs）的双流体平衡模型，发现暗物质（DM）在特定分布下可使中子星壳层厚度减少最多12%，并导致扭转振荡频率整体升高；通过对比电子屏蔽效应，揭示暗物质与重子物质微物理效应之间的简并性可以在部分参数空间被打破，从而为通过扭转振荡推断暗物质核心的存在提供可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质（dark matter, DM）对中子星（neutron star, NS）壳层结构及其扭转振荡（torsional crust oscillations）谱的影响，并评估扭转振荡能否作为探测暗物质核心存在的手段。

Method: 采用双流体平衡解构造，重子物质与暗物质仅通过引力相互作用；重子物质使用统一核物态方程（unified nuclear equation of state），暗物质使用具有排斥自相互作用的费米子物态方程（fermionic equation of state）；在相对论Cowling近似下推导壳层扭转振荡模方程。

Result: 固定总引力质量和暗物质质量分数时，暗物质使壳层厚度减小；暗物质分布超出重子表面时影响可忽略，而暗物质集中于星体内部（“暗核心”）时壳层厚度最多减少12%；推导的近似解析公式与数值计算在最佳情况下误差小于1%；扭转振荡频率整体高于纯重子中子星，频率最大偏移出现在壳层厚度减少最多的参数空间；暗物质与电子屏蔽（electron screening）的简并性在部分参数空间可被打破。

Conclusion: 若扭转振荡能被观测到，其结果可用于推断大质量中子星内部是否存在暗物质核心。

Abstract: We study how dark matter (DM) impacts the crust and the spectrum of torsional crust oscillations of dark-matter-admixed neutron stars (DANSs). We construct two-fluid equilibrium solutions wherein baryonic and DM interact gravitationally only, adopting a unified nuclear equation of state for the former and a fermionic equation of state with repulsive self-interaction for the latter. At fixed total gravitational mass and DM mass fraction, we find that DM reduces the crust thickness in comparison to pure baryonic-matter neutron stars (NSs). The thinning of the crust is negligible when most of the DM distribution extends beyond the star's baryonic surface. However, the crust thickness can decrease by as much as 12% when the DM distribution is within the star's baryonic surface, i.e., when the star has a "dark core." We support these results by deriving approximate analytical formulas for the crust thickness that agree with our numerical calculations at the sub-percent level in best case scenarios. Next, we derive the equation that describes crustal torsional modes of DANSs in the relativistic Cowling approximation. We find that the oscillation frequencies are in general higher than those of a comparable pure baryonic-matter NS, with the largest frequency shifts happening in the same parameter space where the crust thickness decreases the most. Moreover, we study the degeneracy between DM and baryonic-crustal microphysics effects on these modes. As an example, we study electron screening, which softens the crust's shear modulus, thus decreasing the frequencies. We find that the degeneracy between the competing effects of DM and electron screening can be broken in some regions of the parameter space we explored. Should they be measured, our results suggest that torsional oscillations could be used to infer the existence of a DM core within massive NSs. (Abridged)

</details>


### [85] [Determination of the metric of a Schwarzschild black hole surrounded by a halo of dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27482)
*M. Castillo Alarcón,Leonel Bixano,I. A. Sarmiento-Alvarado,Claudio Salas-Perez,Tonatiuh Matos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的方法来分析由史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）和各向异性流体暗物质晕（dark matter halo）组成的系统结构，确保了该度规是爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）的精确解。数值结果和解析证明均显示时间与径向度规函数满足近似倒数关系 $A(r)B(r) = 1 + \mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$，并且通过Darmois-Israel规则实现了内部黑洞与外部暗物质晕的光滑连接。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自首张黑洞图像成功获取以来，黑洞被暗物质晕（dark matter halo）包围的系统引起了广泛关注。本文旨在提出一种新颖方法，精确分析由史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）和各向异性流体暗物质晕构成的复合系统结构，并确保该度规是爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）的精确解。

Method: 采用一种新颖方法，将暗物质晕建模为各向异性流体（anisotropic fluid），并构造一个满足爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）的精确度规解。通过数值计算分析时间度规函数 $A(r)$ 与径向度规函数 $B(r)$ 之间的关系，并进行解析证明加以验证。最后，使用正则的Darmois-Israel连接规则（Darmois-Israel junction）检验内部史瓦西区域与外部暗物质晕的光滑衔接。

Result: 数值结果表明，时间度规函数 $A(r)$ 与径向度规函数 $B(r)$ 保持近似倒数关系 $A(r) \approx 1/B(r)$。解析证明进一步确认二者满足 $A(r)B(r) = 1 + \mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$，与数值结果高度一致。爱因斯坦方程表明，乘积 $A(r)B(r)$ 的变化由因子 $\varepsilon_h = \frac{8\pi G \rho_0 r_0^2}{c^2}$ 控制。此外，内部史瓦西黑洞区域与外部暗物质晕可通过正则的Darmois-Israel连接实现光滑衔接，不产生任何薄壳曲率阶跃（thin-shell curvature steps）。

Conclusion: 本文成功实现了史瓦西黑洞与各向异性暗物质晕复合系统的精确度规解，证实了时间与径向度规函数之间的近似倒数关系，且该关系由参数 $\varepsilon_h$ 控制。同时，通过正则的Darmois-Israel连接实现了内部黑洞与外部暗物质晕的光滑拼接，无需引入薄壳奇异性，为研究黑洞与暗物质相互作用提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Following the landmark acquisition of the first image of a black hole, systems comprising a black hole enveloped by a dark matter halo have have attracted considerable attention. This work implements a novel method to analyze the structure of a system composed of a Schwarzschild black hole and a dark matter halo modeled as an anisotropic fluid, while ensuring that the proposed metric constitutes an exact solution of the Einstein field equations. Numerical results show that the connection between the temporal and radial metric functions preserves an inverse relationship, namely $A(r) \approx 1/B(r)$. Furthermore, we analytically demonstrate that the resulting functions satisfy $A(r)B(r) = 1 + \mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$, in excellent agreement with the numerical findings. In addition, the Einstein equations imply that the variation of the product $A(r)B(r)$ is governed by the factor $\varepsilon_h=\frac{8πGρ_0r_0^2}{c^2}$. Finally, we show that the interior Schwarzschild region and the exterior dark matter halo can be joined smoothly via a regular Darmois-Israel junction, without generating any thin-shell curvature steps.

### [86] [Dynamics of Relativistic Binaries in Structured and Stochastic Environments: A Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27526)
*Lorenz Zwick,Conor Dyson,Brian C. Seymour,János Takátsy,Johan Samsing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为拉格朗日-傅里叶-汉森（Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen）的统一框架，用于刻画引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）驱动下相对论性双星系统在环境中受到的非真空扰动，将环境效应简化为基于滚动平均窗口的共振频谱投影，并通过两个代表性天体物理场景展示了其实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波参数估计（parameter estimation）研究中，需要准确描述非真空环境对相对论性双星的扰动效应，但目前缺乏一个能够统一处理光滑、结构化及随机扰动的通用框架，且现有现象学模型与真实环境双星模型之间存在差距。

Method: 将双星运动受到的扰动效应约化为定义在滚动平均窗口（rolling averaging window）上的共振频谱投影（resonant spectral projection），权重由汉森系数（Hansen coefficients）给出；结合分析模型或数值模拟，建立识别和评估动力学响应（dynamical response）的实用判据；最终导出一组耦合常微分方程（ODEs），用于捕获轨道元素的epi-周期、拱点（apsidal）和节点（nodal）共振，并一致性地纳入辐射反作用（radiation reaction）的反馈。

Result: 在两种代表性天体物理场景中验证了框架的实用性：一是处于变化潮汐场（variable tidal field）中的致密双星，二是在吸积盘（accretion disk）中的极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral, EMRI）。该框架可在粗时间网格上高效求解。

Conclusion: 所提出的拉格朗日-傅里叶-汉森框架（Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen framework）可作为统一工具，用于建模偏心（eccentric）和进动（precessing）双星引力波模板中的环境效应，特别有助于弥合现象学预设与真实环境双星模型之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: We develop a general framework to characterize non-vacuum perturbations to relativistic binaries in the gravitational-wave (GW) driven regime, for use in GW parameter estimation studies. The effect of smooth, structured and stochastic perturbations to the binary's motion is reduced to a resonant spectral projection defined on a rolling averaging window, with weights given by Hansen coefficients. This is combined with practical criteria for identifying and evaluating the corresponding dynamical response to perturbations, starting from either analytical models or numerical simulations of binaries in environments. The result is a set of coupled ODEs for the orbital elements that capture epi-cyclic, apsidal and nodal resonances, consistently incorporate feedback from radiation reaction and can be solved efficiently on a coarse time grid. We demonstrate the practical application of the framework in two representative astrophysical scenarios: a compact binary in a variable tidal field and an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral in an accretion disk. We propose the Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen framework as a unified tool for modeling environmental effects in GW templates for eccentric and precessing binary sources, and particularly for bridging the gap between phenomenological prescriptions and realistic models of binaries in environments.

</details>


### [87] [Geodesic Focusing Conditions in $f(Q)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27532)
*Chao-Qiang Geng,Chunhui Liu,Ling-Wei Luo,Jianhui Qiu*

TL;DR: 本文在对称远程平行几何（symmetric teleparallel geometry, STG）框架下研究了测地偏离方程与修正的Raychaudhuri方程，分析了$f(Q)$引力中的聚焦条件，并将其应用于平坦FLRW背景，得出了三种STG连接分支下的有效能量-动量迹及物质含量约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在将经典广义相对论中的Raychaudhuri方程推广至对称远程平行几何（STG）及$f(Q)$引力理论，探讨该理论中引力聚焦（focusing）的条件及其与物质源的关系。

Method: 在对称远程平行几何（STG）中推导测地偏离方程，基于Weyl型非度规性（nonmetricity）假设，在$f(Q)$引力框架下沿类时测地汇（geodesic congruence）分析修正的Raychaudhuri方程，并将模型依赖项归入有效能量-动量迹$T_{\mathrm{eff}}$。

Result: 得到的Raychaudhuri方程包含物质源贡献项，聚焦条件非自动满足，需满足不等式$T \leq T_{\mathrm{eff}}$。在平坦FLRW背景下的三种STG连接分支中，分别推导了有效迹$T_{\mathrm{eff}}$及对应的物质含量和连接函数约束。

Conclusion: 与广义相对论不同，$f(Q)$引力中的聚焦并非自动成立，需通过有效能量-动量迹来施加聚焦条件；该条件在FLRW背景的不同STG连接分支下对物质内容和连接函数给出具体限制。

Abstract: We study the geodesic deviation equation in symmetric teleparallel geometry (STG), where the relative acceleration is defined with respect to the STG connection. We analyze the modified Raychaudhuri equation along a geodesic congruence in $f(Q)$ gravity under the Weyl-type nonmetricity ansatz. In contrast to the purely geometrical Raychaudhuri equation obtained in general metric-affine settings, the equation derived here contains matter-source contributions through the trace equation of $f(Q)$ gravity. Different from general relativity, focusing in $f(Q)$ gravity is not automatic, and one must impose an appropriate focusing condition. We collect the model-dependent terms in the modified Raychaudhuri equation into an effective energy-momentum trace $T_{\mathrm{eff}}$, so that the focusing condition can be written as the inequality $T\leq T_{\mathrm{eff}}$, where $T$ is the trace of the matter energy-momentum tensor. We also apply this condition to a flat Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker background. The homogeneous and isotropic STG connection admits three branches, each characterized by a single connection function $γ_i$, with $i=1,2,3$. In the symmetric teleparallel equivalent of general relativity, we obtain the corresponding effective traces and derive the resulting constraints on the matter content and the connection functions in each branch.

Method: 本文采用光学反馈（optical feedback）控制这一新型独立范式来抑制参量不稳定性（parametric instability），并在全尺寸引力波探测器上进行了首次实验验证。

Optical feedback offers a novel independent paradigm to mitigate parametric instability. In this Letter, we report the first demonstration of optical feedback control in a full-scale gravitational wave detector. We successfully suppressed an unstable mode at 10.428 kHz, reducing the parametric gain from R = 2 to R < 0.02. This work validates optical feedback control as an effective mitigation scheme for kilometre-scale interferometric gravitational-wave detectors, providing an effective strategy to allow detectors to reach the megawatt level.

### [89] [Can a regular black hole be observationally distinguished from singular black holes as spinning lens partner in PSR-BH binaries?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27730)
*G. Y. Tuleganova,R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,K. K. Nandi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分析光线到达时间差（TOA）诊断旋转透镜的参考系拖拽效应，理论上研究了规则黑洞与奇异黑洞在薄透镜近似下能否被观测区分，结论是在第三阶及以上小量级上存在差异，因此无法通过当前观测手段区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答标题中提出的问题，即能否通过光线到达时间差（time of arrival, TOA）观测区分旋转规则黑洞与奇异黑洞，并检验旋转透镜引起的参考系拖拽（frame dragging）效应。

Method: 提出一种新型诊断方法：测量从透镜后方光源同时发出、分别经过旋转透镜两侧到达观测者的两条光线的到达时间差（TOA）。以带电规则（regular）Ayón-Beato–García黑洞为旋转透镜，在脉冲星-黑洞双星（PSR-BH binary）系统中与奇异（singular）Kerr-Newman和Kerr黑洞进行理论对比，并给出数值估计。

Result: 两个典型双星透镜系统的数值估算显示，在零阶近似下TOA可达微秒（μsec）量级，具有可测量性。但在薄透镜近似下，规则黑洞与奇异黑洞的TOA预测差异仅出现在第三阶或更高阶小量中。

Conclusion: 尽管规则黑洞与奇异黑洞之间存在显著的定性差异，但基于当前光线到达时间差（TOA）的薄透镜近似分析，两者在观测上无法被区分。

Abstract: To answer the question posed in the title, we consider a novel diagnostic, viz., the difference in the times of arrival (TOA) at the observer of two light rays that simultaneously emanate from a source behind a spinning lens and pass by either side of the lens to reach the observer. This is completely different from the usual Shapiro gravitational time delay, where only one onward light ray is reflected back to the observer. The TOA essentially samples the frame dragging caused by the spinning lens, apart from other lens parameters. Assuming a charged \textit{regular} Ayón-Beato and García black hole as the spinning lens partner in some typical astrophysical PSR-BH binaries, which provide the best laboratory for testing the TOA effect, we theoretically study how the prediction depends on the gyromagnetic ratio $\left(Q/M\right)$ and how it compares with those when the role of spinning lens partner is played by the centrally \textit{singular} Kerr-Newman and Kerr black holes. The numerical estimates for two illustrative binary lens systems show $μ$sec level delay at the zeroth order, which should be measurable. However, the TOA predictions under thin-lens approximation are shown to differ only at third or higher orders of smallness indicating that the regular and singular black holes \textit{cannot} be observationally distinguished despite significant qualitative differences existing among them.

### [90] [A Lagrangian formulation for Rastall gravity and a covariant formulation for unimodular gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27761)
*Juilson A. P. Paiva,Julio C. Fabris,Vilson T. Zanchin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非守恒引力模型的拉格朗日表述（Lagrangian formulation），通过引入与里奇曲率标量梯度（gradient of the Ricci curvature scalar）耦合的任意矢量场，在Palatini变分框架下推导出场方程，并在特定条件下还原为Rastall引力和幺模引力（unimodular gravity）模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Rastall引力这种能量-动量张量不守恒的非保守引力模型提供一个协变的拉格朗日表述，并同时给出幺模引力的新拉格朗日表述，弥补以往这些模型缺乏作用量原理支持的不足。

Method: 在弯曲时空中引入一个与里奇曲率标量梯度耦合的任意矢量场；分别采用Palatini变分方法（连接与度规张量独立处理）和标准度规变分方法推导场方程，并通过对该矢量场施加不同物理条件使得场方程分别退化为Rastall引力和幺模引力。

Result: 在Palatini框架下，该矢量场决定了流形几何是Weyl几何还是黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）；施加特定物理条件后场方程分别还原为Rastall引力与幺模引力；标准度规变分方法在适当条件下也能恢复相同的模型。

Conclusion: 核心成果是为Rastall引力推导出了协变的拉格朗日表述，并为幺模引力提供了一种新的拉格朗日表述。

Abstract: We propose a Lagrangian formulation for a non-conservative gravity model in which the divergence of the energy-momentum tensor in curved spacetime does not vanish. This is accomplished by introducing an arbitrary vector field that couples with the gradient of the Ricci curvature scalar. We first derive the field equations using the Palatini variational approach. Because the connection and the metric tensor are independent in the Palatini framework, the auxiliary vector field dictates whether the manifold geometry is Weyl or Riemannian. By assuming certain physically reasonable conditions on this vector field, the resulting field equations reduce to those of Rastall gravity. Furthermore, slightly different conditions on the vector field furnish unimodular gravity. For comparison, we also employ the standard metric variational approach to obtain the field equations, demonstrating that the same models can be recovered under appropriate conditions. Our key results are the derivation of a covariant Lagrangian formulation for Rastall gravity and a new Lagrangian formulation for unimodular gravity.

### [91] [Bounds on the radius of black hole shadows in n-dimensional Einstein gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27795)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对n维（n≥4）爱因斯坦引力中静态、球对称、渐近平坦的黑洞，在物质场满足能量条件的前提下，推导了阴影半径的模型无关下界和上界，并证明其由真空Schwarzschild-Tangherlini黑洞饱和，从而将四维阴影界限推广到任意维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞阴影由最外层不稳定零测地线（光子球）决定，是探测强场引力的直接探针。现有四维界限已被建立，但尚无任意维度下的模型无关界限，因此需要在更高维框架下推广这些约束。

Method: 在n维（n≥4）爱因斯坦引力中，考虑静态、球对称、渐近平坦黑洞，并假设物质场满足弱能量条件（Weak Energy Condition, WEC）以及强能量条件（Strong Energy Condition, SEC）与渐近衰减条件。通过几何分析推导阴影半径r_sh的解析不等式。

Result: 在WEC下，证明下界r_sh ≥ [(n-1)/2]^{1/(n-3)} √[(n-1)/(n-3)] r_H（r_H为视界半径）；在WEC、SEC及渐近衰减条件下，证明上界r_sh ≤ √[(n-1)/(n-3)] [(n-1)M]^{1/(n-3)}（M为ADM质量）。这些界限由真空Schwarzschild-Tangherlini黑洞饱和。

Conclusion: 研究将四维黑洞阴影界限推广到任意维度，为高维黑洞时空的可观测阴影提供了模型无关的几何约束。

Abstract: The dark shadow cast by a black hole, determined by the outermost unstable null circular geodesics (the photon sphere), provides a direct probe of strong-field gravity. In this work, we derive model-independent lower and upper bounds on the shadow radius $r_{\mathrm{sh}}$ for static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat black holes in $n$-dimensional ($n\ge 4$) Einstein gravity, supported by an anisotropic matter field. For the lower bound, assuming the matter satisfies the Weak Energy Condition (WEC), we prove $r_{\mathrm{sh}}\geq \bigl(\frac{n-1}{2}\bigr)^{\frac{1}{n-3}}\sqrt{\frac{n-1}{n-3}}\,r_H$, where $r_H$ is the horizon radius. For the upper bound, under the WEC and the Strong Energy Condition (SEC), together with an asymptotic decay condition on the matter fields, we prove $r_{\mathrm{sh}}\leq\sqrt{\frac{n-1}{n-3}}\bigl[(n-1)M\bigr]^{\frac{1}{n-3}}$, where $M$ is the ADM mass. These results reduce to the known four-dimensional bounds and are saturated by the vacuum Schwarzschild-Tangherlini black hole. Our results generalize the four-dimensional shadow bounds to an arbitrary number of dimensions and provide model-independent geometric constraints on the observable shadow of higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes.

</details>


### [92] [New interpretation of the Minkowski limit of $R^2$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27799)
*Valerio Faraoni,Luca Gallerani,Alain Maltais-Gosselin,Santiago Novoa-Cattivelli,Uri Gorman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor gravity）与Eckart相对论耗散流体之间的热类比，重新解释了纯$f(R)=R^2$引力在闵可夫斯基极限（Minkowski limit）下发散的问题，指出该极限对应有效“引力温度”发散，从而将强耦合问题（strong coupling problem）重新表述为热奇点（thermal singularity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有理论表明纯$R^2$引力的闵可夫斯基极限不成立，但此前缺乏对这一现象的深层物理解释。本研究旨在利用热类比框架，提供一种新的、物理直观的理解途径。

Method: 采用近期提出的标量-张量引力与Eckart相对论耗散流体之间的热学类比理论框架，分析$f(R)=R^2$引力在趋近闵可夫斯基背景时的行为。

Result: 趋近闵可夫斯基背景时，有效“引力温度”发散；$R^2$引力并非恢复为广义相对论（General Relativity），而是无限远离广义相对论。

Conclusion: 强耦合问题可被自然地重新解释为热奇点；该热类比视角为理解纯$R^2$引力与完整Starobinsky理论（$f(R)=R+\alpha R^2$）在闵可夫斯基极限下的定性差异提供了统一且物理的阐释。

Abstract: It is well-established that the Minkowski limit of pure $f(R)=R^2$ gravity breaks down, unlike that of full Starobinsky theory $f(R)=R+αR^2$. We provide a novel interpretation of this phenomenon using the recent thermal analogy between scalar-tensor gravity and Eckart's relativistic dissipative fluids. In this framework, we show that approaching the Minkowski background corresponds to a diverging effective ``gravitational temperature''. This perspective naturally rephrases the strong coupling problem as a thermal singularity, demonstrating that $R^2$ gravity departs infinitely far from General Relativity rather than recovering it.

### [93] [Testing generalized spacetimes for black holes using the Hod function representation of the hoop conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27857)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,G. M. Garipova,R. R. Volotskova,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文检验了Thorne提出的环猜想（hoop conjecture）在最近文献中构建的一类带有任意指数并耦合非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）的规则球对称静态黑洞中的有效性。研究发现，若仅使用渐近质量$M_{\infty}$，环猜想可能被违反；但采用Hod建议的质量函数（即Hod函数）后，该猜想在该类广义时空中得到保护，从而支持这些解作为黑洞。然而，存在包括违反猜想在内的因素，反对将这一“新”类解视为黑洞。最后，论证了猜想中的Hod质量$M(r\leq R)$正是广义相对论中Misner-Sharp几何拟局部质量（quasilocal mass）$m(r\leq R)$的物质对应物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Thorne环猜想在最近构建的一类带有任意指数并耦合非线性电动力学的规则球对称静态黑洞解中是否成立，并澄清Hod函数与广义相对论中Misner-Sharp拟局部质量之间的对应关系。

Method: 基于文献中已构建的广义规则球对称静态黑洞解，分别使用渐近质量$M_{\infty}$和Hod建议的质量函数（Hod函数）检验环猜想的成立与否，并对比Hod质量与Misner-Sharp拟局部质量。

Result: 仅使用渐近质量$M_{\infty}$时环猜想可能被违反；但采用Hod函数后，环猜想在该类广义时空中得到保护，支持这些解作为黑洞。然而，存在包括违反猜想在内的因素反对该“新”类解成为黑洞。Hod质量$M(r\leq R)$恰好是Misner-Sharp几何拟局部质量$m(r\leq R)$的物质对应物。

Conclusion: 基于Hod函数得出的任何结论都严格是广义相对论（general relativity）的结论；Hod函数为检验任意静态时空是否为黑洞提供了有效判据。

Abstract: The hoop conjecture, due to Thorne, is a fundamental aspect of black holes in classical general relativity. Recently, generalized classes of regular spherically symmetric static black holes with arbitrary exponents coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics have been constructed in the literature. The conjecture in those spacetimes could be violated if only the asymptotic mass $M_{\infty}$ is used. To avoid such violations, Hod earlier suggested the appropriate mass function and stated the conjecture in terms of what we call the Hod function. The conjecture can then be applied to any given static spacetime to test whether or not it represents black holes. It is shown here that the conjecture is protected in the above constructed class of generalized spacetimes thus supporting them as black holes. However, it is argued that there are factors, including violation of the conjecture, that militate against the proposed \textit{new} class of solutions to be qualifying as black holes. Finally, we exemplify that the Hod mass $M(r\leq R)$ in the conjecture is exactly the \textit{matter} counterpart of the Misner-Sharp \textit{geometrical} quasilocal mass $m(r\leq R)$ of general relativity. Thus any conclusion based on Hod function is strictly a conclusion of general relativity.

*Maria Alberti,Noa Zilberman,Marc Casals,Adrian C. Ottewill*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文计算了克尔黑洞内视界附近无质量实标量场（具有一般曲率耦合常数ξ）的⟨Φ̂²⟩_ren及能量流⟨T_uu⟩_ren和⟨T_vv⟩_ren，采用Unruh态和态减除重正化方法，发现⟨Φ̂²⟩_ren在趋近内视界时呈现环降相（频率为经典拟正则模频率的两倍）后接反幂律尾巴（r_*^{-2ℓ-3}）的行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: ⟨Φ̂²⟩_ren在克尔内视界附近展现出与经典黑洞外部相似的环降-幂律尾结构，但频率加倍且坐标替换后幂律形式对应，表明内视界附近量子场的行为存在丰富的拟正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）特征。

Abstract: We compute $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ as well as the energy fluxes $\langle \hat{T}_{uu}\rangle_\text{ren}$ and $\langle \hat{T}_{vv}\rangle_\text{ren}$ (where $u$ and $v$ are the standard Eddington-Finkelstein coordinates) associated with a quantum massless real scalar field $\hatΦ$, with a general curvature coupling constant $ξ$, near the inner horizon (IH) of a Kerr black hole, along the axis of rotation. The quantum field is in the Unruh state, corresponding to an evaporating black hole. We renormalize these quantities by the state-subtraction method. We drop the assumption of minimal coupling to the curvature, thereby generalizing the results of arXiv:2203.08502 for the fluxes at the IH. This requires understanding the asymptotic behavior of $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ neat the IH. State subtraction allows us to push the computation of $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ along the axis of rotation in the Kerr interior in arXiv:2409.17464 deeper into the near-IH region, exposing their final asymptotic behavior on approaching the IH. For $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ (a $ξ$-independent quantity in the Kerr case), we find that the approach to its finite asymptotic IH value is given, per $\ell$-mode, by a ringdown phase (namely exponentially damped oscillations), followed by an inverse-power tail, both in the tortoise coordinate $r_{*}$ (which diverges at the IH). Interestingly, in the regime where the ringing dominates, the ringing's complex frequencies are (numerically) found to match twice the well-known classical quasinormal-mode frequencies in Kerr, and the inverse-power tails are found to be $r_{*}^{-2\ell-3}$ (resembling Price's law in the classical black hole exterior, upon replacement $t\to r_*$). ### [95] [Comparing accretion disk profiles of Bogush-Galt'sov naked singularity and Kerr black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27877)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Novikov-Thorne薄吸积盘模型，对Bogush和Gal'tsov近期提出的带标量电荷σ的新型自旋裸奇点（BG裸奇点）进行吸积过程的理论分析，研究其辐射转换效率ε和发射率轮廓（emissivity profiles）的特征。

Result: (1) BG裸奇点的辐射转换效率ε与标量荷σ无关；(2) BG裸奇点发射率轮廓的最大值随a、σ增大以及√(-g)相对收缩而向内盘ISCO边界r=r_{ms}移动，峰值显著大于Kerr黑洞，最大可达Kerr黑洞的10⁵倍。所有效应均以定量表格形式给出。

Abstract: It is well known that the Einstein-scalar system of general relativity can in principle yield non-unique exact spinning naked singularities, which lead to unique Kerr black hole when the scalar field is switched off. It is a challenging task to observationally distinguish these two types of objects. Since accretion process could be a viable diagnostic for this distinction, the purpose of the present work is to explore whether there could be features in the accretion profiles distinguishing the singularity from a Kerr black hole. Here we study the Novikov-Thorne thin accretion to a \textit{new} spinning naked singularity with a scalar charge $σ$ recently reported by Bogush and Gal'tsov (BG). Our study reveals that: (1) The conversion efficiency $ε$ of the BG naked singularity is \textit{independent} of $σ$ and (2) The maxima of emissivity profiles for the BG singularity tend to shift towards the inner disk ISCO boundary $r=r_{ms}$ and peak at a value significantly larger than those of a Kerr black hole with the increase of $a$, $σ$ and relative shrinking of $\sqrt{-g}$. All these effects are \textit{quantitatively} tabulated, which reveal, for instance, that the flux from the naked singularity could be as high as $10^{5}$ times larger than that of a Kerr black hole. Since these distinguishing features are known to be shared also by other models of naked singularity, it is tempting to speculate that such behavior could be hallmark of naked singularities.

### [96] [Superradiant Instability and Two Classes of Scalar Clouds around Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27958)
*Hengyu Xu,Haowei Chen,Shao-Jun Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞周围带电有质量标量场的动力学，通过将Klein-Gordon方程映射为类薛定谔（Schrödinger）形式并采用匹配渐近展开，发现磁场抑制了超辐射不稳定性（superradiant instability），并识别出两类不同的束缚态标量云（scalar clouds）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解磁场对黑洞超辐射不稳定性的影响，并探索磁化天体物理环境中是否存在比标准孤立黑洞更丰富的玻色子（bosonic）配置。

Method: 将Klein-Gordon方程映射为一维类薛定谔方程，并采用匹配渐近展开（matched asymptotic expansions）方法进行解析分析，辅以精确数值积分验证空间结构。

Result: 外部磁场在特定频率带内将视界处的物理边界条件从传播态转变为纯指数衰减态，使耗散严格为零（$\text{Im}(ω) = 0$），从而抑制超辐射不稳定性。系统支持两类束缚态：传统的同步标量云（Type-I）和新发现的在事件视界处指数衰减的标量云（Type-II）。

Conclusion: 磁化天体物理环境可以支持比标准孤立黑洞丰富得多的玻色子束缚态构型。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of a charged massive scalar field around Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson Black Holes. By mapping the Klein-Gordon equation into a one-dimensional Schrödinger-like form and employing matched asymptotic expansions, we unveil the magnetic-field-induced quenching of the superradiant instability. We demonstrate that within a specific frequency band, the external magnetic field alters the physical boundary condition at the horizon from a propagating state to a purely exponentially decaying state, strictly locking the dissipation to zero ($\text{Im}(ω) = 0$). Consequently, the system supports two physically distinct classes of stationary bound states. Alongside the classical synchronized scalar clouds (Type-I) existing strictly at the superradiant threshold, we identify a new class of scalar clouds that exponentially decay at the event horizon (Type-II). Supported by precise numerical integrations, we demonstrate the spatial structure of these configurations. Our findings reveal that magnetized astrophysical environments can harbor significantly richer bosonic configurations than standard isolated black holes.

### [97] [Probing Two Dark Dimensions through Primordial Black Holes, Gravitational Waves, and Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27992)
*Waqas Ahmed,George K. Leontaris*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在二维额外维度（2DD）框架下研究原初黑洞（PBH）暗物质，发现引入量子引力记忆负担效应（memory-burden effect）后，蒸发速率被强烈抑制，使质量低至10⁻³克的PBH可存活至今并构成全部暗物质；同时计算了由此产生的二阶引力波背景信号，指出LISA、DECIGO和脉冲星计时阵列可加以探测，并结合高能对撞机上的微观黑洞衰变信号提供对高维引力和PBH暗物质的互补检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高维膜世界场景（brane-world scenario）中PBH作为暗物质候选者的可行性，并考察量子引力记忆负担效应对PBH蒸发和演化的影响。

Method: 在6维2DD框架下计算高维PBH的演化，引入记忆指数p=2的量子引力记忆负担效应；分析二阶原初曲率扰动诱导的随机引力波背景，并利用Fisher预测（Fisher forecast）评估未来实验对PBH参数的限制能力。

Result: 当记忆指数p=2时，PBH蒸发速率被强烈抑制，初始质量小至~10⁻³g的PBH可存活至今；PBH可在10⁻³g至10²¹g的质量范围内解释全部暗物质；四维标量诱导引力波形式在该质量范围内仍然适用；LISA、DECIGO和脉冲星计时阵列可探测相应信号，Fisher预测表明这些观测能高精度约束PBH质量、暗物质占比及原初曲率谱宽度。

Abstract: We study primordial-black-hole (PBH) dark matter in the two-dark-dimensions (2DD) framework, a six-dimensional brane-world scenario with two compact extra dimensions and a fundamental gravity scale of order $10\,\mathrm{TeV}$. We calculate the evolution of higher-dimensional PBHs including the recently proposed quantum-gravitational memory-burden effect. For a memory exponent $p=2$, the evaporation rate is strongly suppressed, allowing PBHs with initial masses as small as $\sim10^{-3}\,\mathrm{g}$ to survive until the present epoch. Consequently, PBHs can account for the observed dark matter over a mass range extending from $10^{-3}\,\mathrm{g}$ to $10^{21}\,\mathrm{g}$. We further compute the stochastic gravitational-wave background generated at second order by the primordial curvature perturbations responsible for PBH formation. We show that the conventional four-dimensional formalism for scalar-induced gravitational waves remains applicable throughout the mass range accessible to current and future gravitational wave experiments. The resulting signals can be probed by LISA, DECIGO, and pulsar timing arrays. Using Fisher forecasts, we find that these observations can constrain the PBH mass, dark-matter fraction, and width of the primordial curvature spectrum with high precision. The low fundamental gravity scale of the 2DD framework also permits the production of microscopic black holes at future high-energy colliders. Their decay signatures, together with gravitational-wave measurements, provide complementary tests of higher-dimensional gravity, the memory-burden mechanism, and primordial-black-hole dark matter.

### [98] [Revisit Static Aether: Exact Vacuum Solution in Einstein-Aether Theory and Its Analytic Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27995)
*Jie Zhu,Hao Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文严格求解了具有静态以太构型的爱因斯坦-以太理论（Einstein-Aether theory）的精确真空解，发现该解在耦合参数c14非零时不再是黑洞，而是退化为裸奇点或虫洞几何，并通过完整解析延拓揭示了其全局因果结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦-以太理论是洛伦兹对称性破缺的引力理论（Lorentz-violating gravity theory），但其真空解的全局结构尚未被充分探索。作者旨在解析求解严格静态以太构型下的精确解，并研究其最大延拓，以理解该理论中因果结构的完整图景。

Method: 采用精确解析求解方法，对爱因斯坦-以太理论中静态以太（static aether）构型求真空严格解；通过构建完整的解析延拓（analytic extension）分析时空的全局结构，并利用卡特-彭罗斯图（Carter-Penrose diagrams）总结因果结构。

Result: 解仅依赖于耦合参数c14，在c14=0时退化为史瓦西几何（Schwarzschild geometry）。当c14≠0时，时空不再是黑洞：c14<0对应裸奇点（naked singularity），0<c14<2对应虫洞状几何（wormhole-like geometry）。虫洞的内部无限远对应一个极值 Killing 视界（extremal Killing horizon），穿过该视界后时间和径向坐标的因果角色互换，时空最终终止于类空奇点（spacelike singularity）。

Conclusion: 静态以太真空解中，史瓦西解是一个孤立的成员，任何非零c14都会根本性地改变时空类型；该解的全局因果结构揭示了之前未被探索的静态-以太真空时空的因果完备化。

Abstract: We obtain an exact analytical vacuum solution of Einstein-Aether theory with a strictly static aether configuration and investigate its maximal extension. The solution depends only on the coupling $c_{14}$ and reduces to the Schwarzschild geometry in the limit $c_{14}=0$. We show that Schwarzschild is an isolated member of this family: for any nonzero $c_{14}$ the spacetime ceases to be a black hole and instead becomes either a naked singularity ($c_{14}<0$) or a wormhole-like geometry ($0<c_{14}<2$). By constructing the complete analytic extension, we demonstrate that the internal infinity of the wormhole corresponds to an extremal Killing horizon. Crossing this horizon leads to a new spacetime region where the causal roles of time and radial coordinates are exchanged, and the spacetime ultimately terminates at a spacelike singularity. The resulting global structure, summarized by the corresponding Carter-Penrose diagrams, reveals a previously unexplored causal completion of the static-aether vacuum spacetime.

</details>


### [99] [Construction of Sensitivity Curves for Dynamic LISA and Taiji](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28071)
*Hong-Yu Shi,Yong Tang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了动态LISA型探测器在一年日心轨道上的方向依赖性响应与灵敏度，发现相对于静态近似，低频频段灵敏度变化约20%，导致可探测引力波源数量方向依赖性变化约70%，因此应采用全动态、方向依赖的灵敏度曲线进行精确的引力波源计数与参数推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天基引力波激光干涉仪（如LISA和Taiji）通常被建模为静态等边三角形星座，这种近似忽略了轨道运动与方向依赖性，导致对仪器灵敏度和响应特性的描述不够精确，从而影响科学目标评估和参数估计能力。

Method: 基于解析的、时间依赖的日心轨道模型（analytical, time-dependent heliocentric orbital model）和绝热不等臂干涉仪配置（adiabatic unequal-arm interferometer configuration），在迈克尔逊干涉通道中构建了动态LISA和Taiji的方向依赖灵敏度曲线，并推导了角度依赖灵敏度的解析表达式。

Result: 低频频段方向依赖的灵敏度出现象限型图样（quadrant-like pattern）；相对于静态近似，低频灵敏度变化约20%，可探测引力波源数量的方向依赖性变化约70%，在更高频段差异更大。

Conclusion: 为获得准确的引力波源总数预测和双星系统的可靠参数推断，必须采用全动态、方向依赖的灵敏度曲线，而非静态近似。

Abstract: Space-based gravitational-wave (GW) laser interferometers, including LISA and Taiji, are designed to observe gravitational waves in the millihertz band and are expected to open up a frequency range that is otherwise inaccessible. The sensitivity and response of these instruments are central to their scientific goals, mission design and parameter estimation capabilities. However, they are commonly modeled as static, equilateral triangular constellations, an approximation that neglects both orbital motion and directional dependence. In this work, we systematically examine the direction-dependent response and sensitivity of dynamic LISA-like detectors over an entire year of heliocentric orbit. Based on an analytical, time-dependent heliocentric orbital model and an adiabatic unequal-arm interferometer configuration, we construct direction-dependent sensitivity curves in the Michelson interferometric channel for dynamic LISA and Taiji. We obtain analytic expressions for the angular-dependent sensitivity and demonstrate the emergence of a quadrant-like pattern in sky maps at low frequencies. We show that, relative to the static approximation, the low-frequency sensitivity varies by roughly $20\%$, which in turn produces about a $70\%$ variation in the directional dependence of the number of detectable GW sources, with even larger discrepancies at higher frequencies. Therefore, for accurate predictions of the total GW source counts and reliable parameter inference for binary systems, it is necessary to employ fully dynamic, direction-dependent sensitivity curves.

### [100] [Joint inference of line-of-sight acceleration and orbital eccentricity in neutron-star--black-hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28156)
*Lorenzo Pompili,Aldo Gamboa,Alessandra Buonanno*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在引力波波形模型中实现了视线加速度（LOSA）的时域修正，统一适用于高阶模式、自旋进动和轨道离心率，并基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA目录中的五颗中子星-黑洞（NSBH）事件首次对其中三个给出了LOSA约束，所有事件均与零LOSA一致；但对GW200105_162426的联合后验分析在90%置信度下排除了Γ和e同时为零的情形，支持了此前文献中的离心率线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 紧凑双星质心的视线加速度（LOSA）可作为动力学形成环境的单事件诊断，但波形模型中的系统误差——缺失高阶模式、自旋进动或轨道离心率——可能模仿或掩盖非零LOSA，因此波形准确性成为LOSA推断的关键问题。

Method: 将LOSA修正直接以应变重映射（remap of the strain）的方式在时域中实现，该处理统一适用于所有模式内容（mode content）、自旋进动（spin precession）和轨道离心率（orbital eccentricity），并与时域旋进-合并-振铃（inspiral-merger-ringdown）模型自然集成；将其部署到SEOBNRv6EHM（对齐自旋离心率模型）和SEOBNRv5PHM（进动准圆形模型）中，并在模拟信号上验证实现。

Result: SEOBNRv6EHM能在离心率和自旋进动注入信号上正确恢复LOSA，而SEOBNRv5PHM在离心率信号上产生虚假LOSA测量。对五颗中子星-黑洞（NSBH）事件的联合推断报告了其中三个事件的首次LOSA约束；所有五个事件均与零LOSA（Γ=0）一致，但GW200105_162426的联合后验在90%置信度下排除了Γ和e同时为零。

Conclusion: 时域LOSA修正方法有效且适用于包含复杂物理效应的波形模型；针对GW200105_162426的联合推断结果支持了此前分析中报告的离心率线索，强调了对离心率和LOSA进行联合建模的必要性。

Abstract: A line-of-sight acceleration (LOSA) of a compact-binary center of mass, imparted for example by a nearby tertiary perturber, imprints a Doppler modulation on the gravitational-wave signal and provides a single-event diagnostic of dynamical formation environments. Waveform-modeling systematics -- missing higher-order modes, spin precession, or orbital eccentricity -- can mimic or mask a non-zero LOSA, making waveform accuracy a leading concern for LOSA inference. We implement LOSA corrections directly in the time domain as a remap of the strain: the treatment applies uniformly to all mode content, spin precession, and orbital eccentricity, and integrates naturally with time-domain inspiral-merger-ringdown models that best capture these effects. We deploy it in the SEOBNRv6EHM (aligned-spin eccentric) and SEOBNRv5PHM (precessing quasi-circular) models, and validate the implementation on simulated signals; we find that SEOBNRv6EHM recovers LOSA correctly on both eccentric and spin-precessing injections, while SEOBNRv5PHM yields a spurious LOSA measurement on eccentric signals. Motivated by the eccentricity hints in the neutron-star--black-hole (NSBH) event GW200105_162426 and the favorable low-mass regime of these sources, we jointly infer LOSA and orbital eccentricity for the five NSBH events in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA catalog, reporting the first LOSA constraints on three of them. All five events are consistent with a vanishing LOSA, $Γ\equiv a_\parallel/c = 0$; for GW200105_162426, the joint $(Γ, e)$ posterior nonetheless disfavors both $Γ$ and $e$ being zero simultaneously at 90% credibility, supporting the eccentricity hints reported in previous analyses.

### [101] [Finite Coherence in Gravitational Waves from Tidally Excited Axion Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28161)
*Yizhi Liang,Mian Zhu,Wen-Biao Han,Lianfu Wei,Peng Wang,Jun Tao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转黑洞周围轴子云（axion cloud）形成的引力原子（gravitational atom）在双星系统中的潮汐跃迁（tidal transition）辐射引力波的过程，发现跃迁辐射由出射二能级相干性（outgoing two-level coherence）主导，而非仅由跃迁概率决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索旋转黑洞周围轴子云在双星系统中通过潮汐相互作用产生引力波的机制，并揭示相干性在跃迁辐射中的关键作用。

Method: 基于强耦合玻尔穿越（strongly coupled Bohr crossings）下的二能级系统分析，考察不同扫描速率下相干性的演化及其对跃迁波形和轨道响应的影响。

Result: 相干性在绝热分支（adiabatic branch）和弱穿越极限（weak passage limit）下被抑制，但在中间扫描速率下得以存续，产生有限的跃迁波形和局域化轨道响应；更大质量系统中精细与超精细跃迁（fine and hyperfine transitions）会产生窄带引力辐射及对真空双星波形的累积偏离。

Conclusion: 相干潮汐穿越（coherent tidal crossings）为探测轴子云动力学提供了引力波探针。

Abstract: Axion clouds around rotating black holes form gravitational atoms whose tidal transitions can radiate gravitational waves in binaries. For strongly coupled Bohr crossings, transition radiation is governed by the outgoing two-level coherence, not by the transition probability alone. This coherence is suppressed both on the adiabatic branch and in the weak passage limit, but survives for intermediate sweep rates, producing a finite transition waveform and a localized orbital response. In more massive systems, fine and hyperfine transitions produce narrowband gravitational radiation and cumulative departures from vacuum binary waveforms. Coherent tidal crossings offer a gravitational-wave probe of axion-cloud dynamics.

### [102] [Gravitational-wave response functions for space-borne detectors based on multiple geometric time-delay interferometry links](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28173)
*Rui Luo,Pan-Pan Wang,Lin-Lin Yang,Xin-Lei Zhao,Cheng-Gang Shao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将激光多普勒频移的表示扩展至多种几何构型（包括往返链路（round-trip links）和非往返链路（non-round-trip links）），提出基于几何链路的广义TDI组合公式，并重新构建45种第二代TDI组合的响应函数。

Result: 新的链路映射规则显著简化了多个TDI组合的数学表达式，增强了物理清晰度，同时能够高效构建响应函数并降低了计算复杂度。

Conclusion: 该方法为未来星载引力波任务的数据处理提供了可靠的理论与算法基础。

Abstract: The primary challenge for space-borne gravitational wave (GW) detectors lies in extracting the weak GW signal from instrumental noise that exceeds the signal level by many orders of magnitude. Time-delay interferometry (TDI) addresses this by suppressing the dominant laser phase noise through recombination of time-delayed measurement data. The detector's response to a GW signal is represented in the frequency domain by a response function. Currently, the GW signal response is first expressed in terms of the Doppler frequency shift in a single detection arm, and this formulation is then incorporated into specific TDI combinations to derive the corresponding response function. This paper introduces a generalized formulation for TDI combinations based on multiple geometric links. By extending the representation of the laser Doppler frequency shift to include various geometric configurations, such as round-trip and non-round-trip links, we reformulate 45 second-generation TDI combinations. For several of these, the new formulation significantly streamlines their mathematical expressions and enhances physical clarity. Our results demonstrate that the proposed link-mapping rules not only enable efficient construction of response functions for these TDI combinations but also reduce computational complexity. This approach provides a reliable theoretical and algorithmic foundation for data processing in future space-borne GW missions.

### [103] [Nonlinear stability of subextremal Kerr black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28253)
*Peter Hintz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在完全次极端（full subextremal range）范围内，Kerr 黑洞族（Kerr black holes）的整体非线性稳定性（global nonlinear stability）：从接近次极端 Kerr 黑洞的初始数据出发的爱因斯坦真空方程解，会在空间紧致区域中以 $\mathcal{O}(t_*^{-2-\varepsilon_{\mathcal K}})$ 的速率衰减到附近的 Kerr 解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kerr 黑洞的整体非线性稳定性问题是广义相对论中核心的长期开放问题。本文旨在严格证明次极端范围内 Kerr 黑洞族的全局非线性稳定性，填补此前仅在线性或特定参数范围下获得部分结果的空白。

Method: 采用广义波映射规范（generalized wave map gauge），通过规范源项（gauge source terms）进行修正，这些源项位于由初始数据展开所确定的有限维空间中。将规范源项与最终黑洞参数（质量和角动量）及引力波尾（gravitational wave tail）一起作为非线性 Nash-Moser 迭代方案的未知量处理。直接处理张量方程，在线性模式稳定性证明中借助 Teukolsky 方程约化。

Result: 对于初始数据要求 $\mathcal{O}(r^{-1-\varepsilon_0})$ 衰减（$\varepsilon_0>0$），更精确地，允许有限项展开为 $r^{-z}(\log r)^k$ 形式（$z>1, k\in\mathbb{N}_0$），加上 $\mathcal{O}(r^{-3-\varepsilon_0})$ 的剩余项。解在空间紧致区域中以速率 $\mathcal{O}(t_*^{-2-\varepsilon_{\mathcal K}})$ 衰减到 Kerr 族中的邻近成员。

Conclusion: 本文在完全次极端范围内解决了 Kerr 黑洞的整体非线性稳定性问题，表明从接近次极端 Kerr 初始数据出发的爱因斯坦真空方程解会收敛到附近的 Kerr 解。该工作依赖于两篇配套论文，分别引入强形式的约束阻尼（constraint damping）和提供前向解（forward solutions）的驯服估计（tame estimates）。

Abstract: We settle the global nonlinear stability problem for the family of Kerr black holes in the full subextremal range: spacetimes evolving from initial data close to those of a subextremal Kerr black hole as solutions of the Einstein vacuum equation ${\rm Ric}(g)=0$ settle down to a nearby member of the Kerr family at the rate $\mathcal{O}(t_*^{-2-ε_{\mathcal K}})$ in spatially compact regions.
  For the initial data, we require $\mathcal{O}(r^{-1-ε_0})$-decay for $ε_0>0$ -- more precisely, an arbitrary but finite expansion into terms $r^{-z}(\log r)^k$ where $z>1$, $k\in\mathbb{N}_0$, plus a remainder term with $\mathcal{O}(r^{-3-ε_0})$-decay. Similarly to previous work with Vasy in the Kerr-de Sitter setting, we use a generalized wave map gauge modified using gauge source terms that lie in a suitable finite-dimensional space determined by the expansion of the initial data. Like the final black hole parameters (mass and angular momentum) and the gravitational wave tail, the gauge source terms are treated as unknowns in a nonlinear (Nash-Moser) iteration scheme. We work directly with the tensorial equation and in particular do not rely on reductions to scalar equations (except insofar as a reduction to the Teukolsky equation is used in the proof of linear mode stability).
  This paper relies on two companion papers by the author. The first one introduces a strong form of constraint damping in the full subextremal range, which we use in our formulation of the gauge-fixed Einstein equation as a black box. The second one provides tame estimates (albeit with weak decay) for forward solutions of a general class of wave-type equations, which we show here to include the linearizations of the gauge-fixed Einstein equation arising in our nonlinear iteration scheme; these estimates are the starting point for our detailed asymptotic analysis.

</details>


### [104] [Generalizing the interacting dilatonic ghost condensate as a dark energy model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28288)
*Manuel Gonzalez-Espinoza,Ramon Herrera,Johan Casimiro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种广义膨胀鬼凝聚场（generalized dilatonic ghost condensate field）作为暗能量候选者的宇宙演化。该场由包含两个主导动能项（一个线性项和一个任意整数 n>2 的高阶项）及指数势的拉格朗日密度（Lagrangian density）构建，并与暗物质通过源项相互作用。通过三种相互作用模型（无相互作用 Q=0、Q∝ρ_m·φ̇ 和 Q∝ρ_m H）的相空间分析及联合似然分析（联合 Cosmic Chronometers、PantheonPlus 和 DESI 观测数据），发现系统均能复现标准宇宙学动力学并演化至晚期暗能量主导的吸引子（attractor），且能量转移方向与耦合参数 α 的符号及相互作用形式相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统暗能量模型（如宇宙学常数）存在精细调节和巧合问题，亟需更灵活的动力学暗能量候选者。广义鬼凝聚（ghost condensate）场结合非标准动能项与标量-张量耦合，有望统一描述宇宙早期暴胀与晚期加速膨胀，且通过与暗物质的相互作用可缓解巧合问题。

Method: 构建包含线性动能项（系数 α）和任意整数 n>2 的高阶动能项以及指数势的拉格朗日密度。对三种相互作用模型（Q=0、Q∝ρ_m·φ̇、Q∝ρ_m H）进行详细相空间分析（phase-space analysis），求解临界点并导出稳定性条件。进一步利用 Cosmic Chronometers、PantheonPlus 和 DESI 的观测数据，对 n=3 和 n=5 两种情形进行联合似然分析（joint likelihood analysis），获得 68% 和 95% 置信水平下的参数约束。

Result: 所有相互作用模型均能复现标准宇宙学动力学，并演化至暗能量主导的晚期吸引子，呈现精质场（quintessence）或幻象场（phantom）特征，具体取决于标准动能项耦合参数 α 的符号。对于 Q∝φ̇ρ_m 模型，能量流动方向由 α 符号决定；对于 Q∝Hρ_m 模型，能量流动方向与 α 符号无关，始终为负（暗物质→暗能量）。

Conclusion: 广义膨胀鬼凝聚场能够有效描述当前宇宙的加速膨胀，其与暗物质的相互作用为缓解巧合问题提供了可行途径。不同相互作用形式对能量转移方向的影响存在本质差异，这为通过未来观测区分相互作用暗能量模型提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this article, we study the cosmic evolution of a generalized dilatonic ghost condensate field as a dark energy candidate, formulated from a Lagrangian density with two dominant kinetic terms; one linear and one of arbitrary integer $n>2$ in combination with an exponential potential, which interacts with dark matter through a source term. We analyzed three scenarios: the non-interacting situation $Q=0$ and two different interaction models, $Q\proptoρ_m\dotφ$ and $Q\propto ρ_m H$ to describe the evolution of the present universe. For each interaction $Q$, we perform a detailed phase-space analysis to obtain stability conditions and identify critical points. In all situations, the system reproduces the standard cosmological dynamics and evolves toward late-time dark energy-dominated attractors, with quintessence or phantom features depending on the sign of the coupling parameter $α$ associated with the standard kinetic term. Furthermore, a joint likelihood analysis with Cosmic Chronometers, PantheonPlus, and DESI observations is performed for two values of power $n$ ($n=3$ and $n=5$) to determine marginalized parameter constraints at the confidence levels of 68$\%$ and 95$\%$ for the different $Q-$models. For the interaction term $Q\propto \dotφρ_m$, we find that the direction of the flow of energy depends on the sign of the coupling parameter $α$ associated with the standard kinetic term. However, for the interaction $Q\propto H\,ρ_m$, the direction of the energy flow is independent of the sign of the coupling parameter $α$ and always remains negative, corresponding to an energy transfer from dark matter to dark energy.

### [106] [In-flight calibration of the Wide-field X-ray Telescope on board the Einstein Probe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28101)
*Huaqing Cheng,Hai-Wu Pan,Yuan Liu,Jingwei Hu,Haonan Yang,Donghua Zhao,Zhixing Ling,Yifan Chen,Xiaojin Sun,Longhui Li,Ge Jin,Wenxin Wang,Xue Yang,He-Yang Liu,Chen Zhang,Shuang-Nan Zhang,Weimin Yuan*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍了爱因斯坦探针卫星（Einstein Probe）上广角X射线望远镜（WXT）在轨运行两年半期间利用标准天体源（蟹状星云、天蝎座X-1、仙后座A）进行的定标结果，证实其性能与地面测试一致，空间分辨率中位数约4.3角分，0.5-4 keV能段有效面积系统不确定度≤10%，部分探测器在低能端（0.4-0.6 keV）出现约30%-40%的长期退化，所有定标产品已纳入WXT定标数据库（CALDB）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦探针卫星（Einstein Probe, EP）搭载的广角X射线望远镜（Wide-field X-ray Telescope, WXT）采用新型龙虾眼（lobster-eye）光学系统，实现了大瞬时视场（instantaneous field-of-view, FoV）与高灵敏度的独特组合，用于监测动态X射线天空。为确保科学观测数据的可靠性，必须通过在轨运行数据对WXT的各项关键仪器性能进行系统定标与验证。

Method: 通过对标准天体源——蟹状星云（Crab Nebula）、天蝎座X-1（Scorpius X-1）和仙后座A（Cassiopeia A）的观测，系统表征WXT的关键仪器特性。将实测结果与发射前地面定标数据及模型预测进行对比分析，评估空间分辨率、源定位精度、有效面积、探测器稳定性及光谱性能等指标。

Result: WXT在轨性能与地面定标结果一致。空间分辨率以焦斑半高全宽（full width at half maximum, FWHM）表征，在约90%视场内范围为3角分至6角分，中位数约4.3角分；定标后源定位精度在90%置信度下达到1.3角分；0.5-4 keV能段在轨有效面积与模型预测及地面测量一致，系统不确定度≤10%（90% C.L.）；大部分探测器高度稳定，但少数模块在低能端（0.4-0.6 keV）出现约30%-40%的长期退化；利用仙后座A进行的光谱评估证实了焦平面互补金属氧化物半导体（Complementary Metal-Oxide Semiconductor, CMOS）探测器能量刻度与光谱分辨率的稳定性。

Conclusion: 所有定标产品已纳入WXT定标数据库（WXT calibration database, CALDB）。这些结果全面验证了WXT的仪器能力，为可靠的科学观测数据分析提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: By utilizing novel lobster-eye optics, the Wide-field X-ray Telescope (WXT) onboard the Einstein Probe (EP) satellite achieves an unprecedented combination of a large instantaneous field-of-view (FoV) and high sensitivity for monitoring the dynamic X-ray sky. In this paper, we present the in-orbit calibration results of the WXT during its first two and a half years of operations. By conducting observations of standard celestial sources--including the Crab Nebula, Scorpius X-1, and Cassiopeia A--we systematically characterized key instrumental properties. Our analysis demonstrates that the in-orbit performance of the WXT agrees with prelaunch ground calibrations well. The spatial resolution, denoted by the full width at half maximum (FWHM) of the focal spot, typically ranges from $3'$ to $6'$ across $\sim$90% of the FoV, with a median of $\sim 4.3'$. The post-calibration source positioning accuracy achieves $1.3'$ (at the 90% confidence level). The in-orbit effective area is consistent with model predictions and ground measurements, exhibiting an overall systematic uncertainty of $\lesssim 10\%$ (90% C.L.) in the 0.5-4 keV band. While the vast majority of the detectors remain highly stable, a noticeable long-term degradation at the low-energy end ($\sim30\%$-$40\%$, 0.4-0.6 keV) is observed in a few specific modules. Furthermore, spectral evaluations using Cas A confirm the stability of the energy scale and spectral resolution of the focal-plane Complementary Metal-Oxide Semiconductor (CMOS) detectors. All derived calibration products have been incorporated into the WXT calibration database (CALDB). These results comprehensively verify the instrumental capabilities of the WXT, providing a solid foundation for the reliable analysis of scientific observations.

</details>

### [107] [A General Pipeline for Digesting Scientific Literature into a Shared Scientific Knowledge Base](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27384)
*Charles T. Black*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 本文提出Materials Explorer Pipeline，一个从科学论文中自动提取结构化数据的管道，生成带有完整溯源和置信度的样本记录，支持交互式探索和假设候选生成，并在超导量子比特材料文献中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公开发表的科学文献是测量数据、相关性和观察结果的丰富且持续增长的记录，现代AI工具可以以新的方式使其变得可访问，但现有方法缺乏结构化和可查询性。

Method: Materials Explorer Pipeline将科学论文集合消化为结构化、可查询的数据库，生成带有完整溯源（provenance）和置信度（confidence）的样本记录，支持交互式探索，并为科学家评审提供假设候选（hypothesis candidates）。每条提取记录是一个自包含、可移植的知识单元，包含测量数据、研究细节和源引用。

Result: 该管道在Co-design Center for Quantum Advantage（DOE国家量子信息科学研究中心）的超导量子比特材料文献上进行了演示，生成了一个包含10个材料类别、233个样本的语料库。

Conclusion: 该管道架构是领域无关的（domain-agnostic），设计上可便捷地移植到其他科学领域。

Abstract: The published scientific literature is a rich, continuously growing record of measurements, correlations, and observations that modern AI tools can now make accessible in new ways. The Materials Explorer Pipeline digests collections of scientific papers into a structured, queryable database, producing sample records with full provenance and confidence, making them interactively explorable, and surfacing hypothesis candidates for scientist review. Each extracted record is a self-contained, portable unit of knowledge, carrying the measurements, research details, and source citations needed to use and cite the data appropriately. The Pipeline is demonstrated on recent superconducting qubit materials literature of the Co-design Center for Quantum Advantage, a DOE National Quantum Information Science Research Center, producing a corpus of 233 samples across 10 material classes. The Pipeline architecture is domain-agnostic and designed to be readily portable to other scientific domains.

</details>

### [108] [Quantum typicality survives non-Abelian gauge constraints: exact analytical prediction confirmed in $SU(2)$ lattice gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27402)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过二维环面上SU(2)晶格规范理论的数值计算，证明量子典型性（quantum typicality）在规范理论的物理希尔伯特空间中依然成立：严格不相交链接之间的典型互信息（mutual information）符合无参数解析预测，且相关性增长箭头只出现在非典型初始条件下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究涌现时空（emergent spacetime）论证的一个前提——量子典型性在非阿贝尔规范理论（non-Abelian gauge theory）的物理希尔伯特空间（physical Hilbert space）中是否依然成立，因为规范约束可能在原则上注入可支撑几何结构的纠缠（geometry-supporting entanglement）。

Method: 采用二维环面上SU(2)晶格规范理论（lattice gauge theory），物理希尔伯特空间维度d_phys最高达4,193；数值计算严格不相交链接之间的典型互信息，将其与微正则基线（microcanonical baseline）结合哈氏随机涨落（Haar-random fluctuations）的无参数解析预测进行比较。

Result: 典型互信息精确吻合该无参数解析预测。Kogut-Susskind哈密顿量（Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian）能从具有确定几何的初态（如电真空态）生成关联，而典型态仅呈现均值回归（regression to the mean）。

Conclusion: 量子典型性在非阿贝尔规范理论中依然成立；相关性增长箭头（arrow of correlation growth）需要非典型初始条件（non-generic initial condition）才能建立。

Abstract: Arguments for emergent spacetime require that quantum typicality, the generic absence of inter-subsystem correlations, persists on the physical Hilbert space of a gauge theory, where non-Abelian constraints could in principle inject geometry-supporting entanglement. Using $SU(2)$ lattice gauge theory on two-dimensional tori ($d_{\mathrm{phys}}$ up to $4{,}193$), we show that it does: the typical mutual information between strictly disjoint links matches an exact parameter-free analytical prediction combining a microcanonical baseline with Haar-random fluctuations. The Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian generates correlations from states of definite geometry (such as the electric vacuum), while generic states show only regression to the mean, establishing that the arrow of correlation growth requires a non-generic initial condition.

### [109] [Qudit extension of parameterized IQP circuits: A generative quantum machine learning approach to integer data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28236)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参数化IQP电路在二元分布生成学习中表现良好，但处理非二元数据集时，将整数值映射为与量子比特兼容的二进制表示会破坏原始数据的度量结构（metric structure）。因此需要一种更自然的整数映射方案来避免信息损失。

Method: 将IQP量子电路改造为量子比特（qudit）形式：每个整数值像素被编码为固定长度的比特串，量子门遵循qudit形式论进行变换。针对生成式机器学习任务，设计了合适的损失函数（loss function）用于电路训练，并开发了特征间协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）的计算方法。

Result: 该方法在CLIC探测器电磁量能器的单粒子电子簇射能量沉积数据上进行了验证，证明了所提出框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于qudit的IQP电路方法能够适用于非二元数据的量子生成式机器学习，并可推广至其他类似应用场景。

Abstract: Parameterized Instantaneous Quantum Polynomial (IQP) circuits have proven useful in quantum generative learning models, particularly for binary distributions. However, when applied to non-binary datasets, they exhibit notable limitations: mapping integer values into qubit-compatible binary representations often destroys the original metric structure of the data. In this paper we aim to extend them to a qudits formulation operating on an integer mapping of the data. The IQP quantum circuit is adapted to encode each integer valued pixel into a bit-string of fixed length and quantum gates are transformed to follow the qudit formalism. As a generative machine learning approach, a suitable loss function for the circuit training and the calculation of the covariance matrix among features are developed and validated on the energy deposits from single-particle electron showers in the electromagnetic calorimeter of the CLIC detector. The method proposed in this work can be also extended to other applications that utilize quantum generative machine learning for non-binary data.

</details>


### [110] [Static features from mixing in short- and long-range Lindbladians: Markov property and correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28054)
*Paul Rosa-Ruiz,Matteo Scandi,Ángela Capel,Álvaro M. Alhambra*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了林德布拉德算符（Lindbladian）的动力学特征——快速混合（rapid mixing）与无挫性（frustration-freeness）——与其固定点（fixed-point）的互信息（MI）和条件互信息（CMI）衰减行为之间的理论联系，并将该结果推广到长程相互作用系统，证明了多项式衰减而非指数衰减的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合态（mixed-state）相的分类需要超越两点关联函数的判据，如互信息（mutual information, MI）和条件互信息（conditional mutual information, CMI）的衰减行为（后者由马尔可夫长度（Markov length）刻画）。现有理论对林德布拉德算符固定点的静态性质如何从其生成元的动力学特征中产生仍缺乏系统理解，尤其是在长程相互作用（long-range interactions）系统中。

Method: 论文采用数学证明与数值模拟相结合的方法。理论上，分别证明了（全局）快速混合与无挫性保证CMI随屏蔽距离（shielding distance）衰减，以及（局域）快速混合、本原性（primitivity）与正则性（regularity）保证MI的全局衰减。数值上，以长程伊辛模型（long-range Ising model）含与不含横向场为例进行验证。

Result: 对于以幂律α衰减的长程相互作用系统，MI和CMI均呈多项式衰减（polynomial decay），而非有限程或短程系统中的指数衰减（即有限马尔可夫长度）。长程非对易哈密顿量（non-commuting Hamiltonians）的吉布斯态（Gibbs states）在任意温度下满足局域马尔可夫性质（local Markov property），将Chen–Rouzé (2025)的短程结论推广至长程情形。数值结果验证了CMI多项式衰减的边界。

Conclusion: 论文揭示了林德布拉德算符生成元的动力学性质直接决定其固定点的混合态关联结构，并为长程相互作用系统中混合态相的识别提供了理论判据。该结果对多种实验平台具有适用性。

Abstract: The classification of mixed-state phases requires criteria beyond two-point correlation functions, such as the decay of the mutual information (MI) and the conditional mutual information (CMI), with the latter encapsulated in the notion of Markov length. Here we show how such static properties of the fixed point of a Lindbladian follow from natural dynamical features of its generators: rapid mixing and frustration-freeness. We focus on systems with long-range interactions, and prove (i) that local Lindbladians satisfying (global) rapid mixing and frustration-freeness have fixed-points whose CMI decays with the shielding distance, and (ii) that (local) rapid mixing together with primitivity and regularity implies global decay of MI. For long-range interactions decaying with a power law with rate $α$, both quantities decay polynomially rather than exponentially, in contrast to the finite- and short-range regimes where exponential decay (a finite Markov length) is expected within a phase. We further show that Gibbs states of long-range, non-commuting Hamiltonians satisfy a local Markov property at any temperatures, extending the recent results (Chen--Rouzé, 2025) for short-range systems to the long-range regime relevant to a variety of experimental platforms. As a numerical example, we study the long-range Ising model both with and without a transverse field. We find regimes in which the polynomial decay of the CMI holds, in accordance with the bounds proven.

### [111] [Composing Quantum Instruments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28291)
*Robert I. Booth,Dominik Leichtle,Alex Rice,Kim Worrall*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究经典控制的量子仪器（classically-controlled quantum instruments）——马尔可夫核（Markov kernels）的量子对应——的复合结构。通过Heisenberg图像中的积分构造，利用Okamura-Ozawa正规扩张到von Neumann张量积，定义了量子通道值函数关于量子仪器的积分，该积分恢复了有限情形的已知公式，并构成了一个幺半群（monad），其Kleisli范畴即为量子马尔可夫核范畴。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典情形下马尔可夫核通过一个核与另一个核的积分进行复合；然而，将这种复合定义到具有连续结果的量子仪器上，需要构建量子通道值函数（quantum channel-valued function）关于量子仪器的积分，这一数学结构在文献中尚未建立。

Method: 采用Heisenberg图像（Heisenberg picture），借助Okamura-Ozawa正规扩张（Okamura-Ozawa normal extension）将问题归结到von Neumann张量积（von Neumann tensor product）上，从而构造出量子通道值函数关于量子仪器的积分。

Result: 该积分恢复了有限输出情形下预期的已知公式，保持了正规完全正性（normal complete positivity）与次幺正性（subunitality），并为量子仪器复合提供了一个幺半群结构（monad）的乘法运算。

Conclusion: 量子马尔可夫核范畴（category of quantum Markov kernels）被识别为该幺半群的Kleisli范畴（Kleisli category），从而建立了经典控制量子仪器复合的范畴论基础。

Abstract: We study the composition of classically-controlled quantum instruments--the natural quantum analogue of Markov kernels. Classically, Markov kernels compose by integrating one kernel against another. Defining this composition for quantum instruments with continuous outcomes requires an integral of quantum channel-valued functions with respect to a quantum instrument. We construct this integral in the Heisenberg picture using the Okamura-Ozawa normal extension to a von Neumann tensor product. This integral recovers the expected finite formula, preserves normal complete positivity and subunitality, and provides the multiplication for a monad governing the composition of quantum instruments. As an immediate consequence, we identify the category of quantum Markov kernels as the Kleisli category of this monad.

</details>


### [112] [Range-controlled entanglement in Lindbladian skin states of monitored fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09306)
*Gianluca Passarelli,Angelo Russomanno,Davide Rossini,Procolo Lucignano*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文通过受控耗散（controlled dissipation）和可调跳跃程（tunable hopping range）的费米子链模型，在Gaussian轨迹近似（Gaussian trajectory approximation）下发现两种有限尺寸标度行为：短程跳跃导致完全皮肤累积（complete skin accumulation）和面积律纠缠（area-law entanglement），长程跳跃则产生有限体态尾部（finite bulk tail）和有效子体积律纠缠（sub-volume-law entanglement），揭示耗散与相干跳跃共同调控皮肤局域化和量子纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水库工程（reservoir engineering）能够稳定幺正动力学（unitary dynamics）无法达到的量子态。理解耗散与相干跳跃如何共同影响Lindblad皮肤态（Lindbladian skin states）中的局域化和量子纠缠行为，是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 采用受监测的费米子链（monitored fermion chain）模型，引入可调跳跃程（tunable hopping range）的定向粒子数守恒耗散（directed particle-conserving dissipation），并在Gaussian轨迹近似（Gaussian trajectory approximation）框架下进行理论分析。

Result: 识别出两种有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）区域：短程跳跃（short-range hopping）对应完全皮肤累积（complete skin accumulation）和面积律纠缠（area-law entanglement）；长程跳跃（long-range hopping）则产生有限体态尾部（finite bulk tail）和有效代数的子体积律纠缠（effective algebraic sub-volume-law entanglement）。

Conclusion: 耗散（dissipation）与相干跳跃（coherent hopping）共同控制着皮肤局域化（skin localization）和量子纠缠（quantum entanglement），二者之间存在紧密的相互关联。

Abstract: Reservoir engineering can stabilize states inaccessible to unitary dynamics. Directed particle-conserving dissipation creates Lindbladian skin states, where Pauli exclusion turns edge accumulation into a many-body density imbalance. In a monitored fermion chain with tunable hopping range, we identify, within a Gaussian trajectory approximation, two finite-size scaling regimes: short-range hopping is consistent with complete skin accumulation and area-law entanglement, whereas sufficiently long-range hopping produces a finite bulk tail and effective algebraic sub-volume-law entanglement. Dissipation and coherent hopping thus jointly control skin localization and quantum entanglement, highlighting their close interconnection.

</details>


### [113] [Large Fluctuations in Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11822)
*V. Yu. Mylnikov,S. O. Potashin,A. Kamenev*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了驱动开放量子系统稳态中非典型测量结果的统计特性，发现其大偏差函数（large-deviation function）在相空间坐标上丧失解析性，产生导数不连续的线或面，并通过参数驱动的Kerr振子模型结合Keldysh-Lindblad作用量中的半经典瞬子（instanton）轨迹阐明了这一现象的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平衡态系统中，相空间概率分布（如Wigner函数）在坐标上是解析的；但驱动耗散系统中这一性质是否仍然成立尚不明确。作者旨在揭示驱动开放量子系统中大偏差函数的非解析特征及其物理起源。

Method: 以参数驱动的Kerr振子（parametrically driven Kerr oscillator）为示例，该振子与耗散热库存在线性和/或非线性耦合。通过对应的Keldysh-Lindblad作用量（Keldysh-Lindblad action）中的半经典瞬子轨迹描述振幅和相位上的稀有涨落。

Result: 发现同一个涨落可以通过多条不同的瞬子轨迹实现，这些轨迹之间的竞争导致主导瞬子（dominant instanton）发生突变，从而在大偏差函数中产生非解析特征。

Conclusion: 驱动耗散系统中大偏差函数普遍存在非解析性，这源于多条瞬子轨迹的竞争，标志着远离平衡态的统计行为与平衡态系统有本质区别。

Abstract: We study statistics of atypical measurement outcomes in the steady states of driven open quantum systems. In equilibrium, the probability distribution over the phase space, as encoded in, e.g., the Wigner function, is analytic in the phase-space coordinates. We show that this property is generically lost in driven dissipative systems: their {\it large-deviation function} develops lines and surfaces across which its derivatives are discontinuous. As an illustrative example, we consider a parametrically driven Kerr oscillator coupled linearly and/or nonlinearly to a dissipative bath. Rare fluctuations in the amplitude and phase of the induced oscillations are governed by semiclassical instanton trajectories of the corresponding Keldysh-Lindblad action. We demonstrate that a given fluctuation can be realized through multiple distinct instanton trajectories. The competition between these trajectories leads to abrupt switching of the dominant instanton and, consequently, to non-analytic features in the large-deviation function.

</details>


### [114] [Fault tolerant computation of the static structure factor and finite size effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27734)
*Rishabh Bhardwaj,Alexander Reed Muñoz,Travis E. Jones,John Golden*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种量子后处理策略，通过测量小动量静态结构因子 $S(q)$ 来修正周期性材料基态能量估计中的有限尺寸效应（finite-size effect），为容错量子算法提供了一种高效的有限尺寸修正方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 容错量子算法（fault-tolerant quantum algorithms）有望估算经典电子结构方法难以处理的周期性材料基态能量，但面临有限尺寸效应（finite-size effect）这一挑战：量子算法在有限超胞或有限布里渊区网格上计算，而材料性质定义在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下。现有方法需通过降采样（down-sampling）重复进行更大尺寸的计算，代价高昂。

Method: 首先通过扭折平均（twist averaging）减小单体壳效应；然后利用长波密度涨落（long-wavelength density fluctuations）导致的剩余主导误差，该误差编码在小动量静态结构因子 $S(q)$ 中。在布洛赫轨道基（Bloch-orbital basis）中构造对应算子，通过密度算子实现其块编码（block encoding），并采用放大的阿达玛测试（amplified Hadamard test）估计基态期望值。此外引入自适应全局与局部二分搜索（adaptive global and local binary search）以识别用于重构双体有限尺寸误差修正的红外拟合窗口（infrared fitting window）。

Result: 该结构因子修正方案的主导复杂度为 $\tilde{O}(N_bN_k)^3$（取决于布洛赫轨道基大小），避免了全哈密顿量模拟的大平面波预因子，仅需 $\tilde{O}(N_bN_k)$ 逻辑量子比特（logical qubits）。其计算开销相对于主基态能量估计流程仍处于次主导地位。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种容错量子计算中的有限尺寸修正替代方案：用针对控制有限尺寸效应的红外密度关联（infrared density correlations）的目标测量，取代在更大超胞上重复进行能量计算的传统降采样方法。

Abstract: Fault-tolerant quantum algorithms offer a promising pathway for estimating the ground-state energies of periodic materials that are beyond the practical reach of classical electronic-structure methods. A remaining challenge is finite-size mitigation: quantum algorithms evaluate a finite supercell or finite Brillouin-zone mesh, while materials properties are defined in the thermodynamic limit. In this work we develop a quantum post-processing strategy for the leading two-body finite-size correction. After one-body shell effects are reduced by twist averaging, the dominant residual error is controlled by long-wavelength density fluctuations, which are encoded in the small-momentum static structure factor $S(q)$. We formulate the corresponding operator in a Bloch-orbital basis, construct its block encoding through the density operator, and estimate its ground-state expectation value using an amplified Hadamard test. We also introduce adaptive global and local binary search procedures for identifying the infrared fitting window used to reconstruct the two-body finite size error correction. The resulting cost remains subleading relative to the main ground-state energy estimation routine: the structure-factor correction has leading $\tilde{O}(N_bN_k)^3$ dependence on the Bloch-orbital basis size, avoids the large plane-wave prefactor of full Hamiltonian simulation, and requires only $\tilde{O}(N_bN_k)$ logical qubits. This provides a fault-tolerant alternative to down-sampling, replacing repeated energy calculations on larger cells with targeted measurements of the infrared density correlations that control the finite-size effects.

</details>


### [115] [Industry-ready spin-photon interfaces for hybrid photonic quantum computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27787)
*Hêlio Huet,Hubert Lam,Thibaut Pollet,Petr Steindl,Alice Bernard,Albert Adiyatullin,Petr Stepanov,William Hease,Victor Guilloux,Nico Margaria,Joris Verstraten,Raksha Singla,Samuel T. Mister,Anton Pishchagin,Lara Couronné,Samuel Huber,David Sebastian,Duc Duy Tran,Thi Hao Nhi Nguyen,Thi Phuong Do,Joseph Sulpizio,Yann Portella,Kiarn T. Laverick,Thinhinane Bennour,Tomas Alexandre De Sousa,Davide Stefani,Mathias Pont,Maxime Descampeaux,Bianca Scaparra,Martin A. Jacobsen,Klaus D. Jöns,Rinaldo Trotta,Aristide Lemaître,Martina Morassi,Olivier Krebs,Loïc Lanco,Niels Gregersen,Alexia Auffèves,Maria Maffei,Shane Mansfield,Jean Senellart,Thomas Volz,Viviana Villafañe,Stephen C. Wein,Dario A. Fioretto,Sebastien Boissier,Thi Huong Au,Pascale Senellart*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究报告了通过III-V族半导体流片生产线批量制造的量子点器件，实现了接近理想效率的单光子产生、高不可区分性、七部分自旋-多光子纠缠和远距离光子不可区分性，为大规模混合光子量子计算（hybrid photonic quantum computing）提供了可扩展的固态平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合光子量子计算机（hybrid photonic quantum computers）结合静止物质量子比特（matter qubits）与飞行光子量子比特（flying photonic qubits），是实现大规模纠错量子计算的有效路径。其核心是腔耦合物质量子比特，但半导体量子点（quantum dots）平台在性能、可重复性和自旋相干性（spin coherence）方面尚未达到大规模纠错所需的阈值，亟需工业化制造与系统性控制方案。

Method: 采用III-V族半导体（III-V semiconductor）流片生产线工艺，批量制造了数千个单片式量子点器件。通过系统控制源参数优化器件性能；利用场正交态重构（field-quadrature state reconstruction）作为对效率和不可区分性（indistinguishability）的联合检验；在低磁场条件下展示自旋-多光子纠缠和自旋相干性。

Result: 实现了接近理想的单光子产生效率，光学损耗有望低于容错阈值（fault-tolerance threshold）；光子量子纯度（quantum purity）接近单位且在数十分钟内保持稳定；创造了单光子Wigner函数负值（Wigner-function negativity）的记录；实现了七部分自旋-多光子纠缠（seven-partite spin–multi-photon entanglement）；自旋相干时间延长至微秒量级；来自不同光源的光子与同一光源连续发射的光子具有相同的不可区分性。

Conclusion: III-V族量子点器件已具备与工业流片工艺兼容的可扩展性，为混合光子量子计算提供了可靠的固态平台基础。

Abstract: Hybrid photonic quantum computers, combining stationary matter qubits and flying photonic qubits, offer an intrinsically networked and resource-efficient route to large-scale, error-corrected quantum computation. Their core components are cavity-coupled matter qubits that act as light--matter interfaces, enabling: high-efficiency on-demand single-photon generation, stable near-unity photon indistinguishability and spin--multi-photon entanglement. Semiconductor quantum dots in microcavities are a leading platform for realizing such devices. Yet reaching the performance, reproducibility and spin-coherence thresholds for large-scale error correction remains a major challenge requiring industrial fabrication and control. Here we report thousands of monolithic semiconductor quantum-dot devices fabricated using a III--V pilot production-line process compatible with large-scale deployment. Systematic control of source parameters yields state-of-the-art efficiency and supports a path to optical losses below fault-tolerance thresholds. Using field-quadrature state reconstruction as a stringent joint test of efficiency and indistinguishability, we observe near-unity photon quantum purity stable over tens of minutes and a record single-photon Wigner-function negativity. We further demonstrate seven-partite spin--multi-photon entanglement and spin coherence extendable to microsecond timescales in the low-magnetic-field regime. Finally, photons from distant sources are as indistinguishable as photons emitted successively by a single source. These results establish foundry-compatible III--V quantum dots as a scalable platform for hybrid photonic quantum computing.
