### [116] [Hybrid quantum-classical neural network for sample-efficient recognition of topological phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28199)
*Markus K. Hoffmann,Leon C. Sander,Colin Scarato,Christoph Hellings,Johannes Knörzer,Michael J. Hartmann,Petr Zapletal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合量子-经典神经网络（hybrid quantum-classical neural network），由浅层参数化量子电路（shallow parameterized quantum circuit）、测量和经典神经网络组成，用于高效表征复杂量子态的整体性质。通过监督学习，该网络能够区分表面码（surface code）的拓扑相（topological phase）与对称性富集拓扑相（symmetry-enriched topological phase）及随机乘积态，并在识别拓扑相时将推理和训练样本复杂度降低约一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着量子计算机日益成熟，通过直接测量和经典后处理来表征量子态全局性质的标准方法因测量开销过大而变得不切实际。现有量子神经网络虽能减少测量，但往往需要深度量子电路，无法在现有设备上实现。

Method: 提出一种混合量子-经典神经网络架构，包含一个浅层参数化量子电路（进行测量基的非局域变换）、测量操作以及一个经典神经网络；两者通过联合训练最大化不同量子态测量数据之间的统计距离（statistical distance）。

Result: 在监督学习任务中，该混合网络能够区分表面码的拓扑相、对称性富集拓扑相以及随机乘积态。与基于随机泡利测量（randomized Pauli measurements）训练的经典神经网络相比，该混合网络将识别拓扑相所需的推理和训练样本复杂度降低了约一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该混合量子-经典神经网络仅需浅层量子电路，可在现有量子计算机上直接实现，为复杂量子态的高效表征提供了一种可行方案。

Abstract: With increasing maturity of quantum computers, standard methods for characterizing global properties of their output quantum states via direct measurements and classical post-processing are becoming increasingly impractical due to large measurement costs. Although quantum neural networks could directly process quantum states to identify underlying characteristics with reduced measurement efforts, they often require deep quantum circuits that cannot be implemented on existing devices. To overcome these challenges, we introduce a hybrid quantum-classical neural network that consists of a shallow parameterized quantum circuit, measurements, and a classical neural network. The parameterized quantum circuit performs a nonlocal transformation of the measurement basis, which is jointly trained with the classical neural network to maximize the statistical distance between data obtained by measuring different quantum states. Using supervised learning, we demonstrate that the hybrid neural network distinguishes the topological phase of the surface code from a symmetry-enriched topological phase and random product states. Moreover, this hybrid neural network reduces both inference and training sample complexities of recognizing the topological phase by approximately one order of magnitude compared to a classical neural network trained on randomized Pauli measurements. As this hybrid neural network features a shallow quantum circuit that can be readily implemented on existing quantum computers, it enables the efficient characterization of complex quantum states.

### [117] [Diameter truncated operator evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28313)
*Tom Holden-Dye,Max Marvell,Joel Mills,Christoper J. Turner,Arijeet Pal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于算符直径（operator diameter）截断的模拟方法，用于高效计算非平衡量子系统中的局域关联函数与输运性质。该方法在Pauli弦基展开中根据算符在格点上支撑区域的尺寸进行截断，并通过数值模拟（ kicked Ising模型与Heisenberg XXZ模型）验证了其有效性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡量子系统中的算符动力学复杂度增长迅速，导致精确模拟通常不可行。近年来的进展表明，将模拟截断至低权重（low-weight）可观测量（即Pauli弦基展开中非平凡项数较少）在许多场景下是良好近似，但仍需更高效的截断方案。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于算符直径（operator diameter）的截断协议——即根据算符在格点（lattice）上非平凡支撑区域的尺寸进行截断，而非传统的基于权重（weight）的截断。利用通用量子线路的现有分析论证了该协议的物理动机，并在 kicked Ising模型与Heisenberg XXZ模型中进行了广泛的数值模拟。

Result: 数值结果表明，基于直径的截断协议是有效的，能够高效且准确地提取局域关联函数（local correlation functions）与输运性质（transport properties）。该方案相比传统低权重截断更为精简（leaner）。

Conclusion: 基于算符直径的截断协议在物理上是合理且高效的，为模拟非平衡量子系统中的动力学提供了一种实用的近似方法，尤其适用于局域可观测量与输运行为的计算。

Abstract: We present a method for simulating operator dynamics in out-of-equilibrium quantum systems. Due to the rapid growth of complexity in these systems, this is typically speaking an intractable task. However, exceptional progress has been made in recent years to sidestep this barrier, with the introduction of a number of methods that make use of a truncation of the simulation to low-weight (the number of non-trivial terms in a Pauli string basis expansion) observables, which turns out to be a good approximation for many dynamical quantities of interest, e.g., two-point infinite-temperature correlation functions between local operators. In this work, we extend this idea to a leaner truncation protocol, truncating operators based on their diameter - that is, the size of the region on the lattice on which they are non-trivially supported. Using existing analysis for generic circuits we argue that this kind of truncation protocol is physically well-motivated, and show via extensive numerical simulations for a number of systems of interest (here, the kicked Ising model and the Heisenberg XXZ model) that it is effective, and allows us to efficiently and accurately extract local correlation functions and transport properties.

</details>

### [118] [Multiplicity dependence of the size of the common hadron emission source in pp collisions at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28098)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ALICE探测器在LHC采集的$\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV质子-质子（pp）对撞数据（积分亮度$19.3$ pb$^{-1}$），首次同时测量了强子发射源尺寸对多重数和横向质量（$m_{\rm T}$）的依赖关系。通过多种核子-核子（nucleon-nucleon）相互作用模型提取源半径，结果稳健一致，并与铅-铅（Pb-Pb）碰撞结果对比，揭示了粒子发射动力学的系统尺寸依赖性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用费曼图分析（femtoscopic analysis）研究质子-质子（pp）对撞中强子产生的机制，特别是精确测量强子发射源（hadron-emitting source）的尺寸，这是利用费曼学（femtoscopy）研究强子间剩余强相互作用（residual strong interaction）的关键前提。

Method: 基于ALICE探测器在2022年升级后采集的$\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV最小偏差（minimum bias）质子-质子（pp）对撞数据，积分亮度为$19.3$ pb$^{-1}$。通过测量质子-质子（proton-proton）关联函数，并采用多种核子-核子（nucleon-nucleon）相互作用模型提取源半径（source radius）。

Result: 首次同时测量了源尺寸对多重数（multiplicity）和横向质量（transverse-mass, $m_{\rm T}$）的依赖关系。不同相互作用模型下提取的源半径具有一致性，表明测量对相互作用模型假设是稳健的。与$\sqrt{s}=5.02$ TeV铅-铅（Pb-Pb）碰撞结果对比，在相似$m_{\rm T}$区间内观察到显著不同的多重数依赖性。

Conclusion: 该测量为理解粒子发射动力学（particle emission dynamics）的系统尺寸依赖性（system-size dependence）提供了新见解，并为利用费曼学（femtoscopy）研究LHC上稳定和不稳定强子间的剩余强相互作用提供了精确的源尺寸基准。

Abstract: Femtoscopic analysis can shed light on hadron production in pp collisions. In this paper, proton-proton correlations measured in collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV recorded with the ALICE detector at the LHC are presented. The analysis is based on the minimum bias dataset collected in 2022 following the upgrade of the ALICE detector and corresponds to an integrated luminosity of $19.3$ pb$^{-1}$. The increased integrated luminosity allows us, for the first time, to simultaneously measure the multiplicity and transverse-mass ($m_{\rm T}$) dependence of the size of the hadron-emitting source. Precise knowledge of the femtoscopic source size in pp collisions is a crucial ingredient for using femtoscopy to study the residual strong interaction among stable and unstable hadrons at the LHC. In this light, the source radius was determined from the measured correlation functions by assuming several state-of-the-art models of the nucleon$-$nucleon interactions. The consistency among the extracted radii demonstrates the robustness of the measurement with respect to interaction model assumptions. A comparison to femtoscopic radii measured in Pb$-$Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s}=5.02$ TeV reveals a markedly different multiplicity dependence in similar $m_{\rm T}$ intervals, providing new insight into the system-size dependence of particle emission dynamics.

### [119] [Impact of neutrino-electron scattering and an improved treatment of pair processes on binary neutron star mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27425)
*Francois Foucart,Samantha Rath,Rowan Davidson,Patrick Chi-Kit Cheong,Matthew D. Duez,Lawrence Kidder,Harald Pfeiffer,Mark Scheel*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过改进的蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）中微子输运算法，在保持计算成本不显著增加的前提下，将中微子非弹性散射与中微子-反中微子对湮灭过程纳入双中子星并合模拟，发现重轻子中微子的平均能量和总光度降低，抛射质量增加约50%。此外，通过改变双星总质量，发现抛射物质、流出的几何与成分随总质量发生快速变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多信使观测中子星并合是约束致密物质性质与重核素生产场所的独特机会，而模拟所需的电磁信号模型受限于近似中微子物理的使用。

Method: 采用改进的蒙特卡罗输运算法（Monte Carlo transport algorithm），允许根据模拟的中微子能量分布实时计算反应率（包括阻塞因子），但对中微子角分布仍采用近似处理；在此基础上，将中微子与电子的非弹性散射（inelastic scattering）以及中微子-反中微子对湮灭（neutrino-antineutrino pair annihilation）纳入模拟。

Result: 在不增加计算成本的情况下，添加单个包络可使角度积分分布函数变化Δf_ν<1，但代价是流体耦合的散粒噪声增加。引入非弹性散射和改进的对过程后，重轻子中微子的平均能量和总光度降低，抛射质量增加约50%（总抛射质量<0.005M⊙）。改变双星总质量（远离瞬塌阈值）时，抛射物质、流出物的几何与成分随总质量快速变化。

Conclusion: 改进的输运方案能够更精细地研究并合残余中微子的能谱，揭示了中微子微观过程对抛射物质性质的显著影响，以及系统总质量对流出物几何与成分的敏感调控作用。

Abstract: Multimessenger observations of neutron star mergers are unique opportunities to constrain the properties of dense matter and the production site of heavy nuclei. To leverage these observations, we require reliable models of the electromagnetic signals powered by mergers. An important limitation to our ability to develop such models is the use of approximate neutrino physics in simulations. Here, we present simulations using an improved version of our Monte Carlo transport algorithm specifically designed to allow for more advanced on-the-fly calculations of reaction rates that use the simulated energy distribution of neutrinos, including in blocking factors, while still relying on approximations for the angular distribution of neutrinos. We use these new methods to include in simulations inelastic scattering of neutrinos on electrons, and to improve our treatment of neutrino-antineutrino pair annihilation. We find that, without increasing the cost of simulations, we can marginally get to the point when the addition of a single packet represents a change $Δf_ν<1$ in the angle-integrated distribution function, at the cost of increased shot noise in the coupling to the fluid. With inelastic scattering and a better treatment of pair processes, we find a reduction in the average energy and total luminosity of heavy-lepton neutrinos, and an increase in the amount of mass ejected -- here by $50\%$, although on a relatively low amount of total ejected mass $<0.005M_\odot$. In a separate set of simulations varying the total mass of the binary away from its prompt collapse threshold, we find rapid variations in the amount of ejected matter and in the geometry and composition of the outflows with the total mass of the system. Finally, we use the simulations with our more advanced transport scheme to study in more detail the energy spectrum of neutrinos across the merger remnant.

### [120] [Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals in Light of Quasi-periodic Eruptions: Milli-Hertz Gravitational Wave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27661)
*Brennen Black,Xian Chen,Zhen Pan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文基于准周期喷发（QPEs）的盘碰撞模型，计算了恒星质量极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）和黑洞EMRIs的基准发生率，并评估了二者对LISA频段随机引力波背景（SGWB）的贡献，发现仅黑洞EMRIs在1-10毫赫兹频段内对LISA可分辨信号有显著贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用QPEs作为圆轨道EMRIs的示踪物，推断EMRI的形成率并估计其对LISA频段SGWB的贡献，从而厘清次天体是恒星质量黑洞还是主序星这一争议问题。

Method: 采用QPEs的盘碰撞模型（disk-collision model），分别针对恒星EMRIs（stellar EMRIs）和黑洞EMRIs（black hole EMRIs）推导基准发生率，并估算两者对SGWB的贡献。

Result: 恒星EMRIs的基准发生率为每星系每年2.88×10⁻⁶，黑洞EMRIs为每星系每年6.07×10⁻⁶；仅黑洞EMRIs对LISA可分辨的1-10毫赫兹频段有贡献，其信号强度可从略低于LISA灵敏度曲线到高出约两个数量级；恒星EMRIs在进入1-10毫赫兹频段前已因潮汐瓦解，仅贡献亚毫赫兹频率且低于LISA灵敏度曲线。

Conclusion: QPEs的盘碰撞模型支持黑洞EMRIs作为LISA频段SGWB的潜在重要来源，而恒星EMRIs的贡献在LISA可探测范围内可忽略；两类EMRIs的发生率及引力波贡献存在系统性不确定度。

Abstract: Quasi-periodic eruptions (QPEs) are repeated X-ray bursts originating in galactic nuclei. Of the many proposed models, the favored model is the disk-collision model in which a stellar mass orbiter collides with a disk formed from a tidal disruption event, generating flares twice per orbit. In this model QPEs are tracers of circular extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs) and can be used to infer the EMRI formation rate and estimate their contribution to the stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) in the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) band. Whether the secondary is a stellar-mass black hole or a main sequence star is still debated and leads to different results for the EMRI rate and SGWB. We obtain fiducial rates -- subject to systematic uncertainties -- of $R_{\rm SE} = 2.88\times10^{-6}$ per galaxy per year for stellar EMRIs and $R_{\rm BHE} = 6.07\times10^{-6}$ per galaxy per year for black hole EMRIs, then estimate their contribution to the SGWB. We find that only black hole EMRIs contribute to the 1 - 10 milliHertz band resolvable by LISA, and depending on the secondary mass and formation radius can contribute from just below the LISA sensitivity curve to roughly two orders of magnitude above it. Stellar EMRIs, being tidally disrupted before reaching the 1 - 10 milliHertz band, only contribute to sub-milliHertz frequencies and remain below the LISA sensitivity curve.

</details>


### [121] [Continuation of Force-Free Electrodynamics upon the loss of magnetic dominance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28317)
*Morifumi Mizuno*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出在无力电动力学（FFE）失去磁主导条件后，可用零场（null field）理论替代它，该理论将场约束为满足零几何条件且漂移速度积分曲线为直线。在一维PIC模拟中，FFE结合零延续（null continuation）方法在宏观层面与模拟结果高度一致，包括零区域（null region）的生成演化与电流片（current sheet）的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无力电动力学（Force-Free Electrodynamics, FFE）在磁主导等离子体中是有效的，但一旦失去磁主导条件（即 $F^{ab}F_{ab}>0$ 不再成立），其双曲性丧失，原有方程失效。因此需要寻找一个在磁主导丧失后仍然有效的替代理论。

Method: 提出零场（null field）理论，其核心条件为 $F^{ab}F_{ab}=0=F^{ab}\tilde{F}_{ab}$，且场的主零方向（principal null direction）与测地线汇（geodesic congruence）相切。在平直时空下等价于 $\vec{B}^2-\vec{E}^2=0=\vec{E}\cdot\vec{B}$，且漂移速度 $\vec{E}\times\vec{B}/\vec{B}^{2}$ 的积分曲线为直线。通过一维PIC（Particle-in-Cell）模拟平面对称Alfvén波碰撞进行测试，并用该理论分析Adhikari的type-changing精确解。

Result: FFE结合零延续（null continuation）在宏观层面与PIC模拟结果高度一致，成功再现了零区域（null region）的诞生与演化以及电流片（current sheet）的形成。在Adhikari的type-changing解中亦取得宏观一致结果。

Conclusion: 零场理论可作为FFE在磁主导丧失后的有效延续，能够在宏观尺度上描述磁主导等离子体中零区域的形成和电流片演化，与PIC模拟定性一致。

Abstract: Force-Free Electrodynamics (FFE) describes the evolution of the electromagnetic field in magnetically dominated plasmas, but ceases to be hyperbolic once the magnetic dominance condition $F^{ab}F_{ab}>0$ is lost. We demonstrate that, after the loss of magnetic dominance, FFE may be replaced by a theory of null fields, $F^{ab}F_{ab}=0=F^{ab}\tilde{F}_{ab}$, characterized by the condition that its principal null direction is tangent to a geodesic congruence. In flat spacetime, this theory may be equivalently stated as the condition that the field satisfies $\vec{B}^2-\vec{E}^2=0=\vec{E}\cdot\vec{B}$ and the integral curves of the drift velocity $\vec{E}\times\vec{B}/\vec{B}^{2}$ are straight lines. We develop the general structure and the properties of this theory and test it against 1D PIC simulations using the collision of planar symmetric Alfvén waves. We find that the force-free combined with the null continuation shows remarkable macroscopic agreement with PIC simulations, including the birth and evolution of the null region ($F^{ab}F_{ab}=0$) and the formation of a current sheet. As an independent test, we apply the null continuation to Adhikari's type-changing solution, an exact FFE solution exhibiting finite-time loss of magnetic dominance, and also find macroscopic agreement with 1D PIC simulations.

</details>

### [122] [Porosity Effects on Cyclic Gas Invasion and Trapping in Deformable Porous Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28003)
*Haiyi Zhong,Jieting Long,Xiangyu Ding,Zhongzheng Wang,Yixiang Gan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过准二维Hele-Shaw池中软水凝胶颗粒的实验，研究了不同初始孔隙率下可变形多孔介质（deformable porous media）中气-液多相流的行为，揭示了孔隙率对气体侵入压力、入侵模式、压力波动及残余气体捕获（gas trapping）的系统性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可变形多孔介质中的流体输运是许多生物物理和地球物理过程的核心。尽管已有大量研究，但循环注入过程中孔隙率（porosity）如何控制可变形系统中的流体行为仍不清楚。

Method: 在填充软水凝胶颗粒的准二维Hele-Shaw池中，以不同初始孔隙率进行交替气体和水注入实验，结合高分辨率成像和连续压力监测，量化气体动力学和压力演化。

Result: 气体进入压力随孔隙率降低而增加，符合基于有效孔喉宽度（effective pore-throat width）的杨-拉普拉斯估计（Young-Laplace estimation）。入侵模式从高孔隙率下的腔主导膨胀（cavity-dominated expansion）转变为低孔隙率下的局部孔隙入侵（localised pore invasion），中间孔隙率出现混合腔-指进（mixed cavity-fingering） regime。低孔隙率产生频繁小振幅压降，高孔隙率产生更离散的压力松弛。残余气体饱和度（residual gas saturation）随注入循环增加而上升，低孔隙率下终值更高。比界面长度（Specific interfacial length）与气体团簇尺寸呈幂律关系（power-law relationship），标度指数（scaling exponent）随孔隙率降低和循环进行而减小。

Conclusion: 可变形多孔介质中的气体捕获依赖于初始堆积结构和循环演化的气-固相互作用。该研究为解释重复气体注入过程中孔隙率依赖的捕获与再侵入（reinvasion）提供了见解。

Abstract: Fluid transport in deformable porous media is central to many biophysical and geophysical processes. While extensive studies exist, how porosity governs fluid behaviour in deformable systems during cyclic injection remains elusive. Here, we investigate gas-liquid multiphase flow in a quasi-2D Hele-Shaw cell packed with soft hydrogel particles at different initial porosities. Alternative gas and water injection experiments, combined with high-resolution imaging and continuous pressure monitoring, are used to quantify gas dynamics and pressure evolution. Results show that the gas entry pressure increases as porosity decreases, consistent with a Young-Laplace estimation based on effective pore-throat width. After entry, invasion shifts from cavity-dominated expansion in high porosity packings to localised pore invasion in low porosity packings, with a mixed cavity-fingering regime at intermediate porosity. Pressure fluctuations are linked to pore-scale gas escape and internal gas redistribution. Low porosity packings produce frequent small-amplitude pressure drops, whereas higher porosity packings produce more discrete pressure relaxations. Across cycles, the decreasing mean pressure suggests preferential-pathway reuse and reduced local capillary constraints. Residual gas saturation increases systematically with injection cycles and reaches higher terminal values as porosity decreases. Specific interfacial length increases as available pore space decreases and follows a power-law relationship with gas cluster size, with scaling exponent decreases as porosity decreases and cycling progresses. Together, these results demonstrate that gas trapping in deformable porous media depends on both initial packing structure and cyclically evolving gas-solid interactions. This study provides insights for interpreting porosity-dependent trapping and reinvasion during repeated gas injection.

</details>


### [123] [Universality of Bubble Coalescence in Electrolytic Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28181)
*Afsal Chakkam Palliyalil,Gaurav Tomar,Susmita Dash*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验揭示了电解液中气泡聚并（bubble coalescence）过程中液膜排液（thin film drainage）的三个阶段机制，发现液膜形态对排液的影响强于界面边界条件（如 Marangoni 应力），且电解液效应仅通过重整化时间尺度（renormalize timescales）影响动力学，而不改变其普适性规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电解液中的气泡聚并现象在矿物浮选、电化学能量转换等技术中具有重要应用，但其控制物理机制尚未明确，尤其是 Marangoni 应力如何通过调控界面迁移率（interfacial mobility）影响聚并时间的问题存在长期争议。

Method: 实验测量了气泡聚并过程中液膜厚度随时间的变化，通过观察不同电解液类型和浓度下的薄膜排液行为，识别出三个特征阶段，并利用特征膜厚与时间尺度对数据进行无量纲化缩放（rescaling）分析。

Result: 液膜排液经历三个阶段：初始黏弹性阶段（visco-capillary stage）呈幂律（power-law）减薄；随后由于边缘稳定化（rim stabilisation）作用，膜厚呈指数衰减；最后受分离压（disjoining pressure）支配，膜厚指数松弛至平衡厚度。不同电解液类型和浓度下的数据经缩放后均坍塌至同一曲线，呈现普适行为。

Conclusion: 液膜形态对排液的决定性作用强于界面边界条件；电解液效应仅重整化时间尺度，不改变排液的根本动力学机制。该结论解决了关于 Marangoni 应力影响的长期争论，并为相关技术中的气泡行为调控提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Bubble coalescence phenomenon in electrolytic media finds applications in technologies from mineral flotation to electrochemical energy conversion. However, the underlying governing physics still remains unresolved, with longstanding disagreement over the extent to which Marangoni stresses affect the coalescence time by modulating the interfacial mobility. Here, we show that the thin film morphology governs drainage more strongly than the interfacial boundary conditions. We demonstrate experimentally that thin film drainage during bubble coalescence proceeds through three distinct regimes. An initial visco-capillary stage that exhibits a power-law thinning, followed by an exponential decrease in film thickness with time induced by rim stabilisation. The final regime is governed by disjoining pressure and is marked by an exponential relaxation of the film to the equilibrium thickness. We show that, irrespective of the electrolyte type and concentration, film evolution exhibits universal behavior by collapsing onto a single curve when rescaled with the characteristic film thickness and time scale, demonstrating that electrolyte effects act only to renormalize timescales rather than alter the underlying dynamics.

</details>


### [124] [Entropy density functional theory for inhomogeneous fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28240)
*Matthias Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种精确变分方案（exact variational scheme），用于处理非均匀经典流体的热平衡统计力学问题，通过联合元密度最小化原理（joint metadensity minimization）绕过二体密度计算，并引入普适过剩熵泛函（universal excess entropy functional），在保持计算简洁性的同时完整描述多体关联效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非均匀经典流体理论需要求解复杂的非均匀二体密度（inhomogeneous two-body density），计算成本高且难以推广。本文旨在构建一种绕过二体密度、保持计算简洁性（computationally simple）的精确变分框架。

Method: 证明了一个联合元密度最小化原理，同时优化单体密度（one-body density）和全局粒子间距离分布（global interparticle distance distribution）；引入一个普适的过剩熵泛函（excess entropy functional）来描述任意成对相互作用系统（arbitrary pairwise interacting systems）中的所有多体关联（many-body correlations）。

Result: 该理论绕过了非均匀二体密度，因此保持了计算上的简单性；同时，该方法与神经函子机器学习（neural functional machine learning）、软物质设计（soft matter design）以及通过熵测试粒子（entropic test-particle）和元-Ornstein-Zernike（meta-Ornstein-Zernike）路径预测结构关联函数具有相关性。

Conclusion: 该精确变分框架为非均匀经典流体平衡态物理提供了一种兼顾理论完整性与计算效率的新路径，并在机器学习、软物质设计与结构预测领域展现出潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We present an exact variational scheme for the physics of inhomogeneous classical fluids in thermal equilibrium. A joint metadensity minimization principle is proven for the one-body density and the global interparticle distance distribution. The theory bypasses the inhomogeneous two-body density and thus remains computationally simple. A universal excess entropy functional accounts for all many-body correlations in arbitrary pairwise interacting systems. The framework is relevant for neural functional machine learning, for soft matter design, and for predicting structural correlation functions via entropic test-particle and meta-Ornstein-Zernike routes.

</details>

### [125] [Superoscillatory initial states during inflation: theory, CMB constraints, and prospects for galaxy clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25133)
*Ali Nayeri*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文构建了暴胀过程中超振荡初始态（SIS）的边界作用量实现，证明量子干涉可在带限初始波泛函中产生具有快速缠绕相位的谱局域Bogoliubov激发，并系统分析了该特征在CMB角功率谱、极化、双谱及星系成团性观测中的可观测印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，暴胀初始态的量子干涉效应大多以唯象方式引入，缺乏从第一性原理出发的、可显式计算并直接约束的可实现模型。作者希望构造一个基于边界作用量的具体框架，使超振荡初始态（superoscillatory initial states for inflation）的谱特征由参数(a, N)内生确定，而非人为设定。

Method: 在初始时间面上引入一个二次边界项，导出Bogoliubov系数与对应的原初曲率谱；通过投影计算超振荡特征在CMB角功率谱中的响应，并利用CAMB进行完整数值验证；基于Planck 2018 TT数据，采用匹配滤波（matched-filter）方法给出参数λ的约束边界；进一步推导极化与双谱（bispectrum）的关联预言，并与普通激发态模型进行比较。

Result: CMB投影中的传递函数（transfer-function）涂抹效应会强烈抑制超振荡的振荡成分；CAMB数值计算表明，简单的高斯近似会高估峰值信号约三倍。基于Planck 2018 TT数据，在第一个声峰附近（k_* = 1.45×10^(-2) Mpc^(-1)，Δk/k_* = 0.05）得到匹配滤波约束λ ≲ 0.05。星系成团性（galaxy clustering）因保留完整的振荡结构，成为比CMB投影更为灵敏的探测手段。

Conclusion: 该框架为初始态量子干涉如何在宇宙学可观测量上留下印记提供了一种具体且可检验的实现路径；SIS模型在结构约束上可区别于一般的激发态模型，并具备多探针联合检验的潜力。

Abstract: We construct an explicit boundary-action realization of superoscillatory initial states (SIS) for inflation, in which quantum interference within a band-limited initial wavefunctional generates a spectrally localized Bogoliubov excitation with a rapidly winding phase. Starting from a quadratic boundary term on the initial time surface, we derive the Bogoliubov coefficients and the resulting primordial curvature spectrum, obtaining a localized oscillatory feature fixed by the superoscillatory parameters $(a,N)$ rather than imposed phenomenologically. We compute the projection of this feature onto CMB angular power spectra and show that transfer-function smearing strongly suppresses the oscillatory component; full CAMB calculations confirm the qualitative effect and show that a simple Gaussian approximation overestimates the peak signal by about a factor of three. Using Planck 2018 TT data, we obtain an indicative matched-filter bound $λ\lesssim 0.05$ for a representative feature centered near the first acoustic peak, $Δk/k_* = 0.05$ at $k_* = 1.45\times 10^{-2}\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. We further derive correlated predictions for polarization and the bispectrum, identify structural constraints that distinguish SIS from generic excited-state models, and show that galaxy clustering provides a qualitatively more powerful probe because it preserves the full oscillatory structure that CMB projection suppresses. This framework provides a concrete and testable realization of how initial-state quantum interference can imprint itself on cosmological observables.

</details>

*Alexander C. Jenkins,Diego Blas,Joshua W. Foster*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究利用平方公里阵列天文台（SKAO）对毫秒脉冲双星进行高精度计时，通过探测引力波对双星轨道的共振扰动，在微赫兹频段搜索引力波，有望实现对这一频段前所未有的灵敏度并探测大质量黑洞双星。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波天文学在不同频段有望提供对宇宙的新认识，但目前微赫兹（μHz）频段的探测能力有限，亟需发展新的搜索方法。

Method: 利用SKAO对毫秒脉冲双星（binary millisecond pulsars）进行高精度计时，通过检测引力波对双星轨道的共振扰动（resonant gravitational-wave perturbations）来搜索微赫兹频段的引力波。

Result: 仅利用少数已知的脉冲双星系统，SKAO即可实现对微赫兹引力波前所未有的探测灵敏度，能够探测该频段内正在旋进的大质量黑洞双星（inspiralling massive black hole binaries）。

Conclusion: 该方法与传统脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array）分析互补，为SKAO的引力波科学研究增加了新的维度。

Abstract: The gravitational-wave sky is expected to contain a rich variety of sources across a very broad range of frequencies. Much like in electromagnetic astronomy, exploring new gravitational-wave frequency bands therefore has the potential to unlock powerful new insights into the Universe. In this chapter, we investigate the prospects for using high-precision timing of binary millisecond pulsars with the Square Kilometre Array Observatory (SKAO) to search for gravitational waves in the microhertz ($μ$Hz) frequency band by targeting resonant gravitational-wave perturbations to the orbits of these binaries. Using only a handful of known systems, we show that SKAO observations can achieve unprecedented sensitivity to microhertz gravitational waves, with the potential to detect inspiralling massive black hole binaries in this band. These searches are complementary to conventional pulsar timing array analyses, adding a new dimension to the gravitational-wave science achievable with the SKAO.

### [127] [UV artefacts in ultra-slow-roll models of inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28005)
*Gerald Barnert,Laura Iacconi,Hooshyar Assadullahi,Kazuya Koyama,David Wands*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了单场暴胀（single-field inflation）中利用解析哈勃流参数化（Hubble-flow parametrisation）建模瞬态非吸引子相（如超慢滚）的物理一致性，发现该参数化会引入尖锐的紫外（UV）赝结构，并通过离散傅里叶变换滤波证明其破坏了模型的物理鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单场暴胀框架下，原初黑洞（primordial black hole）和标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational wave）的产生通常需要增强的原初扰动，这往往要求一个瞬态非吸引子相（transient non-attractor phase），例如超慢滚（ultra-slow roll）。然而，解析哈勃流参数化在建模此类场景时的物理一致性尚未得到充分检验。

Method: 通过重建底层标量场势（scalar field potential），检验慢滚参数（slow-roll parameters）中平滑过渡所隐藏的高阶导数尖锐尖峰；引入基于离散傅里叶变换（discrete Fourier transform）的紫外滤波（UV-filtering）程序，系统性地抑制场空间中的高频模式，以评估这些结构的影响。

Result: 即使慢滚参数中的过渡看似平滑，哈勃流参数化在势的高阶导数中仍隐藏着尖锐的局域化尖峰（sharp localized spikes），这在解析势中通常不存在。紫外滤波能有效移除哈勃流导出势中的尖锐特征，使得滤波后的模型在从超慢滚演化回慢滚时，通常满足Wands对偶不变性（Wands duality invariance）。

Conclusion: 哈勃流参数化引入的虚假紫外效应可能影响非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）和圈修正（loop contributions）等可观测量的预测。因此，简单解析哈勃流参数化用于建模包含瞬态非吸引子相的暴胀模型的鲁棒性值得怀疑。

Abstract: Within single-field inflation, primordial black hole and scalar-induced gravitational wave production from enhanced primordial perturbations typically requires a transient non-attractor phase, such as ultra-slow roll. We investigate the physical consistency of modeling such scenarios through analytical Hubble-flow parametrisation. By reconstructing the underlying scalar field potential, we show that even slow transitions in the slow-roll parameters can hide sharp, localised spikes in higher-order derivatives of the potential at the transition from ultra-slow-roll to slow-roll. These are typically not found in analytic potentials. To evaluate the impact of these structures, we implement a UV-filtering procedure based on discrete Fourier transform to systematically suppress high frequency modes in field space in both classes of models. We find that the filter effectively removes sharp features in Hubble-flow-derived potentials. As a consequence, we show that UV-filtered models typically respect Wands duality invariance as the field evolves back from ultra-slow roll to slow roll. Beyond linear perturbation theory, the introduction of spurious UV effects might affect other observables, such as non-Gaussianity and loop contributions. Our results thereby question the robustness of simple analytical Hubble-flow parametrisation for modeling inflationary models with a transient non-attractor phase.

</details>


### [128] [The effect of dark energy on the void-halo perpendicular alignments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28151)
*Geonwoo Kang,Jounghun Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过AbacusSummit模拟套件，在10种不同暗能量状态方程（equation of state）的宇宙学模型中发现，暗能量的压强越负、演化越剧烈，空洞表面（void surface）的星系晕会更强地垂直于指向空洞中心的方向排列。研究利用一个修正线性扰动理论（linear perturbation theory）得到的单参数解析公式拟合数值结果，并排除质量与球形度分布的干扰后，检测到暗能量对垂直排列强度的净效应，进而提出一个双线性模型（bilinear model）来刻画该效应，最终论证这种垂直排列可作为暗能量动力学性质的独立指示器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究暗能量（dark energy）的动力学性质是否会在空洞表面星系晕的形态排列中留下可观测的信号，从而为约束暗能量状态方程提供一种新的、独立于传统探针的几何与统计手段。

Method: 基于AbacusSummit模拟套件（包含1个Planck ΛCDM、4个wCDM和5个w₀wₐCDM宇宙学模型，初始条件相同但暗能量状态方程不同），在红移z=0.1处识别空洞（voids）及其表面的星系晕。计算星系晕形状轴（shape axes）与指向空洞中心方向之间夹角余弦的概率密度函数p(cosθ)，并用一个通过经验修正线性扰动理论得到的单参数公式拟合该分布。通过消除不同宇宙学间星系晕质量与球形度分布差异造成的假信号，提取净效应。

Result: 暗能量的压强更负且演化更快的宇宙学中，参数dₜ（描述垂直排列强度）取更高值。不同宇宙学间的dₜ差异可由一个关于w=−1与w≠−1情况的双线性模型精确描述。验证表明，该双线性关系与数值结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 空洞表面星系晕的垂直排列在原理上可作为暗能量动力学性质的一个强有力的独立指示器（independent indicator），为未来通过星系团与空洞结构约束暗能量状态方程提供了新的观测途径。

Abstract: We report a numerical discovery that in a more rapidly accelerating spacetime, the galactic halos on void surfaces develop stronger perpendicular alignments with the directions toward the void centers. We utilize the halo catalogs from the AbacusSummit suite of simulations for $10$ different cosmologies that include one Planck $Λ$CDM, four $w$CDM and five $w_{0}w_{a}$CDM, which share the identical initial conditions except for the dark energy equation of state. For each cosmology, we identify the voids and void-surface galactic halos at $z=0.1$ and determine the probability density functions of the cosines of the angles, $p(\cosθ)$, between the shape axes of void-surface galactic halos and the directions toward the void centers. The numerically obtained $p(\cosθ)$ is fitted to an analytic single-parameter formula derived through an empirical modification of the linear perturbation theory. Eliminating spurious signals caused by the differences in the mass and sphericity distributions of void-surface galactic halos among different cosmologies, we detect a clear net effect of dark energy on the strengths of the perpendicular alignments of void-surface galactic halos, quantified by the single parameter, $d_{t}$. Noting that $d_{t}$ has higher values in the cosmologies where dark energy has more negative pressure and evolves more rapidly, we put forth a bilinear model for the difference in $d_{t}$ between the two cases of $w=-1$ and $w\ne -1$. Demonstrating that this bilinear relation excellently describes the numerical results, we conclude that the perpendicular alignments of void-surface galactic halos should in principle be a powerful independent indicator of the dynamic nature of dark energy.

</details>


### [129] [HIcosmo: a differentiable JAX-based framework for cosmology inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28175)
*Jing-Zhao Qi,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文介绍 HIcosmo，一个基于 JAX 的开源宇宙学推断框架，通过自动微分（automatic differentiation）和即时编译（just-in-time compilation）实现高效的后验采样与 Fisher 预测，其采样吞吐量较 Cobaya 提升约 8.7 倍（CPU），GPU 加速最高可达 20 倍，并在多种巡天数据中完成验证与联合约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 第四阶段宇宙学巡天（Stage IV cosmological surveys），如 Euclid、LSST、DESI 和 SKA，将产生空前规模的观测数据，亟需高效且可靠的推断工具来处理日益增长的计算需求。

Method: HIcosmo 基于 JAX 构建，所有前向模型（forward model）、距离积分（distance integrals）、似然评估（likelihood evaluations）、后验采样（posterior sampling）和 Fisher 预测（Fisher forecasts）均由 JAX 原语实现；对数似然的梯度和 Hessian 矩阵通过自动微分直接计算，无需有限差分近似。框架支持 ΛCDM、wCDM、w₀wₐCDM 及相互作用暗能量（interacting dark-energy）模型，并提供多种巡天似然函数；其范围限于背景宇宙学（background cosmology），玻尔兹曼求解器（Boltzmann solvers）与完整扰动层次似然交由外部工具处理。

Result: HIcosmo 在验证中与各似然函数的参考实现及 Cobaya 高度一致，χ² 绝对差异在 10⁻⁶–10⁻² 之间，边际约束差异小于 0.2σ。端到端采样吞吐量在 CPU 上约为 Cobaya 的 8.7 倍，GPU 加速相对 CPU 最高可达 20 倍。作为应用，给出了多探针 ΛCDM 联合约束、暗能量状态方程（equation-of-state）约束，以及六个 21 cm 强度映射巡天（包括 SKA1、MeerKAT、BINGO、天籁（Tianlai）和 CHIME）的 Fisher 预测。

Conclusion: HIcosmo 是一个开源、高效、基于 JAX 的宇宙学推断框架，通过自动微分和即时编译在大规模数据场景下实现了显著的性能提升，验证结果与现有基准高度一致，可有效支持第四阶段宇宙学巡天的推断需求。

Abstract: The Stage IV cosmological surveys, such as Euclid, LSST, DESI, and SKA, will deliver observational data of unprecedented volume, calling for efficient and reliable inference tools. This paper presents HIcosmo (High-performance Inference for Cosmology), an open-source JAX-based framework for cosmology inference. In HIcosmo, the forward model, distance integrals, likelihood evaluations, posterior sampling, and Fisher forecasts are all built from JAX primitives, so that gradients and Hessians of the log-likelihood are obtained directly by automatic differentiation, without any finite-difference approximation. The framework implements the $Λ$CDM, $w$CDM, $w_0 w_a$CDM, and interacting dark-energy models, and provides likelihoods for Type Ia supernovae (Pantheon+, DES-SN5YR, Union3), baryon acoustic oscillations (DESI DR1/DR2, SDSS), Planck 2018 distance priors, local $H_0$ measurements, and strong-lensing time delays. Its scope is restricted to background cosmology, with Boltzmann solvers and full perturbation-level likelihoods left to external tools. We validate HIcosmo against the reference implementation of each likelihood and against Cobaya. $χ^2$ values agree to absolute differences of $10^{-6}$-$10^{-2}$, and the marginalized constraints from the two codes differ by less than $0.2σ$ in every analysis tested. Leveraging just-in-time compilation and automatic differentiation, HIcosmo achieves about $8.7\times$ the end-to-end sampling throughput of Cobaya on CPU. As the dataset grows to survey scale, GPU acceleration over CPU reaches up to $20\times$. As applications, we present multi-probe $Λ$CDM joint constraints, dark-energy equation-of-state constraints, and Fisher forecasts for six 21 cm intensity-mapping surveys, including SKA1, MeerKAT, BINGO, Tianlai, and CHIME.

</details>


### [130] [Cancellation of one-loop time dependence in superhorizon curvature perturbations from all scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28247)
*Keisuke Inomata*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明在空间平坦规范（spatially-flat gauge）下，超视界曲率扰动（superhorizon curvature perturbations）在单圈阶（one-loop level）具有守恒性。与以往工作不同，本文未假设圈积分波数k与功率谱波数q之间存在k≫q的层级关系，并明确包含了k≲q的贡献。通过使用δN形式论考虑暴胀子扰动与曲率扰动之间的非线性关系，证明了单圈曲率功率谱中表观的时间依赖性会被所有贡献（包括边界项）的一致组合所抵消。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前关于超视界曲率扰动在圈层次守恒性的研究通常假设了波数层级关系（k≫q），忽略了k≲q的贡献，从而无法全面检验曲率扰动的守恒性。

Method: 采用空间平坦规范（spatially-flat gauge）下的量子场论框架，计算包含所有尺度圈波数（包括k≲q区域）的单圈贡献；结合δN形式论处理暴胀子扰动与曲率扰动之间的非线性关系，并系统包含边界项（boundary terms）。

Result: 在包含所有尺度及边界项贡献的一致组合下，单圈曲率功率谱中表观的时间依赖性被完全抵消，表明超视界曲率扰动在单圈阶仍然是守恒的。

Conclusion: 空间平坦规范下单圈超视界曲率扰动的守恒性普遍成立，无需依赖k≫q的层级假设；δN形式论中边界项的合理纳入是确保守恒性的关键。

Abstract: We show the conservation of the superhorizon curvature perturbations at one-loop level in spatially-flat gauge, including contributions from loop wavenumbers on all scales. In contrast to previous works, we do not assume a hierarchy $k \gg q$ between the wavenumber of the loop integral, $k$, and that of the power spectrum, $q$, and we explicitly include the regime $k \lesssim q$. Taking into account the nonlinear relation between the inflaton fluctuation and the curvature perturbation with the $δN$ formalism, we show that the apparent time dependence of the one-loop curvature power spectrum cancels once all contributions, including boundary terms, are combined consistently.

### [131] [Memoirs of the curvaton: non-perturbative non-Gaussianity and supermassive primordial black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28296)
*S. Allegrini,A. J. Iovino,G. Perna,H. Veermäe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究超越标准二次势的 curvaton 动力学，构建了局部非高斯映射 $ζ=F(ζ_{\rm G})$，揭示了自相互作用通过修饰振荡起始时刻和有效状态方程产生非高斯性的机制，并将其应用于轴子类 curvaton 模型，证明强正非高斯性可在 COBE/FIRAS 限制下产生峰值振幅 $\mathcal{A}_{\rm pk}\sim10^{-5}$ 的原初超大质量黑洞种子，为 JWST 观测到的"小红点"提供新解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: curvaton 机制（curvaton mechanism）能够在暴胀后产生强非高斯（non-Gaussian）曲率扰动，对小尺度宇宙学具有重要潜在影响。然而，现有研究多局限于标准二次势（quadratic potential），缺乏对自相互作用（self-interactions）效应的系统理解。

Method: 采用缩减作用量（abbreviated action）方法，将冻结态（frozen regime）与振荡态（oscillatory regime）紧凑地连接起来。构建局部非高斯映射（local non-Gaussian map）$ζ=F(ζ_{\rm G})$，将曲率扰动与辅助高斯场（auxiliary Gaussian field）$ζ_{\rm G}$ 相关联。

Result: 对于二次势、单项式势（monomial potential）、四次势（quartic potential）和余弦势（cosine potential），推导出映射函数 $F(ζ_{\rm G})$。发现自相互作用可增强或抑制非高斯性，取决于势能形式和初始条件。在强非高斯区域，非高斯性可压制功率谱（power spectrum）。在底向上场景中，强正 curvaton 非高斯性产生峰值振幅 $\mathcal{A}_{\rm pk}\sim10^{-5}$ 的原初超大质量黑洞种子，与 COBE/FIRAS 的 $μ$ 畸变（$μ$-distortion）限制兼容。

Conclusion: 曲率扰动的自相互作用是产生强非高斯性的关键来源，超越标准二次势的 curvaton 动力学为原初超大质量黑洞种子提供可行的生成机制。轴子类 curvaton（axion-like curvaton）为这一机制提供了特别自然的实现框架，可解释 JWST 观测到的"小红点"（Little Red Dots）现象。

Abstract: The curvaton provides a simple mechanism for generating strongly non-Gaussian curvature perturbations after inflation, with potentially important consequences on small scales. We study curvaton dynamics beyond the standard quadratic potential and construct the local non-Gaussian map $ζ=F(ζ_{\rm G})$ relating the curvature perturbation to an auxiliary Gaussian field $ζ_{\rm G}$. Curvaton self-interactions make the onset of oscillations field dependent and modify the effective equation of state once the curvaton enters the adiabatic regime. We incorporate these effects using the abbreviated action, which provides a compact way to connect the frozen and oscillatory regimes and exposes sources of non-Gaussianity absent in the purely quadratic case. We apply the formalism to quadratic, monomial, quartic, and cosine potentials, for which we derive the mapping $F(ζ_{\rm G})$ and show that self-interactions can either enhance or suppress the resulting non-Gaussianity depending on the potential and initial conditions. We consider non-perturbative aspects in the strongly non-Gaussian regime, and show how strong non-Gaussianity can suppress the power spectrum. As an application, we provide a bottom-up scenario in which strongly positive curvaton non-Gaussianity allows primordial supermassive black hole seeds at peak amplitudes $\mathcal{A}_{\rm pk}\sim10^{-5}$, which are compatible with the COBE/FIRAS $μ$-distortion bounds. This opens a new primordial scenario for the Little Red Dots observed by the JWST. The axion-like curvaton provides a particularly natural setting for this mechanism.

### [132] [Active-Line Dynamics and Residual Work in a Reduced Oldroyd-B Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27606)
*Sai Peng*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究高魏森贝格数Oldroyd-B动力学约化得到的一维活性线方程，证明了正密度局部适定性、无破裂原理、小振荡全局稳定性、有限带宽弛豫及单尾替代方案，并建立了有限厚度抬升的残余功不等式，排除了某些活性线集中结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高魏森贝格数（high-Weissenberg number）下Oldroyd-B流体动力学在薄片约化机制中的行为，尤其是活性线方程的正密度解的存在性、稳定性及相关集中结构的可行性问题。

Method: 采用活性线方程（active-line equation）作为薄片约化机制，结合对数构型变量（log-conformation variables）A=exp(B)进行有限厚度抬升分析；通过残余功不等式（residual-work inequality）和紧致性提取（compactness extraction）论证结构排除。

Result: 证明了正密度局部适定性、无破裂原理、小振荡全局稳定性、有限带宽弛豫及单尾替代方案；推导出残余功不等式W_E ≤ (α/2) η_E L_E S_E，排除了残余功间隙为正的有限厚度活性线浓度结构。

Conclusion: 活性线方程在高魏森贝格数Oldroyd-B约化中具有良好数学性质，但某些集中结构因不满足残余功预算而被排除；二维非紧致性情景的紧致性定理仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: We study a one-dimensional active-line equation arising as a thin-sheet reduced mechanism for high-Weissenberg Oldroyd-B dynamics. The unknown is a positive periodic line density rho=m+eta satisfying rho_t+c rho Lambda rho-c(H rho)rho_s+gamma(rho-m)=0, where m>0 and Lambda=H partial_s. We prove positive-density local well-posedness, a no-rupture principle, small-oscillation global stability, finite-band relaxation, and a one-tail alternative for any remaining positive-density obstruction. We also separate the reduced scalar mechanism from the two-dimensional positive-cone Oldroyd-B admissibility problem. For finite-thickness lifts written in log-conformation variables A=exp(B), we prove the residual-work inequality W_E <= (alpha/2) eta_E L_E S_E, which excludes structured active-line lifts whose pressure-free work is too large relative to the lever, residual size, and alignment. Under an active-line compactness extraction, an admissible noncompactness profile must either retain a non-vanishing active one-tail clock or satisfy this residual-work budget. Finite-thickness active-line concentrations with a positive residual-work gap are therefore ruled out. The compactness theorem that would place every two-dimensional noncompactness scenario in this class is left as a separate problem.

### [133] [Redshift Suppression of Nonlinear Scalar Fields in Accelerating FLRW Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28020)
*Mirda Prisma Wijayanto,Emir Syahreza Fadhilla,Ryan Sugihakim,Iwan Setiawan,Fiki Taufik Akbar,Bobby Eka Gunara*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在空间平坦的d维FLRW时空（d≥4）中，非线性标量场小初值解的全局存在性与渐近行为。通过对加速共形膨胀（H(τ)=H₀(1+τ)^{-α}, 0≤α<1）和幂势V(φ)∝-|φ|^{m+1}的设定，引入共形变换消去一阶哈勃阻尼，并基于共形幂m_conf = (d+2)/(d-2)识别了红移抑制的阈值条件。当m > m_conf时，证明了小初值全局存在性与散射/渐近线性化；在扩散主导区域1<m<1+2/(d-1)中，通过加权能量方法推导了显式的L²和L¹衰减率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究膨胀宇宙中非线性标量场的长时间行为，尤其是红移效应对非线性自相互作用的压制机制。该问题在早期宇宙模型和暗能量建模中具有重要物理意义。

Method: 采用共形变换φ = a^{(d-2)/2} φ消去一阶哈勃阻尼项，将原方程转化为含时耦合系数的半线性波动/克莱因-戈登方程。对于超共形相互作用（m > m_conf），利用耦合函数g(τ)=a(τ)^σ可积性（g∈L¹([0,∞))）证明小初值全局存在性与散射；对于扩散主导区域（1<m<1+2/(d-1)），采用可变阻尼的加权能量方法推导衰减率。

Result: 在加速共形膨胀（0≤α<1）和超共形相互作用（m > m_conf）条件下，证明了小初值全局解的存在性以及散射/渐近线性化。在扩散主导区域（1<m<1+2/(d-1)）中，给出了解在L²和L¹范数下的显式衰减率。

Conclusion: 该工作为红移诱导的非线性标量场自相互作用在晚期共形时间上的压制提供了定量的偏微分方程表述，明确了共形幂m_conf是决定非线性耦合强度随时间演化的临界阈值。

Abstract: We study small--data solutions of a nonlinear scalar field equation on spatially flat $d$--dimensional FLRW spacetimes ($d\ge4$). In conformal time $τ$ the field satisfies a damped semilinear wave/Klein--Gordon equation with time--dependent coefficients determined by the scale factor $a(τ)$ and the conformal Hubble rate $H(τ)=\dot a/a$. We focus on accelerated conformal expansion of the form $H(τ)=H_0(1+τ)^{-α}$ with $H_0>0$ and $0\leα<1$, for which $a(τ)$ grows stretched--exponentially, and we assume a power potential $V(\varphi)=-\frac{\varepsilon}{m+1}|\varphi|^{m+1}$. For global solutions arising from sufficiently small, spatially localized initial data, we introduce the conformal rescaling $φ=a^{(d-2)/2}\varphi$, which removes the first--order Hubble damping and exposes the interaction as a \emph{time--dependent coupling}. In the rescaled equation the nonlinearity is weighted by $g(τ)=a(τ)^σ$ with $σ=\frac{d+2-(d-2)m}{2}$, so the conformal power $m_{\mathrm{conf}}=\frac{d+2}{d-2}$ is the sharp threshold for redshift suppression: $g$ decays for $m>m_{\mathrm{conf}}$, is constant for $m=m_{\mathrm{conf}}$ (classical conformal invariance), and grows for $1<m<m_{\mathrm{conf}}$. For accelerated conformal expansion $H(τ)=H_0(1+τ)^{-α}$ with $0\leα<1$ and for superconformal interactions $m>m_{\mathrm{conf}}$, we prove that $g\in L^1([0,\infty))$ and deduce small--data global existence together with scattering/asymptotic linearization for $φ$. As a complementary result in the diffusion--dominated regime $1<m<1+\frac{2}{d-1}$, we adapt a weighted energy method for variable damping to deduce explicit $L^2$ and $L^1$ decay rates. These bounds provide a quantitative PDE formulation of redshift--induced suppression of nonlinear scalar self--interactions at late conformal times.

</details>


### [134] [Constraint damping on subextremal Kerr spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27658)
*Peter Hintz*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明，在任意次极端克尔（subextremal Kerr）黑洞度规附近，可以对爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）的线性化形式实施一种增强形式的约束阻尼（constraint damping），该结果是非线性稳定性证明的关键组成部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约束阻尼（constraint damping）在双曲形式（hyperbolic formulations）的爱因斯坦场方程中能够抑制规范条件（gauge condition）与约束方程（constraint equations）的违反，在数值相对论（numerical relativity）与时空稳定性证明中均有重要应用。本文旨在证明在次极端克尔黑洞背景上可实现增强形式的约束阻尼，从而为后续的非线性稳定性证明奠定基础。

Conclusion: 该结果是作者后续证明次极端克尔族（Kerr family）非线性稳定性（nonlinear stability）的关键前提条件。

Abstract: In the context of hyperbolic formulations of Einstein's field equations obtained via gauge fixing, constraint damping is a desirable feature that ensures that violations of the gauge condition and thus of the constraint equations are suppressed in evolution. Besides its utility in numerical relativity, it has played a key role in several (linear and nonlinear) stability proofs of spacetimes as solutions of the Einstein equations. In this paper, we show that an enhanced form of constraint damping can be implemented for the linearization of the Einstein equations around any subextremal Kerr black hole metric. The results proved here are a key ingredient in the author's proof of the nonlinear stability of the subextremal Kerr family.

### [135] [Mellin Moments of Pion and Kaon Unpolarized PDFs from Nonlocal Operators in Lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28102)
*Joshua Miller,Joseph Torsiello,Krzysztof Cichy,Martha Constantinou,Joseph Delmar*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理格点QCD计算，利用含Wilson线的非定域算符，在短距离分解框架下提取了无粲π介子和K介子部分子分布函数的Mellin矩，最终在NNLO精度下给出μ=2 GeV的结果，并研究了SU(3)味对称性破缺效应及价PDF的重建。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了从第一性原理出发精确确定π介子和K介子的部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions, PDFs）的Mellin矩，弥补唯象模型和实验拟合的不足，并检验格点QCD在矩提取中的系统误差。

Method: 采用Nf=2+1+1最大扭质量费米子（maximally twisted-mass fermions）加clover项的格点系综，体积32³×64，格距a=0.0934 fm，π质量260 MeV。通过含直Wilson线的非定域算符计算增强动量的介子矩阵元，在短距离分解（short-distance factorization）框架下分析，比较NLO和NNLO的Wilson系数，并进行重整化群改进（RG-improved）分析作为微扰一致性检验。

Result: 在动量为P₃=0, 0.41, 0.83, 1.25, 1.66, 2.07 GeV下计算矩阵元；最终结果来自(P₃, z)空间的NNLO联合拟合，在μ=2 GeV处引用；考察了OPE截断、坐标空间拟合窗及微扰精度对矩提取的影响；获得了SU(3)味对称性破缺效应并重建了价PDF。

Conclusion: 通过NNLO精度的短距离分解框架结合格点QCD，能够可靠提取π和K介子PDF的Mellin矩，RG改进分析验证了微扰处理的一致性，SU(3)破缺效应可被定量研究并用于价PDF重建。

Abstract: We present a first-principles lattice-QCD determination of Mellin moments of the unpolarized pion and kaon parton distribution functions using matrix elements of boosted mesons coupled to nonlocal operators containing a straight Wilson line. The calculation is performed on an $N_f=2+1+1$ ensemble of maximally twisted-mass fermions with a clover term, with lattice volume $32^3\times64$, lattice spacing $a=0.0934$ fm, and pion mass $m_π=260$ MeV. Matrix elements are computed for hadron momenta $P_3=0$, 0.41, 0.83, 1.25, 1.66, and 2.07 GeV and analyzed within the short-distance factorization framework. We investigate the dependence of the extracted moments on the truncation of the operator-product expansion, the coordinate-space fit window, and the perturbative accuracy of the Wilson coefficients, comparing next-to-leading-order and next-to-next-to-leading-order results. We also perform an RG-improved analysis as a consistency check of the perturbative treatment. Our final results are obtained from combined fits in $(P_3,z)$ space at next-to-next-to-leading-order and are quoted at $μ=2$ GeV. We also study the SU(3) symmetry-breaking effect and reconstruct the valence PDFs from the moments.

</details>


### [136] [The QCD energy-momentum tensor on the lattice: non-perturbative renormalization with $N_f=3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28035)
*Matteo Bresciani,Mattia Dalla Brida,Leonardo Giusti,Mitsuaki Hirasawa,Michele Pepe,Luca Virzì*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文在晶格上构造了N_f=3味QCD的无迹能量-动量张量（traceless energy-momentum tensor），通过非微扰方法确定其重整化常数（renormalization constants），使其关联函数在连续极限下满足适当的Ward恒等式（Ward identities）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在晶格规范理论中离散化时空会导致SO(4)群的不可约九重态表示分裂为超立方群（hypercubic group）的三重态和六重态表示，因此需要非微扰地确定胶子和费米子的重整化常数，以确保能量-动量张量在连续极限下满足Ward恒等式。

Method: 采用Wilson-plaquette作用量和O(a)改进的Wilson作用量分别描述胶子和夸克；胶子部分通过clover离散化定义场强张量，费米子部分通过对称协变导数（symmetric covariant derivatives）组合离散化。通过引入移位边界条件（shifted boundary conditions）和虚化学势（imaginary chemical potential），对单点关联函数施加连续Ward恒等式的离散版本，非微扰地固定三重态和六重态表示中各自的两个独立重整化常数，并通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行计算。

Result: 在裸耦合常数平方0 ≤ g₀² ≤ 0.96的范围内，最终确定的重整化常数精度达到百分之几。

Conclusion: 本文提出的非微扰重整化方案能够有效构造晶格QCD中满足Ward恒等式的无迹能量-动量张量分量，为后续格点计算中的热力学和输运性质研究提供了可靠的基础。

Abstract: We construct the traceless components of the energy-momentum tensor on the lattice for QCD with $N_f=3$ flavours, such that their correlation functions satisfy the appropriate Ward identities in the continuum limit. To carry out this program, we define the theory on the lattice by the Wilson-plaquette and the $O(a)$-improved Wilson actions for gluons and quarks respectively. The discretization of the space-time entails that (i) the irreducible nonet representation of the SO($4$) group splits into a triplet and a sextet irreducible representations of the hypercubic group, and (ii) for each multiplet non-perturbative determinations of the the gluonic and fermionic renormalization constants are required. The bare gluonic components of the energy-momentum tensor are defined via the clover discretization of the field strength tensor, while the fermionic ones are discretized by appropriate combinations of symmetric covariant derivatives. Either for the triplet or the sextet representations, the two independent renormalization constants are then fixed non-perturbatively by imposing discretized versions of continuum Ward identities for one-point correlation functions in the presence of shifted boundary conditions and an imaginary chemical potential. The non-perturbative calculation is then carried out by Monte Carlo simulations, and the resulting renormalization constants are determined with a final accuracy of a few percent for values of the bare coupling constant squared in the range $0 \leq g_0^2\leq 0.96$.

</details>


### [137] [The QCD phase diagram for three-flavor Möbius domain-wall fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28086)
*Yu Zhang,Yasumichi Aoki,Jishnu Goswami,Shoji Hashimoto,Issaku Kanamori,Takashi Kaneko,Yoshifumi Nakamura*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文利用Möbius畴壁费米子（Möbius domain-wall fermions）在三个不同的时间格点尺寸（Nt=6,8,12）上研究了三味简并夸克QCD在零重子化学势下的相变。通过分析多种序参量（plaquette、手征凝聚等）的质量与体积依赖性，发现相变为连续交叉（crossover），而非一阶或二阶相变，并给出了各格点参数下的赝临界夸克质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解三味简并夸克QCD在有限温度下的相变性质（一阶相变、二阶相变或连续交叉）是格点QCD的核心问题之一，对理解强相互作用物质相图至关重要。

Method: 采用Möbius畴壁费米子作为格点费米子方案，在固定格距a=0.1361(20) fm下选取Nt=6,8,12三种时间格点尺寸，对应温度242、181、121 MeV。分析plaquette、plaquette磁化率（plaquette susceptibility）、手征凝聚（chiral condensate）、手征磁化率（chiral susceptibilities，包括总手征磁化率和断开手征磁化率）及Binder累积量（Binder cumulant）的质量和体积依赖性。

Result: 基于最大格点体积得到赝临界夸克质量：Nt=6时为184(10) MeV（由plaquette磁化率确定）；Nt=8和12时分别在36(1)–39.1(9) MeV和3.5(3)–3.7(2) MeV范围（取决于使用总手征磁化率还是断开手征磁化率，在MS̃重正化方案（MS̃ scheme）下μ=2 GeV标度）。有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis）显示Nt=12时体积增长显著弱于一阶或二阶相变预期，结合Nt=6和8可忽略的体积依赖性，表明这些夸克质量点对应连续交叉。

Conclusion: 在研究的参数范围内，三味简并夸克QCD的有限温度相变为连续交叉，而非一阶或二阶相变。此外，残余手征对称性破缺（residual chiral symmetry breaking）对手征凝聚和手征磁化率的影响通过两种不同的第五维尺寸Ls值进行了评估。

Abstract: We investigate the phase transition of Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) with three degenerate quark flavors at zero baryon chemical potential. Using Möbius domain-wall fermions as the lattice fermion formulation, we ensure excellent chiral symmetry preservation. Our simulations are performed at three different temporal lattice extents, $N_{t}=6, 8, 12$, with a fixed lattice spacing $a=0.1361(20)$ fm, corresponding to temperatures of 242(4), 181(3), and 121(2) MeV, respectively. We explore a range of quark masses and spatial volumes with aspect ratios $N_{s}/N_{t}$ spanning from 2 to 4. By analyzing the mass and volume dependencies of the plaquette, plaquette susceptibility, chiral condensate, chiral susceptibilities, and Binder cumulant, we identify the pseudocritical transition quark masses from our largest lattice volumes. For $N_t=6$, this is 184(10) MeV (determined from the plaquette susceptibility). For $N_t=8$ and 12, the transition points vary slightly depending on whether the total or disconnected chiral susceptibility is used, yielding ranges of 36(1)-39.1(9) MeV and 3.5(3)-3.7(2) MeV, respectively, in the $\overline{\text{MS}}$ scheme at a scale of $μ=2$ GeV. The negligible volume dependence at $N_t=6$ and 8, combined with finite-size scaling analysis at $N_t=12$ revealing volume growth significantly weaker than expected for a first- or second-order phase transition, points to a continuous crossover at these specific quark mass points. Additionally, we study the effects of residual chiral symmetry breaking on the chiral condensate and chiral susceptibilities using two different values of $L_s$.

### [138] [Spectral densities from Euclidean correlators via integral transforms: theoretical framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28167)
*Leonardo Giusti,Matteo Saccardi,Diego Toniolo*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过解析逆拉普拉斯变换（inverse Laplace transform）公式，从欧几里得时间关联函数中提取谱密度（spectral densities），并系统分析了格点离散步长效应、有限时间截断导致的非完全积分变换及其误差控制方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谱密度将实验测量与量子场论（quantum field theory）的动力学性质联系起来，但非微扰地从欧几里得时间关联函数中提取谱密度在数学上具有挑战性，现有方法缺少严格的解析框架。

Method: 利用积分变换（integral transforms）给出解析的逆拉普拉斯变换公式，适用于连续或离散采样的欧几里得时间关联函数；同时引入非完全积分变换（incomplete integral transforms）及相应的非完全涂抹谱密度（incomplete smeared spectral densities），严格界定未知贡献的误差边界。

Result: 证明若格点关联函数是O(a)改进的（O(a)-improved），则所提出的格点解在格点间距a上以O(a^2)精度趋向连续极限；涂抹函数（smearing function）的积分变换在共轭变量上足够快衰减时，未知部分对涂抹谱密度的贡献可被严格有界并可控。

Conclusion: 所提出的公式可为格点场论（lattice field theory）中谱密度重建提供精度目标规划；该方法易于推广至其他研究领域。

Abstract: Spectral densities link experimental measurements to dynamical properties of a quantum field theory which, in turn, can be resolved non-perturbatively from the Euclidean time-dependence of correlation functions. By making extensive use of integral transforms, we present analytic formulae to carry out the inverse Laplace transform so as to extract spectral densities from either the continuum or the discrete sampling of correlation functions in the Euclidean time. Formulae extend to regulated and/or smeared spectral densities as well. We explicitly show that the proposed lattice solution tends to its continuum counterpart up to $O(a^2)$ effects in the lattice spacing $a$ if the lattice correlator is $O(a)$-improved. In practical computations, lattices have necessarily a finite Euclidean temporal extent, a lack of knowledge which suggests to introduce incomplete integral transforms and the corresponding incomplete smeared spectral densities. The contribution from the unknowns to a smeared spectral density can then be rigorously bound and kept under control if the integral transform of the smearing function decays fast enough with the conjugate variable. Conversely, the bound can be used to plan lattices so as to achieve a given target precision on the reconstructed spectral density of interest. The formulae presented here in the context of lattice field theory can be easily applied or extended to other areas of research.

### [139] [Sampling the Schwinger Model with Gauge-Equivariant Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27481)
*Octavio Vega,Aida X. El-Khadra*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文首次研究了基于扩散（diffusion）的生成模型，用于加速 $N_f = 2$ 格点Schwinger模型的采样，旨在克服临界慢化（critical slowing down）问题。该U(1)等变（equivariant）得分匹配（score-based）生成模型通过计算模型似然（likelihood），可获得与MCMC模拟一致的无偏观测估计，并在临界参数附近展现出比HMC更优的拓扑冻结（topological freezing）缓解效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在格点场论（Lattice Field Theory, LFT）中，蒙特卡洛（MCMC）模拟面临众所周知的临界慢化（critical slowing down）问题，导致在接近连续极限时采样效率显著下降。受近期生成模型在格点系综生成中成功应用的启发，本文旨在探索扩散模型（diffusion model）作为加速格点场论采样的替代方案。

Method: 本文训练了一个U(1)等变（U(1)-equivariant）的得分匹配生成模型（score-based generative model），用于从边缘化（marginal）Schwinger模型中采样规范链接（gauge link）构型。该方法基于扩散过程，通过逆扩散生成样本，并利用模型似然（model likelihood）计算无偏估计量。

Result: 该生成模型产生的观测估计值与传统的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）模拟结果高度一致。定性分析表明，在临界参数附近，该方法相比混合蒙特卡洛（Hybrid Monte Carlo, HMC）有效减少了拓扑冻结（topological freezing）现象。

Conclusion: 基于扩散的生成模型在格点场论加速采样方面展现出潜力，能够缓解临界慢化和拓扑冻结问题，同时保持无偏估计能力。该工作为后续将深度生成模型应用于更复杂格点规范理论（lattice gauge theory）提供了基础。

Abstract: We present a first study of a diffusion-based approach to accelerated sampling of the $N_f = 2$ lattice Schwinger model. Our work is inspired by recent and growing successes in developing such generative models for ensemble generation in LFT to overcome the well-known critical slowing down problem. We train a U(1)-equivariant score-based generative model to sample gauge link configurations from the marginal Schwinger model. By computing model likelihoods, we obtain unbiased estimates for observables that closely match those produced by MCMC simulations. We also demonstrate improvement over HMC as measured qualitatively by a reduction in topological freezing near critical parameters.

### [140] [Bottleneck Effects and Harmonic-Type Velocity Bounds for Periodic Quantum Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27740)
*Houssam Abdul-Rahman,Thomas A. Jackson,Darren C. Ong*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文对具有任意周期硬币（coin）的一维量子游走（one-dimensional quantum walk）的传播速度给出了显式的上界和下界。在微扰（perturbative）条件下，速度被透射参数线性界住；在一般非零透射参数下，给出了基于调和平均的通用先验界，以及检测相邻硬币空间变化的精细化版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子游走的传播速度是理解其传输性能的关键量，但目前对具有周期性硬币的量子游走的速度缺乏显式的上界分析，特别是当硬币周期任意且透射参数可调时，其传播速度与参数之间的定量关系尚未明确。

Method: 论文区分了两种互补情形：在微扰（perturbative）框架下，假设某个透射参数很小，分析其作为瓶颈对速度的线性约束，并给出显式的领头阶估计；在一般非零透射参数情形下，利用调和平均（harmonic mean）推导通用先验上界，并引入能检测相邻硬币空间变化的精细化版本。同时证明了一个速度下界。这些结论直接适用于相应的CMV（ Cantero-Moral-Velázquez）设定。

Result: 在微扰情形下，速度被透射参数线性上界，且获得显式的领头阶估计。在一般非零透射参数情形下，速度上界由其调和平均控制，且存在一个能反映相邻硬币空间变化的精细化版本。此外，论文证明了速度的一个通用下界。

Conclusion: 论文为一维周期硬币量子游走的传播速度建立了显式的上、下界，揭示了透射参数对速度的定量约束关系，并表明这些结果可直接应用于相应的CMV设定。

Abstract: We prove explicit upper bounds on the propagation velocity of one-dimensional quantum walks with periodic coins of arbitrary period. We treat two complementary settings. First, in a perturbative regime where one transmission parameter is small, we show that the corresponding almost reflecting coin acts as a bottleneck for transport: the velocity is bounded linearly in this parameter, with an explicit leading order estimate. Second, for arbitrary nonzero transmission parameters, we prove a general a priori bound in terms of their harmonic mean, together with a refined version that detects the spatial variation of neighboring coins. Moreover, we prove a general lower bound on the velocity. These bounds apply directly to the corresponding CMV setting.

### [141] [Uniqueness, analyticity and mixing for Gibbs point processes via spectral gaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28009)
*Andreas Göbel,Matthew Jenssen,Marcus Michelen,Marcus Pappik,Will Perkins,Leon Schiller*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过对吉布斯点过程（Gibbs point process）谱阈值（spectral threshold）λ_spec的分析，证明了硬球模型（hard-sphere model）在λ_spec以下的无限体积吉布斯测度唯一性、压力解析性及混合性质，并在高维及E8与Leech格点等特殊维度上给出了无相变的最优结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典硬球模型在连续统中通过势能（potential）相互作用，其相变（phase transition）行为与临界活度（activity）的精确刻画长期未完全解决。巴黎（Parisi）和赞波尼（Zamponi）曾预测快速混合（rapid mixing）的最大密度，但缺乏严格证明。本文旨在通过引入谱阈值λ_spec，统一改进已有唯一性与解析性边界，并验证该预测。

Method: 作者将Kondratiev-Kuna-Ohlerich（2013）工作中隐含定义的谱阈值λ_spec显式化，并证明该阈值对应的谱隙（spectral gap）能够导出多种强意义的无相变条件。对于硬球模型，通过分析λ_spec的行为获得改进的唯一性、解析性与混合时间（mixing time）上界。在维度8和24中，结合Cohn-Kumar-Miller-Radchenko-Viazovska的格点工作，构造了无相变的排斥径向对势（repulsive radial pair potentials）。

Result: 对于任意固定维度d≥2，硬球模型的唯一性与解析性边界得到改进；当d→∞时，改进幅度呈指数增长。首次证明了硬球模型在期望密度为Θ(d/2^d)时的最优混合时间上界，渐近匹配了Parisi-Zamponi预测的快速混合最大密度。构造了λ_spec=+∞的排斥径向对势，表明对应吉布斯点过程在任何活度λ>0下均无相变；在维度8和24中，该无相变势能的唯一基态（ground state）分别为E₈格与Leech格。

Conclusion: 谱阈值λ_spec是刻画吉布斯点过程无相变行为的关键量，谱隙的存在能够蕴含唯一性、解析性与混合性等多种强性质。对于硬球模型，该方法在有限维与高维渐近意义下均显著优于经典结果，并严格证实了Parisi-Zamponi关于快速混合密度的猜想。

Abstract: A Gibbs point process models particles interacting in the continuum through a potential. Among the most classical examples is the hard-sphere model, where given an activity parameter $λ$, a radius $r$, and a bounded set $Λ\subset \mathbb{R}^d$ one samples a Poisson process of intensity $λ$ in $Λ$ conditioned on the points forming the centers of an $r$-sphere packing. We prove uniqueness of infinite-volume Gibbs measure, analyticity of the pressure, and various notions of spatial and temporal mixing for activities up to what we define as the spectral threshold $λ_{spec}$ of the potential. For each fixed dimension $d \geq 2$, this improves the uniqueness and analyticity bounds for the hard-sphere model. As $d \to \infty$, our improvement over the classical bounds grows exponentially. We also prove an optimal mixing time bound for heat bath dynamics for the hard-sphere model up to an expected density of $Θ(d / 2^d)$, the first result that asymptotically matches the maximum density for rapid mixing predicted by Parisi and Zamponi.
  We also exhibit repulsive, radial pair potentials for which $λ_{spec} = + \infty$, showing that the corresponding Gibbs point processes have no phase transition at any activity $λ> 0$. Further, in dimensions $8$ and $24$ we exhibit such a potential with no phase transition for which the work of Cohn-Kumar-Miller-Radchenko-Viazovska proves that the unique ground state at any fixed density is given by the $E_8$ and Leech lattices, respectively. Our work builds upon a 2013 work of Kondratiev-Kuna-Ohlerich that implicitly defined $λ_{spec}$ and proved a spectral gap for a Glauber-like continuum birth-death dynamics. Our main work shows that such a spectral gap implies several strong notions of absence of phase transition and analyzes the behavior of $λ_{spec}$ for interesting potentials.

</details>


### [142] [Shirokov realizations of low dimensional Lie algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28140)
*Severin Pošta*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文运用Shirokov方法，计算了维数不超过四的低维实李代数（real Lie algebras）的传递实现（transitive realizations），包括一般实现与非一般实现，并将结果与Popovych等人的已有分类进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实李代数的传递实现在微分方程对称性分析和几何等领域有重要应用，但低维情形下的完整分类仍有待补充和验证，因此有必要采用统一方法系统计算并与其他分类结果对照。

Method: 采用Shirokov方法，先计算一般传递实现（generic realizations），再基于已知的子代数（subalgebras）列表计算非一般传递实现（nongeneric realizations）。

Result: 成功给出了维数不超过四的实李代数的全部传递实现，包括一般实现和非一般实现。

Abstract: We compute the transitive realizations for the low dimensional cases of real Lie algebras up to dimension four using Shirokov's method. First, the generic realizations are given, then, making use of the known list of subalgebras, nongeneric realizations are computed. The result is compared with the known classification of Popovych et al.

</details>


### [143] [Which Saddles Contribute? The South-East Rule for Multidimensional Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28271)
*Inês Aniceto,Job Feldbrugge,Christopher J. Howls*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于几何的简单算法，用于确定在形如 e^{ikf(x)} 的指数型多重积分渐近展开中起贡献的临界点（包括实临界点和复临界点）。该算法通过组合 Borel 平面上的临界点值、代数复兴/超渐近方法中的邻接概念以及新提出的几何“东南法则”，避免了传统 Picard-Lefschetz 方法中需要计算复流形的繁琐步骤，并适用于有界和无界函数 f。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多重指数型积分（如路径积分）的渐近展开中，确定哪些临界点（包括复临界点）实际贡献于积分值是核心问题。传统 Picard-Lefschetz 方法虽有效，但需要计算复空间中的梯度流（flow of -Re(i∇f)），计算复杂且繁琐。因此，亟需一种更简洁、几何直观的算法来替代这一过程。

Method: 该算法基于三个核心要素：1) 将函数 f 在所有临界点处的值绘制在复 Borel 平面（Borel plane）上；2) 利用代数复兴（algebraic resurgence）/超渐近（hyperasymptotic）方法导出的临界点之间的“邻接”（adjacency）关系；3) 新提出的几何“东南法则”（South-East rule），用于判断哪些临界点在渐近展开中实际贡献。算法无需计算复空间中的梯度流，且适用于定义在实数域 R^d 上有界或无界的函数 f。

Result: 通过教学性和高阶实例展示了该算法的有效性。结果表明，该算法能够系统地识别在真实时间路径积分（real-time path integrals）中起关键作用的瞬子（instanton）贡献，并为解决 Wick 旋转（Wick rotation）相关问题提供了一种新的几何工具。

Conclusion: 该几何算法是朝着系统化识别真实时间路径积分中瞬子贡献的重要一步。它简化了临界点筛选过程，为处理 Wick 旋转及相关渐近展开问题提供了更简便、更直观的替代方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce and demonstrate a simple geometric algorithm to determine which critical points, both complex as well as real, contribute to the asymptotic evaluation of multiple integrals with exponential integrands of the form $e^{ikf(\boldsymbol{x})}$ over $\mathbb R^d$, for finite $d\ge 1$ and $f$ is analytic. In so doing, the algorithm removes the need to compute the flows of $-\text{Re} (i\nabla f)$ in $\mathbb C^d$ that is required to identify such relevant critical points in Picard-Lefschetz approaches to the derivation of such asymptotic expansions. By contrast, our algorithm relies on the combination of three simple features: the values of $f$ at all the critical points plotted in the complex Borel plane, the concept of adjacency between such points derived from algebraic resurgence/hyperasymptotic approaches and the new result here of a geometric "South-East" rule. The algorithm incorporates functions $f$ that remain bounded or unbounded on $\mathbb R^d$. We illustrate this new approach with both pedagogical and advanced examples, and draw conclusions as to its importance for resolving issues associated with Wick rotations and its implications for path integrals. This is a significant step towards a systematic way of identifying instanton contributions in real-time path integrals.

</details>

### [144] [Universal EOS-Radius Inverse Mappings Govern Precision-Dependent Inference of the Neutron Star Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28183)
*Bao-An Li*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文发现中子星（NS）物态方程（EOS）的贝叶斯推断中，观测精度的提高会导致EOS参数后验均值发生系统性偏移，其根源在于中子星半径$R_{1.4}$与经验EOS参数之间存在近乎普适的逆映射关系，该映射定义了贝叶斯推断背后的低维EOS流形，而精度依赖性源自后验半径分布通过该逆映射的非线性滤波效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统贝叶斯推断假设改进观测主要减少后验不确定性而不改变EOS参数推断值。本文旨在检验这一假设，并揭示观测精度变化对EOS参数推断的系统性影响及其物理机制。

Method: 利用典型$1.4\,M_\odot$中子星半径$R_{1.4}$的模拟测量数据，设定相同中心值但不同观测精度，进行贝叶斯推断。通过分析后验样本的分布特性，识别半径与经验EOS参数之间的逆映射关系，并推导非线性滤波（nonlinear filtering）效应及窄分布极限下的Jensen型修正（Jensen-type correction）。

Result: 观测精度提高时，EOS参数的后验均值发生系统性偏移。后验样本在不同观测精度下均坍缩到近乎唯一的函数曲线上，表明存在与精度无关的普适逆映射。窄分布极限下该效应等价于与逆映射局部曲率成正比的Jensen型修正，而在当前实际精度范围内，完整的非线性滤波关系能准确复现后验均值。

Conclusion: 中子星EOS贝叶斯推断中存在精度依赖性的几何起源，观测精度的提高会通过非线性滤波机制系统性改变推断结果。该发现为将天体观测与微观核多体理论直接连接提供了新框架。

Abstract: Bayesian inference of the neutron star (NS) equation of state (EOS) generally assumes that improved observations primarily reduce posterior uncertainties while leaving inferred EOS parameters unchanged. Using mock measurements of the radius of a canonical $1.4\,M_\odot$ NS with identical central values but varying observational precisions, we show that the inferred posterior means of EOS parameters can shift systematically as the measurement uncertainty changes. We demonstrate that this behavior originates from previously unidentified nearly universal inverse mappings between the NS radius $R_{1.4}$ and empirical EOS parameters. Across a broad range of observational precisions, posterior samples collapse onto nearly unique functions. These mappings are largely independent of observational precision and define a low-dimensional EOS manifold underlying Bayesian inference. We show that the precision dependence of inferred EOS parameters arises from nonlinear filtering of the posterior radius distribution through these mappings. In the narrow-distribution limit this effect reduces to a Jensen-type correction proportional to the local curvature of the inverse mapping, while for presently realistic uncertainties the full nonlinear-filtering relation accurately reproduces the posterior means. Our results reveal a geometric origin of precision-dependent inference in NS EOS studies and provide a new framework for connecting astrophysical observations directly to microscopic nuclear many-body theories.

Result: 结果表明存在一个相图（phase diagram），在不同的参数数量下呈现不同的缩放区间（scaling regimes）；泛化误差服从由目标谱结构（spectral structure of the target）控制的数据依赖幂律（data-dependent power laws）。此外，还刻画了不同区间之间的转变（transitions），包括插值（interpolation）的起始点及其对泛化的影响。

Conclusion: 本文在特征学习模型框架下，明确了泛化误差随模型大小与数据量缩放的理论规律，指出了由目标谱结构主导的不同缩放区间及其转变条件，为理解有限样本下深度模型的泛化行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Understanding how performance scales jointly with model size and data is a central problem in modern machine learning. Existing theoretical works on scaling laws typically describe generalization as a function of data or compute, often in fixed-feature or infinite-width regimes and for online SGD. Here, we instead study how generalization scales with the number of trainable parameters and the number of samples in a feature-learning model. We analyze $\ell_2$-regularized empirical test error minimization in a quadratic two-layer network in a finite-sample setting with structured data. This setting allows for an explicit characterization of the generalization error as a function of the number of samples, model width, and regularization. Our results reveal a phase diagram with distinct scaling regimes as the number of parameters varies. In particular, the generalization error follows data-dependent power laws controlled by the spectral structure of the target. We further characterize the transitions between regimes, including the onset of interpolation, and their impact on generalization.

### [146] [Jarzynski equality for counterwork under reversed memory-filtered driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27486)
*Pierre Nazé*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由符号反转的记忆滤波有效协议生成的逆功泛函（counterwork functional）。该有效协议通过对原协议变化率施加主动协议-记忆核（active protocol-memory kernel）而非被动浴响应得到。逆功直接服从Jarzynski等式；当有效协议反转原协议端点时，逆功与原始功的指数平均互为倒数，且平均逆功与平均功之和非负。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平衡统计力学（non-equilibrium statistical mechanics）中，Jarzynski等式及其衍生关系是连接功与自由能差的核心工具。作者旨在构造一种新的功泛函——逆功（counterwork），使其能直接应用Jarzynski等式，并与原始功建立对偶关系，从而拓展非平衡涨落定理（fluctuation theorems）的适用范围。

Method: 通过引入符号反转的记忆滤波有效协议（sign-inverting memory-filtered effective protocol）$Λ(t)$，该协议由原协议$λ(t)$的变化率$\dotλ(t)$经主动协议-记忆核（active protocol-memory kernel）变换得到，而非通过被动浴响应。逆功定义为与哈密顿量$H(Γ,Λ(t))$对应的普通哈密顿功，从而使Jarzynski等式直接适用于逆功。

Result: 当$Λ(t)$反转$λ(t)$的端点时，对应的自由能差满足$ΔF_C=-ΔF_W$，且逆功的指数平均是原始功指数平均的倒数。由Jensen不等式导出平均功与平均逆功之和的非负条件$\langle C\rangle+\langle W\rangle\geq0$，表明负平均逆功仅在原始功的平均值补偿下才能实现。

Conclusion: 推导了实现端点反转所需的核归一化条件；讨论了在不完全热力学信息（incomplete thermodynamic information）下的逆操作策略，指出最稳健的方法是强制端点反转同时最小化耗散逆功（dissipated counterwork）。

Abstract: We introduce a counterwork functional generated by a sign-inverting memory-filtered effective protocol. Given an imposed protocol $λ(t)$, the effective protocol $Λ(t)$ is obtained by applying an active protocol-memory kernel to $\dotλ(t)$, rather than by invoking a passive bath response. The counterwork is then the ordinary Hamiltonian work associated with $H(Γ,Λ(t))$, so that Jarzynski's equality applies directly to it. When $Λ(t)$ reverses the endpoints of $λ(t)$, the corresponding free-energy difference satisfies $ΔF_C=-ΔF_W$, and the exponential average of the counterwork is the reciprocal of that of the original work. We derive the kernel normalization realizing this reversed displacement and show, by Jensen's inequality, that the product of the exponentials of the average work and counterwork is bounded by unity, implying $\langle C\rangle+\langle W\rangle\geq0$. Thus negative average counterwork is possible only when compensated by the average work of the original operation. We further discuss the counteroperation under incomplete thermodynamic information, showing that the robust strategy is to enforce endpoint reversal while minimizing dissipated counterwork.

</details>


### [147] [Rare Events Govern Defect Formation under Weak Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27835)
*Jiang Liu,Peng Yang,Matteo Baggioli*

TL;DR: 本文利用大偏差理论（large-deviation theory）揭示，弱显式对称破缺（weak explicit symmetry breaking）下拓扑缺陷密度的指数抑制源于驱动局部区域进入不利对称破缺态的稀有涨落（rare fluctuations），并给出了任意维度下缺陷密度的闭式表达式，经一维与二维随机Ginzburg-Landau模型模拟验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期的数值研究发现，在存在弱显式对称破缺时，Kibble-Zurek机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism）预测的拓扑缺陷密度普适幂律标度会出现系统性偏离，表现为额外的指数抑制。然而，这一修正的起源及其通用理论框架尚不明确。

Method: 采用大偏差理论（large-deviation theory）分析弱对称破缺下的缺陷生成过程，推导出任意维度中缺陷密度的闭式表达式，并在弱场和弱噪声极限下有效。通过一维和二维随机Ginzburg-Landau模型（stochastic Ginzburg-Landau models）的直接模拟进行验证。

Result: 缺陷生成受稀有涨落（rare fluctuations）控制，这些涨落将局部区域驱动至不利的对称破缺态，从而产生对缺陷密度的指数抑制。理论预测与一维和二维数值模拟结果吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作为弱显式对称破缺下偏离Kibble-Zurek标度（Kibble-Zurek scaling）的现象提供了一个严格的理论框架，揭示了稀有涨落的关键作用。

Abstract: Crossing a continuous phase transition out of equilibrium typically generates topological defects whose density obeys a universal power-law scaling predicted by the Kibble-Zurek mechanism. Recent numerical studies have revealed systematic deviations from this scaling in the presence of weak explicit symmetry breaking, manifested as an additional exponential suppression of defect formation. However, the origin of this correction and a general theoretical framework to describe it have remained elusive. Here, using large-deviation theory, we show that defect formation under weak symmetry breaking is controlled by rare fluctuations that drive local regions into the disfavored symmetry-broken state. This mechanism yields a closed-form expression for the defect density in arbitrary dimensions, valid in the weak-field and weak-noise limits. These theoretical predictions are verified through direct simulations of stochastic Ginzburg-Landau models in one and two spatial dimensions.

### [148] [Quantum enhancement of information-mediated energy transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27868)
*Shotaro Oki,Yuki Kadono,Kaito Tojo,Takahiro Sagawa,Ken Funo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过推导一个适用于相互作用开放量子系统的热力学不确定关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation），该关系在非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states）下将信息流与熵产（entropy production）联系起来。构建了一个具有N重简并基态和激发态并与热浴集体耦合的量子引擎（quantum engine）。

Conclusion: 量子相干性和集体效应在量子引擎中展现出可扩展的热力学优势，为设计高性能低耗散的量子热机提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Thermodynamics of information identifies information flow as a thermodynamic resource, but whether quantum coherence and collective coupling can enhance it at low entropy-production cost remains unresolved. We address this question for interacting open quantum systems by deriving a thermodynamic uncertainty relation that bounds information flow by entropy production in nonequilibrium steady states. We construct a quantum engine in which N-fold degenerate ground and excited states are collectively coupled to heat baths. Collective jumps enhance heat currents and information flow linearly with N, while entropy production remains independent of N, realizing a high-power, low-dissipation autonomous quantum Maxwell's demon that leverages collectively enhanced information flow to pump heat against a temperature gradient. Beyond steady states, collective interactions amplify the unitary component of quantum information flow, yielding a quadratic enhancement of the free-energy charging power of quantum batteries. Our results reveal scalable advantages of quantum coherence and collective effects in quantum engines.

### [149] [A Finite Element Method for Fluctuating Navier--Stokes Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27972)
*Dimitrios Gourzoulidis,Mirko Gallo,Soumaya Elkantassi,Toby Kay,Serafim Kalliadasis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于模拟可压缩流体中热涨落的有限元框架，基于涨落纳维-斯托克斯（fluctuating Navier-Stokes）方程。该方法通过在弱形式中定义随机强迫项并确保其协方差与离散粘性耗散算子成正比，在离散层面上保持了涨落-耗散平衡（fluctuation-dissipation balance）。采用节点求积规则消除非物理的网格尺度相关性，并使用克兰克-尼科尔森（Crank-Nicolson）格式进行时间积分。一维、二维和三维空间的数值验证表明，该方法能在不同离散参数下正确捕获平衡涨落统计特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可压缩流体中的热涨落模拟需要数值方法在离散层面上精确保持涨落-耗散平衡（fluctuation-dissipation balance），这是确保热力学一致性的关键。现有方法在处理这一平衡时面临挑战，特别是在有限元框架中难以避免非物理的网格尺度相关性。

Method: 提出一种有限元（finite-element）框架，基于涨落纳维-斯托克斯方程（fluctuating Navier-Stokes equations）模拟热涨落。随机强迫项在弱形式（weak formulation）中定义，其协方差被设置为与离散粘性耗散算子成正比，从而在离散层面上保持涨落-耗散平衡。采用节点求积规则（nodal quadrature rule）消除非物理的网格尺度相关性，并使用克兰克-尼科尔森格式（Crank-Nicolson scheme）进行时间积分。

Result: 该方法在一维、二维和三维空间中进行了数值验证，结果表明其能够在不同离散化参数下正确捕获平衡涨落（equilibrium fluctuation）的统计特性。

Conclusion: 所提出的有限元框架能够有效模拟可压缩流体中的热涨落，并在离散层面上保持涨落-耗散平衡，具有较好的精度和普适性。

Abstract: We introduce a finite-element framework for simulating thermal fluctuations in compressible fluids governed by the fluctuating Navier-Stokes equations. The method is designed to preserve the fundamental fluctuation-dissipation balance at the discrete level. This is achieved by defining the stochastic forcing term in the weak formulation, ensuring its covariance is proportional to the discrete viscous dissipation operator. A nodal quadrature rule is employed to eliminate unphysical mesh-scale correlations. The time integration is performed using the Crank-Nicolson scheme to maintain numerical stability and accuracy. The proposed approach is numerically validated in one, two, and three spatial dimensions, demonstrating its capability to correctly capture equilibrium fluctuation statistics across various discretisation parameters.
