### [150] [Nonextensive Statistical Signatures of the Bilaterian Transition in Proteome Length Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27985)
*Sertac Eroglu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文发现，跨生命界的蛋白质长度分布（protein length distributions）可通过Tsallis广义熵形式下的非广延统计力学（nonextensive statistical mechanics）进行描述。基于22个参考蛋白质组（proteomes）的分析表明，熵指数（entropic index）q可分为三个统计上不同的区域：原核生物及低等真核生物对应q<1，刺胞动物和基础两侧对称动物对应q跨越1的边界区，高等两侧对称动物对应q>1且随复杂度单调递增。q-指数分布优于普通指数分布，表明该指数可作为蛋白质组组织复杂度的连续物理指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Boltzmann-Gibbs统计无法描述具有长程关联（long-range correlations）、标度不变性（scale invariance）和层级组织（hierarchical organization）的复杂系统。该研究旨在利用非广延统计力学框架，探究蛋白质长度分布是否携带生物体复杂度的定量信号，并检验Tsallis熵指数能否作为组织复杂度的可解释指标。

Method: 对涵盖古菌域（Archaea）、细菌域（Bacteria）和真核域（Eukarya）的22个完全测序生物体的参考蛋白质组进行分析，重点在从海绵和刺胞动物到高等两侧对称动物的动物过渡区进行采样。采用截断离散q-指数分布（truncated discrete q-exponential distributions）进行最大似然估计（MLE）拟合，并通过bootstrap方法计算95%置信区间（CIs）。

Result: 熵指数q呈现三个统计学显著不同的区间：原核生物、单细胞和非动物多细胞真核生物及基础动物为超广延（superextensive, q<1）；两种刺胞动物和基础两侧对称动物C. teleta为边界区（置信区间跨越1）；所有高等两侧对称动物为亚广延（subextensive, q>1），且q在四种后口动物中从S. purpuratus（1.033）到H. sapiens（1.147）单调递增。q-指数分布在所有22个蛋白质组中均优于普通指数分布，并随着蛋白质组复杂度增加，逐步与替代的两参数分布竞争。

Conclusion: Tsallis熵指数可作为一个连续、物理上可解释的蛋白质组组织复杂度指标。该研究将非广延统计力学的适用范围扩展到蛋白质组系统，表明其能够刻画从原核生物到人类的蛋白质长度分布演化规律。

Abstract: Protein length distributions across the tree of life carry a quantitative signature of organismal complexity. Nonextensive statistical mechanics, through the Tsallis generalized entropy formalism, provides a natural framework for describing complex systems characterized by long-range correlations, scale invariance, and hierarchical organization -- features that classical Boltzmann-Gibbs statistics cannot accommodate. In this work, the complementary cumulative distribution function (CCDF) of protein lengths is analyzed within this framework for the reference proteomes of 22 fully sequenced organisms spanning the domains Archaea, Bacteria, and Eukarya, with deliberate sampling across the animal transition zone from sponges and cnidarians to higher bilaterians. Maximum likelihood (MLE) fitting of truncated discrete q-exponential distributions, with bootstrap 95% confidence intervals (CIs) reveals that the entropic index q resolves into three statistically distinct regimes: superextensive (q < 1) for prokaryotes, unicellular and non-animal multicellular eukaryotes, and basal animals; a boundary regime (CI on spanning unity) for the two cnidarians studied and the basal bilaterian C. teleta; and subextensive (q > 1) for all higher bilaterians, with q increasing monotonically across the four deuterostomes sampled from S. purpuratus (1.033) to H. sapiens (1.147). The q-exponential outperforms the ordinary exponential distribution across all 22 proteomes and becomes progressively more competitive against alternative two-parameter distributions as proteome complexity increases. These results identify the Tsallis entropic index as a continuous, physically interpretable indicator of proteome organizational complexity and extend the applicability of nonextensive statistical mechanics to proteomic systems.

</details>


### [151] [Optimal parameterization of nonequilibrium generalized master equations from discrete-time experimental data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28289)
*Chih-Wei Joshua Liu,Jérémie Klinger,Grant M. Rotskoff*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于最大似然估计（maximum-likelihood）的方法，用于从实验和模拟数据中参数化形式上精确、物理可行的离散时间广义主方程（generalized master equations, GMEs），作为马尔可夫状态模型（Markov state models, MSMs）的替代方案，以处理粗粒化（coarse-graining）过程中不可避免的记忆效应（memory）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验动力学分析常依赖粗粒化描述，但复杂系统通常不满足马尔可夫性（Markovianity）与热力学平衡（thermodynamic equilibrium）的常用假设；粗粒化必然引入记忆效应。现有方法中，MSMs要求微观状态分配可实验调控，而GMEs虽能显式捕捉记忆但难以参数化，且在离散时间设定下通常仅为形式近似。

Method: 采用基于最大似然估计的程序，对实验和模拟数据（平衡与非平衡条件下）参数化形式上精确、物理可行的离散时间GMEs。通过适配最优输运（optimal transport）算法，构建满足物理约束的条件最大似然估计器（conditional-maximum-likelihood estimators），同时估计精确的Nakajima-Zwanzig记忆核（memory kernels）和时域卷积less GME传播子（propagators）。

Result: 将方法应用于三个实例：离子通道中Förster共振能量转移（Förster-resonance energy-transfer）实验记录、过程性分子马达（processive molecular motor）的纳米颗粒追踪实验，以及基准蛋白质结构域（benchmark protein domain）的模拟折叠。成功恢复包括弛豫率（relaxation rates）、不可逆性（irreversibilities）、停留时间（dwell times）和首次通过时间（first-passage times）在内的动力学参数。

Conclusion: 离散时间GMEs可成为实验和模拟生物分子系统动力学分析中一种兼具物理与统计原则性的方法，是MSMs的有效替代方案。

Abstract: Kinetic analyses of experiments often require coarse-grained descriptions, but complex systems rarely conform to the widely used modeling assumptions of Markovianity and thermodynamic equilibrium. Memory is indeed a general and often inevitable consequence of coarse-graining. Markov state models (MSMs) are a popular choice of coarse-grained description, but require microstate assignments -- which are rarely experimentally tunable -- to macrostates that minimize memory. Generalized master equations (GMEs) circumvent this limitation of MSMs by explicitly capturing memory. However, GMEs are difficult to parameterize and usually formally approximate in the experimentally relevant discrete-time setting. Here we introduce a maximum-likelihood-based procedure to parameterize formally exact, physically feasible, discrete-time generalized master equations from experiments and simulations in and out of equilibrium. By adapting algorithms typically used in optimal transport, we construct physical-constraint-satisfying conditional-maximum-likelihood estimators of both exact Nakajima-Zwanzig memory kernels and time-convolutionless GME propagators in discrete time. Applying these estimators to three examples -- experimental recordings of Förster-resonance energy-transfer in an ion channel, experimental nanoparticle tracking of a processive molecular motor, and simulated folding of a benchmark protein domain -- we recover kinetic parameters including relaxation rates, irreversibilities, dwell times, and first-passage times. These results establish discrete-time GMEs as a physically and statistically principled alternative to MSMs for kinetic analyses of experimental and simulated biomolecular systems.

</details>

### [152] [A single platform with van der Pauw geometry for measurement of Seebeck coefficient, resistivity, and Hall effect of thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28137)

Method: 采用范德堡构型（van der Pauw configuration）进行电阻率与塞贝克系数的同步测量；通过优化偏移电压（offset voltages）、导线贡献（wire contributions）和热接触电阻（thermal contact resistances）等误差源来提升测量精度；使用LabVIEW程序实现测量流程的完全自动化控制；采用可拆卸模块化设计增强装置的灵活性与扩展性。

Result: 装置可在25°C至600°C的宽温区范围内同时测量电阻率和塞贝克系数，并能在室温下进行霍尔测量；具备良好的用户友好性和全自动化控制能力；模块化设计使其成为一个除热导率（thermal conductivity）外热电性能测量的集成解决方案。

Conclusion: 该模块化装置实现了热电材料关键电学性能参数的高精度、宽温区、自动化集成测量，为热电材料研究提供了一种可靠且便捷的测量工具。

Abstract: A modular thermoelectric properties measurement setup in van der Pauw configuration was developed for a straightforward and simultaneous measurement of electrical resistivity and Seebeck coefficient in an extensive temperature range of 25°C - 600°C and can also perform Hall measurements at room temperature. The setup is optimized for accurate measurement of voltages and temperatures gradients by minimizing possible errors from offset voltages, wire contributions and thermal contact resistances which helps getting reliable data. The setup is user friendly, and the measurements are fully automated and controlled using a LabVIEW program. The detachable modules make this setup quite versatile and provide an all-in-one (except thermal conductivity) solution for thermoelectric measurements.

### [153] [Magnetic long-range order at finite temperature in two-dimensional hyperbolic lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27422)
*Alexander Hickey,Joseph Maciejko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过研究双曲平面（hyperbolic plane）上规则铺砌的自旋-S Heisenberg 模型，证明负曲率空间可以规避有限温度下戈德斯通模（Goldstone modes）导致的长程磁序缺失，从而实现 Mermin-Wagner 定理的几何绕过。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统二维系统中无能隙的戈德斯通模（gapless Goldstone modes）的红外奇异性（infrared singularities）阻止了有限温度下的磁性长程序（magnetic long-range order）。本文旨在探究负曲率空间能否消除这一障碍，从而在不破坏或修改连续对称性的前提下实现有限温度磁有序。

Method: 采用自旋波理论（spin-wave theory）对双曲平面上规则铺砌的自旋-S Heisenberg 模型进行分析，研究对称性所要求的零能集体模（zero-energy collective modes）的局域谱权重、热力学体态磁振子连续谱（thermodynamic bulk magnon continuum）的能隙，以及负曲率对量子涨落的抑制效应。

Result: 零能集体模携带的局域谱权重（local spectral weight）为零，且与体态局域谱密度（bulk local spectral density）中的磁振子连续谱之间被有限能隙分离；局域横向关联（local transverse correlations）仍为短程，具有有限关联长度。更强的负曲率进一步抑制体态热力学量中的量子涨落，使有序态趋向"平均场行为"（mean-field-like behavior）。

Conclusion: 双曲几何（hyperbolic geometry）提供了一条绕过 Mermin-Wagner 障碍（Mermin-Wagner obstruction）的途径，无需破坏或修改连续对称性即可在有限温度下实现磁有序。

Abstract: Infrared singularities of gapless Goldstone modes preclude magnetic long-range order at finite temperature in conventional two-dimensional systems. By studying the spin-$S$ Heisenberg model on regular tilings of the hyperbolic plane, we show that this obstruction is absent in negatively curved space. Using spin-wave theory, we find that the zero-energy collective modes required by symmetry carry vanishing local spectral weight and are separated from the thermodynamic bulk magnon continuum by a finite gap in the bulk local spectral density. As a result, local transverse correlations remain short ranged, with a finite correlation length, despite the presence of Goldstone modes associated with the broken SO(3) spin-rotation symmetry. Stronger negative curvature is found to suppress quantum fluctuations in bulk thermodynamic quantities, pushing the ordered state toward "mean-field-like" behavior. We further estimate the ordering temperature from the thermal spin-wave correction to the ordered moment. These results establish hyperbolic geometry as a route to finite-temperature magnetic order that circumvents the Mermin-Wagner obstruction without breaking or modifying the continuous symmetry.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三维投影纠缠对态（projected entangled pair states, PEPS）作为变分波函数，并利用环展开（loop expansions）在树状晶格上快速收敛地计算基态物理可观测量。

Result: 外推到无限键维（bond dimension）极限的结果表明，该模型基态为无能隙自旋液体（gapless spin-liquid）。

Conclusion: 超蜂窝晶格上的SU(4)海森堡模型可能具有无能隙自旋液体基态，三维PEPS结合环展开是研究此类系统的有效数值方法。

We show that it is possible to compute physical observables for the ground states using loop expansions, which converge quickly on tree-like lattices. Our extrapolations to the limit of infinite bond dimensions point toward gapless spin-liquid ground state.

### [155] [Metamagnetism in UTe2: the roles of itinerancy and localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27913)
*Theodore I. Weinberger,Daniel Shaffer,Zheyu Wu,Dmitry V. Chichinadze,Jinxu Pu,Gang Li,Rui Zhou,Yurii Skourski,Dave Graf,Andrej Cabala,Vladimir Sechovsky,Michal Valiska,Michal P. Kwasigroch,F. Malte Grosche,Alexander G. Eaton*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过稳态磁场实验（扭矩磁强法、提取磁强法及磁导测量）系统研究了UTe₂中的变磁相变（metamagnetic transition），揭示了其复杂的子结构，区分了巡游（itinerant）与局域（localized）磁矩贡献，并理论建模指出磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）的坍塌增强了沿硬b轴的纵向自旋涨落（longitudinal spin fluctuations），从而稳定了p波配对（p-wave pairing）的SC2超导相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UTe₂中的变磁相变对稳定两个场致超导相（SC2和SC3）起关键作用，但现有研究多基于脉冲磁场，稳态磁场下的精细结构尚不明确，亟需系统实验刻画其微观机制。

Method: 采用扭矩磁强法（torque magnetometry）和提取磁强法（extraction magnetometry）在常压下测量UTe₂的变磁特性，并在压力下测量磁导（magnetoconductance）；同时基于Kondo与RKKY相互作用的演化进行理论建模。

Result: 稳态测量揭示了变磁相变内部的复杂子结构，不同特征具有不同的温度演化行为，指向巡游与局域磁矩的分别贡献；巡游贡献可能与自旋密度波态（spin-density wave state）相关。理论模型表明，压力下磁各向异性坍塌增强了沿硬b轴的纵向自旋涨落，有利于p波通道的配对形成。

Conclusion: SC2超导相在压力下被稳定是由于磁各向异性的坍塌，进而增强纵向自旋涨落，为p波配对提供了条件；这一机制解释了变磁相变与场致超导相之间的关联。

Abstract: The metamagnetic transition in UTe$_2$ plays a key role in stabilizing two enigmatic field-induced superconducting phases. One of these phases (SC2) is truncated by the transition, lying directly below it, while the other (SC3) sits predominantly above it and appears to be stabilized because of it. While numerous pulsed field studies have examined this transition, comparatively few steady field experiments have investigated it. Here we report a suite of measurements of metamgnetism in UTe$_2$, at ambient pressure by torque magnetometry and extraction magnetometry techniques, and of the magnetoconductance under pressure. Our steady field measurements resolve a complex sub-structure within the transition, with separate features that possess different temperature evolutions, pointing to distinct contributions from itinerant and localized moments. The itinerant contribution might relate to a possible spin-density wave state. We theoretically model the evolution of Kondo and RKKY interactions and propose that the SC2 state is stabilized under pressure due to the collapse of magnetic anisotropy, leading to an enhancement of longitudinal spin fluctuations along the hard $b$ axis, which are pair-forming in the $p$-wave channel.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Hybridized magnon-phonon modes in magnetically ordered FeF_2 were observed and successfully analysed half a century ago.

### [157] [Competing spin-1 and spin-2 regimes in a frustrated four-leg spin-1/2 ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27991)
*D. S. Almeida,R. R. Montenegro-Filho*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算，研究了一个受挫的四腿自旋-1/2梯子模型，揭示了三种不同区域：短程反铁磁腿、短程铁磁腿以及一个有效的自旋-2海森堡链，并通过交叉（crossover）和一阶相变（first-order transition）分隔。通过将模型重组为两个受挫的两腿梯子耦合系统，追踪了平庸相与Haldane相的演化，阐明了有效自旋-1与自旋-2行为的涌现机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解受挫多腿自旋梯子模型中有效高自旋行为（effective high-spin behavior）的涌现机制，以及不同自旋区域（如自旋-1和自旋-2）之间的相变和交叉现象。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算方法，并引入投影自旋-2有效哈密顿量（projected $S_r=2$ effective Hamiltonian）进行对比验证。通过将四腿梯子重新解释为两个受挫的两腿梯子耦合系统，分析层间耦合（interladder couplings）引入后平庸相与Haldane相的演化。

Result: 均匀系统展现出三个区域：短程反铁磁腿、短程铁磁腿和有效自旋-2海森堡链，由交叉和一阶相变分隔。自旋-2区域通过有限弦序参量（string order parameter）、边缘局域激发（edge-localized excitations）以及与投影自旋-2有效哈密顿量的高度一致得到确认。相图揭示了交叉线和一阶相变线，并展示了单重态主导与三重态主导区域的重新组织方式。

Conclusion: 成功刻画了四腿自旋-1/2梯子模型的完整相图，阐明了有效自旋-1与自旋-2行为随耦合强度变化的涌现过程，为理解多腿梯子系统中的高自旋有效理论提供了定量框架。

Abstract: We investigate a frustrated four-leg spin-$1/2$ ladder using density matrix renormalization group calculations. The uniform system displays three regimes: short-range antiferromagnetic legs, short-range ferromagnetic legs, and an effective spin-2 Heisenberg chain, separated by a crossover and a first-order transition. The spin-2 regime is confirmed through its finite string order parameter, edge-localized excitations, and excellent agreement with a projected $S_r=2$ effective Hamiltonian. Recasting the model as two frustrated two-leg ladders coupled by rung and diagonal interactions, we track how the trivial and Haldane phases of an isolated ladder evolve as interladder couplings are introduced. The resulting phase diagrams reveal crossover and first-order lines whose locations are captured by the spin-2 projection and show how singlet- and triplet-dominated regimes reorganize when two ladders merge into a four-leg structure, clarifying the emergence of effective spin-1 versus spin-2 behavior.

</details>


### [158] [Ferrimagnetic and Haldane-type phases in a mixed-spin $1$-$\tfrac{1}{2}$-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ quantum trimer chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28000)
*A. Felinto,R. R. Montenegro-Filho*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）研究混合自旋 Heisenberg 三聚体链，发现当侧向耦合 $J_t>0$ 时出现强铁磁平台（$m=1$），当 $J_t<0$ 时系统映射为自旋-1 Heisenberg 链并呈现 Haldane 相（$m=0$），边缘态与纠缠谱简并证实了其对称性保护拓扑特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究准一维量子磁体中二分 Lieb-Mattis 铁磁序（bipartite Lieb-Mattis ferrimagnetism）与对称性保护 Haldane 相（symmetry-protected Haldane phase）这两种基本机制如何在混合自旋链中出现并相互转换。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，计算磁化曲线、纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）和纠缠熵（entanglement entropy），分析不同耦合符号下的相行为。

Result: $J_t>0$ 时出现稳健的 $m=1$ 铁磁平台，其多自旋纠缠熵反映磁化在链两半之间的分配；$J_t<0$ 时 $m=0$ 平台随 $|J_t|$ 增大而扩张，而 $m=1$ 平台闭合。当 $J_t\to-\infty$，链映射为耦合 $J/2$ 的自旋-1 Heisenberg 链，$m=0$ 平台宽度 $\Delta h\simeq 0.196$ 恰好等于 Haldane 能隙的一半。此外，指数局域的自旋-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ 边缘态和纠缠谱的偶重简并证实了 $m=0$ 相的 Haldane 特征。

Conclusion: 混合自旋 $1$-$\tfrac{1}{2}$-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ Heisenberg 三聚体链在侧向耦合符号变化下可分别实现铁磁序相与 Haldane 相，且 $J_t<0$ 极限下系统与自旋-1 Heisenberg 链等价，揭示了从铁磁序到对称性保护拓扑相的平滑过渡机制。

Abstract: Bipartite Lieb-Mattis ferrimagnetism and the symmetry-protected Haldane phase are paradigmatic mechanisms in quasi-one-dimensional quantum magnets. Both emerge, in distinct regimes, in a mixed-spin $1$-$\tfrac{1}{2}$-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ Heisenberg trimer chain with antiferromagnetic backbone exchange $J$ and a side spin-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ coupled to each backbone spin by an exchange $J_t$ of either sign. Using the density matrix renormalization group, we compute magnetization curves and the entanglement spectrum and entropy. For $J_t>0$ a robust ferrimagnetic plateau forms at magnetization per unit cell $m=1$, whose multiplet entropy reflects how the conserved magnetization splits between the halves. For $J_t<0$ an $m=0$ plateau opens and grows with $|J_t|$, while the $m=1$ plateau closes. As $J_t\to-\infty$ the chain maps onto a spin-$1$ Heisenberg chain with coupling $J/2$: the $m=0$ width $Δh\simeq 0.196$ matches half the Haldane gap. Exponentially localized spin-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ edge states and the even-fold degeneracy of the entanglement spectrum confirm the Haldane character of the $m=0$ phase.

</details>

### [159] [Self-organized robustness in mean-field interacting systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27626)
*Emmy Blumenthal,Gautam Reddy*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个可解的平均场（mean-field）模型，将自组织鲁棒性（self-organized robustness）形式化为对系统扰动响应的元优化（meta-optimization），揭示了相互作用结构可视为一种动态调制的“景观海（seascape）”，并指出集体动力学在状态空间中遵循优化的Wasserstein梯度流（Wasserstein gradient flow）趋向吸引子。模型预测了受限通信下对慢弛豫模式与频繁扰动模式的优先编码，以及平坦平衡景观与中间“库状态（reservoir states）”的存在，最终将自组织诠释为一种层次化的联想记忆（hierarchical associative memory）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统的一个重要特征是自组织——秩序往往源于组分间的相互作用而非集中式的反馈控制。作者希望构建一个可解析处理的理论框架，用以理解这种分布式自组织如何产生鲁棒性。

Method: 模型采用平均场近似，将自组织鲁棒性形式化为一种对系统扰动响应的元优化问题。推导出的相互作用结构对应一个动态调制的“景观海”，其形状由自洽条件决定以加速弛豫回到平衡。集体动力学被刻画为状态空间中优化的Wasserstein梯度流。

Result: 当通信受限时，相互作用会优先编码慢弛豫模式和频繁被扰动的模式。模型还预测鲁棒集体态对应更平坦的平衡景观，并在这类系统中存在一个连续的中间“库状态”谱。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一个新的理论视角：自组织可以被理解为一种层次化的联想记忆，其运行尺度是一个由相互作用的计算单元构成的集体。

Abstract: Self-organization is a defining feature of living systems, with order often maintained through interactions between constituent units rather than centralized feedback. We introduce a tractable mean-field model of self-organized robustness, formulated as meta-optimization over the system's response to perturbations. The resulting interaction structure has an intuitive picture as a dynamically modulated landscape (``seascape'') whose shape is determined self-consistently to accelerate relaxation back to equilibrium. The collective dynamics follows an optimized Wasserstein gradient flow toward an attractor in the space of collective states. When communication is limited, interactions preferentially encode slowly relaxing modes and modes that are frequently perturbed. The model further shows that robust collective states are associated with flatter equilibrium landscapes and predicts a continuum of intermediate ``reservoir states'' in such systems. The model offers a perspective of self-organization as a hierarchical associative memory that operates on the scale of a collective of interacting computational units.

</details>


### [160] [The Allee Effect in Compressible Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28260)
*Jonathan Bauermann,Roberto Benzi,David R. Nelson,Federico Toschi*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 研究了海洋微生物在近表层被湍流平流时，Allee效应与压缩流共同作用对种群存活的影响，推导了小和大Damköhler数极限下的承载能力解析表达式，并通过数值模拟揭示了两种极限的衔接关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海洋微生物常被限制在近表层并被湍流平流，这种受限平流产生有效压缩流，使繁殖与输运之间的相互作用变得复杂。本文旨在探究当种群增长受Allee效应（Allee effect）支配时，压缩流产生的汇（sink）与源（source）如何影响此类物种的生存。

Method: 在Allee效应框架下，推导了小Damköhler数（Damköhler number）和大Damköhler数极限下承载能力（carrying capacity）关于Allee强度的解析表达式；采用数值模拟揭示两种极限之间的连续过渡关系。Damköhler数定义为大涡周转时间与生物生长率的乘积。

Result: 在小Damköhler数极限下，存在一个由压缩流统计特性决定的最大Allee强度，超过该阈值会导致物种在充分发展的湍流中灭绝。数值模拟展示了两种极限如何相互连接。

Conclusion: 压缩流产生的源汇结构对具有Allee效应的种群存活具有显著影响；小Damköhler数极限下的灭绝阈值由湍流压缩流的统计特性决定。

Abstract: Microbes in marine environments are often confined to thin near-surface layers while being advected by turbulent flows. Because such constrained advection generates an effectively compressible flow, reproduction and transport interact in a nontrivial way. Here, we focus on populations whose growth is governed by an Allee effect and show that sinks and sources, generated by the compressible flow, have dramatic consequences for the survival of such species. We derive analytical expressions for the carrying capacity as a function of the Allee strength in the limit of small and large Damköhler number, which measures the product of the large eddy turnover time and the organism growth rate. Numerical simulations reveal how these two limits connect. In the limit of small Damköhler number, we find a maximal Allee strength, set by the statistics of the compressible flow, that leads to species extinction in fully developed turbulence.

</details>

### [161] [High-Order Asymptotic-Preserving Schemes for Kinetic Equations from Rarefied to Incompressible Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28040)
*Giacomo Dimarco,Axel Klar,Theresa Köfler,Lorenzo Pareschi,Tiwari Sudarshan*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于求解动理学方程（kinetic equations）的新型高阶数值框架，该框架基于微观-宏观分解（micro-macro decomposition）和隐式-显式龙格-库塔方法（Implicit-Explicit Runge-Kutta methods），具备渐近保持（Asymptotic-Preserving, AP）性质，能够在平均自由程（mean free path）从稀薄动理学尺度到不可压缩流体动力学极限（incompressible hydrodynamic limit）的全部范围内保持均匀有效，并在极限条件下自洽退化为不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的高阶有限差分格式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动理学方程在不同稀薄度（rarefaction）下的数值求解面临挑战，尤其是在从稀薄动理学尺度到不可压缩流体动力学极限的宽泛平均自由程范围内，需设计一种能够全程保持有效性和精度的统一数值框架。

Method: 该方法基于微观-宏观分解（micro-macro decomposition）将动理学方程重构为宏观流体动力学演化部分和微观非平衡偏离部分的耦合系统；时间方向上采用隐式-显式龙格-库塔方法（Implicit-Explicit Runge-Kutta methods）保证刚性区域（stiff regimes）的稳定性与高阶精度；空间方向上结合有限差分WENO重构（finite-difference WENO reconstructions）与高阶中心差分近似（high-order central difference approximations）提升分辨率；该方法具有渐近保持（Asymptotic-Preserving, AP）性质。

Result: 理论分析表明，在平均自由程趋于零的渐近极限下，该格式一致地退化为不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的高阶有限差分格式。一维和二维基准问题的数值实验验证了该方法在不同流动区域中的精度、稳定性和通用性。

Conclusion: 该高阶数值框架在全部流动区域（流动区域）上保持均匀有效，兼具渐近保持特性与高阶时空精度，为动理学方程的跨尺度数值模拟提供了一种统一且可靠的方法。

Abstract: This work introduces a novel high-order numerical framework for solving kinetic equations, designed to remain uniformly valid across all regimes of the mean free path, spanning from the rarefied kinetic scale to the incompressible hydrodynamic limit. The method is built upon a micro-macro decomposition, which reformulates the underlying kinetic equation into a coupled system consisting of a macroscopic part, representing the fluid-dynamic evolution, and a microscopic part, describing the non-equilibrium deviations. The proposed framework ensures high-order temporal accuracy through the use of Implicit-Explicit Runge-Kutta methods, which provide stability and efficiency in stiff regimes, while spatial resolution is enhanced by combining finite-difference WENO reconstructions with high-order central difference approximations. A key feature of the proposed methodology is its Asymptotic-Preserving (AP) property. We demonstrate that, in the appropriate asymptotic limit as the mean free path tends to zero, the scheme consistently reduces to a high-order finite-difference formulation of the incompressible Navier-Stokes equations. To support the theoretical findings, a set of numerical experiments are performed on one- and two-dimensional benchmark problems, which confirm the accuracy, stability, and versatility of the method across different flow regimes.

</details>

### [162] [Collision and coalescence dynamics of bosonic quantum Hall droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27768)
*Xinyi Liu,Zhendong Li,Yuwen Zhou,Siying Li,Haoran Xu,Zihe Liu,Rongzhen Jiao,Mingyuan Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文基于Gross-Pitaevskii框架系统研究了快速旋转玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中量子霍尔液滴（bosonic quantum Hall droplets）的碰撞与合并动力学，发现了由初始相对速度控制的合并/分离两种碰撞结果，给出了临界速度的标度律，并揭示了涡旋阵列形成机制及系统的局域化特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验在快速旋转的二维BEC中观测到了具有鲁棒动力学稳定性的玻色量子霍尔液滴，然而其碰撞与合并等非平衡动力学行为尚未被深入理解，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在Gross-Pitaevskii（GP）框架下对双液滴碰撞及多液滴重叠过程进行数值模拟，并结合简化的解析模型对临界速度标度律进行理论解释。

Result: (1) 双液滴碰撞存在合并与分离两种结果，由初始相对速度决定，临界速度满足标度律 $v_c \propto (gN)^{1/4}$；(2) 碰撞显著改变液滴形状，但质心轨迹因角动量守恒几乎不受影响；(3) 重叠静止液滴中，相诱导剪切流可通过Kelvin-Helmholtz不稳定性（Kelvin-Helmholtz instability）产生涡旋阵列；(4) 多个液滴重叠无法构建扩展态，系统动态重组为新的孤立液滴，呈现出体区域（bulk region）的局域化特性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了量子霍尔液滴独特的非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics），为操控强关联旋转量子流体（strongly correlated rotating quantum fluids）提供了新的途径。

Abstract: Recently bosonic quantum Hall droplets have been observed in rapidly rotating two-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs), which exhibit robust dynamical stability. Inspired by this, we systematically investigate the collision and coalescence dynamics of these droplets within the Gross-Pitaevskii framework. For two-droplet collisions, we find two distinct collision outcomes, namely merging and separation, that are controlled by the initial relative velocity. The critical velocity exhibits a universal scaling law with the interaction and the particle number as $v_c \propto (gN)^{1/4}$, which can be interpreted from a simplified analytical model, revealing the essential role of the collision time. It differs fundamentally from the mechanism governing the conventional Lee-Huang-Yang stabilized quantum droplets. Furthermore, while the collision can change the shape of the droplet significantly, the center of mass trajectory remains nearly unaffected, owing to the conservation of angular momentum. For overlapping stationary droplets, vortex arrays can emerge through Kelvin-Helmholtz instability driven by phase-induced shear flow. Although two droplets may merge into a larger one, extended states cannot be constructed from multiple overlapping droplets. Instead, the system dynamically reorganizes into new isolated droplets, revealing the localized property in the bulk region. Our results reveal the unique nonequilibrium dynamics of quantum Hall droplets and suggest new pathways for manipulating strongly correlated rotating quantum fluids.

</details>


### [163] [Universality in strongly interacting bosonic clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27823)
*L. Madeira,F. Pederiva,U. van Kolck*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文针对强相互作用的玻色子团簇（bosonic clusters）建立有效场论（effective field theory, EFT），以$^4$He为范例，在领头阶（leading order, LO）和次领头阶（next-to-leading order, NLO）分别拟合二体、三体及四体基态能量，实现对最多$N=15$个粒子系统的系统收敛描述，并与真实势结果高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以系统描述具有大散射长度（large scattering length）的强相互作用玻色子团簇，需要一种模型无关且可系统改进的有效场论框架，以捕捉从少体到多体及体相氦（bulk helium）的普适性（universality）。

Method: 在领头阶中，二体和三体零程相互作用（zero-range interactions）由二聚体（dimer）和三聚体（trimer）基态能量完全确定；在次领头阶中，引入两体相互作用程修正和四体力（four-body force），通过四聚体（tetramer）基态能量校准，减少对截断（cutoff）的敏感性。

Result: 领头阶下，最多$N=15$个粒子的基态能量收敛至截断无关的极限，外推系数为自然大小；次领头阶显著降低截断敏感性；领头阶即与真实势结果接近，次领头阶进一步改善。

Conclusion: 该有效场论在每阶仅需少数参数即可实现系统收敛，直接适用于更大团簇及体相氦，验证了强相互作用玻色系统的普适性。

Abstract: We develop an effective field theory (EFT) for strongly interacting bosonic clusters, using $^4$He as a paradigmatic example of universality in systems with large scattering length. At leading order (LO), two- and three-body zero-range interactions are entirely determined by the dimer and trimer ground-state energies. We show that ground-state energies for up to $N=15$ particles converge to cutoff-independent limits with extrapolation coefficients of natural size. At next-to-leading order (NLO), corrections stemming from the two-body interaction range and a four-body force, calibrated to the tetramer ground-state energy, reduce cutoff sensitivity. Close agreement with results from a realistic potential is found at LO and improved at NLO, demonstrating systematic convergence with few parameters at each order. The resulting EFT is directly applicable to larger clusters and bulk helium.

</details>


### [164] [Coexisting Regular and Chaotic Dynamics in the Dysprosium Feshbach Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28233)
*Julie Veschambre,Alexandre Journeaux,Maxime Lecomte,Alice Belmon,Ethan Uzan,Inès de Verdelhan,Patricia Christina Marques Castilho,Jakub Zakrzewski,Jean Dalibard,Raphael Lopes*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过精确校准$^{162}$Dy的Feshbach谱并结合超过80个共振态的微分磁矩测量，发现强偶极气体的能级统计并非均匀：磁矩分布中心附近的共振态表现出增强的能级排斥，而低能边缘附近则接近泊松统计。结果表明，分子态组成是强偶极散射中量子混沌涌现的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强偶极气体（如镝、铒、铥）的Feshbach谱具有密集的能级结构，其能级统计被认为与多分子通道耦合引发的量子混沌（quantum chaos）有关。但该混沌谱的内部结构尚不明确，需要更精细的探测量子混沌涌现的微观机制。

Method: 对$^{162}$Dy的Feshbach谱进行精确校准，并对0至30高斯（G）范围内超过80个共振态进行微分磁矩（differential magnetic moments）的光谱测量。磁矩作为本征态敏感探针（eigenstate-sensitive probe），用以解析共振谱背后的分子态性质。

Result: 能级统计并非均匀：磁矩分布中心附近的共振态显示出增强的能级排斥（level repulsion），而低能边缘附近的共振态则接近泊松统计（Poisson statistics）。这表明Feshbach谱中存在隐藏的局域结构。

Conclusion: 分子态组成（molecular-state composition）是强偶极散射中量子混沌涌现的关键因素。该发现揭示了混沌的镝Feshbach谱内部的隐藏结构，加深了对量子混沌在强偶极系统中起源的理解。

Abstract: Strongly dipolar gases, such as dysprosium, erbium and thulium, exhibit dense Feshbach spectra whose level statistics have been associated with quantum chaos arising from couplings among many molecular channels. Here, we combine a precise calibration of the Feshbach spectrum of $^{162}$Dy with spectroscopic measurements of the differential magnetic moments of bound states associated with more than 80 resonances between 0 and 30 G. These magnetic moments provide an eigenstate-sensitive probe of the molecular states underlying the resonance spectrum. We find that the level statistics are not uniform: resonances associated with states near the center of the magnetic-moment distribution display enhanced level repulsion, whereas those near the lower edge remain close to Poisson statistics. Our results reveal hidden structure within the chaotic dysprosium Feshbach spectrum and identify molecular-state composition as a key ingredient in the emergence of quantum chaos in strongly dipolar scattering.

</details>
